thar chos kyi 'byung gnas su rgyas par gsungs pa ni/ a ti sha spyan 'dren pa'i pho nya la/ nag tso lo tsA ba rgyu mtshan du mas legs par dgongs te/ lha btsun pas spyan
sngar bos/ bsnyen bkur nas/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa la zhu na/ nga'i yab mes rgyal blon byang chub sems dpa' de rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i dbu brnyes/ srol btod/ dar
zhing rgyas par mdzad pa yin pa la/ dus ding sang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nyam dmas/ bdud rigs kyi sems can kha rgyal/ chos ltar bcos pa rnams dar bas/ shes pa skyo bar
byung/ nged khu dbon gnyis kyis mi 'dis go chod dam/ 'dis sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la sems snyam pa rnams la/ gser srang brgya skor res ma mtha' byas jo bo gdan 'dren
du btang ba yin na'ang/ bstan pa'i bya ba ches pas gdan ma 'drongs drongs/ des kyang blo ma bsad par/ lha chen po des bal yul gyi mtha' mkhob tu jo bo gdan 'dren pa'i gser
'tshol du byon pas/ gar log gi rgyal pos/ chos kyi rgyal po paNDi ta gdan 'dren pa'i gser 'tshol bar rig nas/ 'di'i pha mes rnams kyis sngon yang sangs rgyas kyi bstan
pa dar bar byas 'dis kyang paNDi ta gdan 'dren/ bstan pa dar bar byed pas/ gzung la btson khang du chug zer nas mnar/ de bdag gis thos pas khu bo ldog tu phyin yang/ gar
log gi rgyal po tshan ches nas ma ldog yang dmag byas na ldogs par snang ste/ de'i bar du 'gro ba mang po'i srog 'chad pa dang/ nga rang la yang bar chad byung na jo bo spyan
mi 'drongs drongs par gda' bas/ khong rang dang bstun/ kho na re/ 'o na

paNDi ta gdan 'dren pa'i 'phro bshol/ nga'i bstan pa la zhugs/ yang na gser rgyal po rang dang mnyam pa khyer la shog/ de nas btang gi zer bas/ gser la 'dams nas/ lus dang
mnyam pas blus kyang ma nyan de nas khu bo la/ da ngas dbu tsam zhig rnyed pa dang blur 'ong gi zhus pas/ bzhad lo gcig mdzad nas da des chog/ nga'i bsam pa la/ bod 'dir
chos khrims shig ma 'chos par shi na mi rung snyam pa yin te/ da na so yang rgas/ 'khor ba thog med nas chos kyi phyir lus btang ba med/ da lan chos kyi phyir shi na legs
pa yin bas/ sdig rgyal 'di la gser se ba gcig kyang ma ster/ gser thams cad rgya gar du khyer la/ da dung a ti sha gdan ci 'drongs drongs gyis/ paNDi ta chen po'i snyan
du yang/ ngas khyed dang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i phyir du lus srog gar log gi rgyal po ngan pa la byin yod pas kho tshe rabs thams cad du bdag thugs rjes 'dzin pa dang/
nga'i bsam pa'i gtso bo khyod bod du byon nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar byed pa yin pas/ de kho na bzhin du mdzad par zhu/ skye ba 'di'i 'og rol du khyed dang nges
par mjal bar byin gyis brlab tu gsol/ zhes nga'i 'phrin mdzod cig/ de ltar lags pas nga blos thongs la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la soms shig gsung/ de nas khu bo gar
log gi rgyal pos med par byas pas/ gtam de rnams mgon po a ti sha'i snyan du thongs/ nged bod mtha' mkhob kyi sems can ma rig pa rnamasakyi snying stobs de 'dra na/ khyed
'gro ba'i skyabs gnas thugs rje can ji ltar song zhes zhus shig/ 'di na gser srang bdun brgya yod pa bla ma'i phyag tu phul/ nged bod pre ta pu ri'i grong khyer lta bu na
gser se ba re tsam la'ang rtsis chen po yod la/ da 'dis bdag cag gi mi nor

thams cad rdzogs nas yod kyi/ da lan jo bo bod du ma byon na khyed dam pa rnams kyi thugs rje yang de ltar bas pas/ nged kyang bya ba ci bder spyad par bgyi'o zhes/ khyed 'dul
ba 'dzin pas lo brgyus rgyus 'di rnams jo bo la zhus pa'i tha la 'byon du ma bzhed na'ang/ snyan du thebs par mdzad do gsungs nas/ bshum cing gsung byon te/ lha btsun
mi chen po gcig gis de ltar mdzad pas/ lo tsA bas kyang yin min gyi tshig zur tsam yang smra ma nus/ de'i stobs kyis lus srog dang/ bar chad kyi dka' tshegs/ tshe 'di'i
bde skyid gang la'ang ma chags par dpon g.yog bdun gyis gser rnams khyer te/ rgya gar gyie lam du zhugs pa dang/ lha btsun pas skyel thung mdzad de/ dge slong khyod kyis
nga phyogs bya ba byas/ da lan dka' ba chen na'ang phar byon la/ 'bad rtsol chen pos lus dang srog la bsdos/ 'khor nas byas shes bka' drin gzo bar bya/ zhes gsungs nas/ phyi
phyag mdzad de gshegs/ slar yang jo bo thugs rje chen po la gsol ba 'debs kyi gshegs par zhu gsung/ de nas bal po rdzong la byon tsa na mi ring gcig dang phrad pas/ khyed
yul sa thag ring por don chen po la 'gro bar snang ba/ 'di skad zer gyi song dang/ don grub nas 'ong gi/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ kha ba can gyi rgyal khams
su/ rgyal ba thams cad kyi 'byung gnas/ dam pa'i chos 'phel bar gyur cig/ ces brjod cing song na/ lam du'ang nye zho mi 'byung zer/ khyed su lags byas pas/ rim gyis shes
par 'gyur gyi zer/ de nas bal po'i mtha' mkhob tu sleb pa na/ a tsa ra la gnas g.yar bas/ snyug khang gcig tu bsnyal/ khos gser yod par shes nas snyug khang la me spar
te/ bsad nas gser 'khyer bar 'dod pa dang/

lo tsA ba dpon g.yog sa thag ring po la ngal zhing tshad pas gdungs te gnyid kyis myos pa'i sngas mgor mi ring dkar po gcig snyug khang gi mthongs phye nas byung ste/ ma nyal
ma nyal myur du yar la longs/ ma phebs da lta longs la lam du zhugs/ nyal na rin chen srog dang 'bral bar yod/ nga ni bod khams yongs kyi yi dam yin/ zhes gsungs pas/
thugs rje chen po la gsol ba btab nas bros/ nam langs pa dang bal po'i rgyal phran gcig bi kra ma lar 'gro ba dang 'dzoms te/ de dang 'grogs nas chu bo gangga'i 'gram du
sleb pa dang/ rgyal po dbang ches pas sngon du gru la song/ der nyi ma 'phyis pas gser rnams bye ma'i 'og tu sbas nas/ phyogs gzhan zhig tu nyal ba na/ mnyan pa dkar po gcig
gru la skya ba chal chal 'debs kyi byung/ der lo tsA bas khyed su yin gar gshegs dris pas/ dpon g.yog 'khor bcas bsu ru 'ongs pa yin/ sems can snying stobs chen pos 'dir
'ongs tshe/ 'phags pa gru dang mnyan pa lta bu yis/ 'jigs pa'i dus su bsu skyel ma byas na/ sems can nyon mongs can gyis ji ltar 'grub/ tshur zhugs bdun brgya po de ma
lus par/ 'bol le kra ma la ru sgrol bar bya/ zhes zer ba dang/ gser rnams bton te grur zhugs/ ma Ni bgrangs pas/ mnyan pa na re/ nged kha ba can gyi thugs rje chen po de
ma Ni 'di ltar byed pa yin zer nas bgrangs tsa na/ snyan pa/ yid 'dzin par gyur pas/ the tshom du gyur te khyod su yin nam gsung tsag 'byon par zhu byas pas/ mnyan pa na
re tshe dang ldan pa snga 'grogs kyi dus spobs pa ma myur gzhung 'grogs kyi dus khrel gzhung ma chung/ phyi 'grogs kyi dus su phyi thag ma thung bya ba/ ma nus pa'i dus
phan pa dang/

dgos dus sleb pa bya ba yun du 'grogs pa la dgos pa yin/ rim gyis shes par 'gyur gsung/ de ma thag gru sgrol ba dang/ da nam phyed du song dug sbrul dang chom rkun gyi 'jigs
pa 'ong bas de nub bi gsum ma la'i sgo spe'i 'og tu nyol gsung nas gzhan du song/ der sleb pa na/ rgya brtson 'grus seng ge sgo khang steng na bzhugs pas gsan te/ khyed
rnams gang nas 'ongs gsung/ nged mnga' ris stod nas yin zhus pas/ 'don sgo ba byis pa cig yod pa de la khyed rang gi nor rnams chol la der gzims gsung/ de nas byis pa la
gser rnams bcol bas/ blo gtad thub pa grogs kyi mchog bya ba yin/ khyed rang rnams bag phel par gzims zer/ nang par sgo phye ma thag byis pa gzhon nu cig gis/ bod kyi skad
du khyed rnams gang nas byon/ lam la 'jigs pa mi 'dug gam zer bas/ nged mnga' ris nas 'ongs/ lam 'jam par byung/ khyed su yin byas pas nga yang bod ciig yin/ nged rang
bod 'di kha mang la gting lhod/ gtam kham chen sbed mi shes/ bya ba gal chen gsangs nas bsgrub dgos pa yin/ rgya brtson seng bod kyi spyi khang na yod/ der song zer nas
kho yud kyis song/ de nas srang ring po gcig la phyin tsa na/ drang srong rgan po chu shing gi mkhar ba thogs pa gcig dang 'phrad pas/ de na re/ khyod gang nas 'ongs/ gang
du 'gro/ don ci la 'ongs zer bas nged bod mnga' ris nas/ a ti sha spyan 'dren du 'ongs pa yin/ rgya brtson seng gi khang pa gang na yod byas pas/ kho mkhar ba la brten
nas phyi mig gcu ba zhig byas/ da nang gi byis pa re bden/ bod kyi mi la ol mdud med pas/ srang nang gi mi 'khyams po tshun la yin

tshul sang nge 'chad pa khyod kyis kyang don 'grub tu re ba ang/ da lan nga'i rtsar byas pas drag/ da jo bo min pa gzhan gyi rtsar khar ma 'don/ rgya brtsoon seng la zur tsam
zer na'ang rigs/ sga sgo ngas bstan zer nas kho ga le song ba'i phyi la lo tsA bas mgyogs por phyin pas ma sleb/ kho bod kyi spyi khang sgor bsgugs 'dug pas/ lo tsA ba
ya mtshan zhing the tshom du gyur pa dang/ kho na re/ bya ba chen po bsgrub pa la go le mgyogs pa yin/ 'dood thag ma nye bar ri bo bags kyis 'dzegs/ khang pa 'di yin zer/
nang du phyin pa na lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng rgya dpe tshan ci gzigs kyi 'dug pa la/ phyag rten gser mtshon byed re phul nas/ lo tsA bas khyod rnams don ci la 'ongs gsung/
de la gong gi lo brgyus rgyus rnams zhib par zhus pas/ khong gi zhal nas/ da a ti sha gdan 'dren du 'ongs skad ye ma zer/ slob gnyer la yongs zer ba smos/ gnas brtan
ratnA a kA ra dbang che bas/ des tshor du ye mi btub/ da lta rang khong la gser srang phyed phul la/ nged bod nas 'ongs/ paNDi ta ni spyan ma 'drongs/ da khyed kyis paNDi
ta dang khyad med pa'i slob gnyer cig thugs la 'dogs pa zhu zhes zhus/ de nas kyang rings rings dang blo ma phebs pa ma byed par slob gnyer gyis la sos bsdol/ de nas 'o
cag thabs mkhas pos jo bo la zhu ba byed pa yin gsung/ de nas nag tsho lo tsA ba ci gsung lta ba'i ched du mgon po a ti sha cis kyang gdan ma 'drongs drongs na/ de'i 'og
nas gang che ba'i paNDi ta cig gdan drangs na zhus pas/ lo tsA ba'i zhal nas

de 'dra so sgor ma 'don de yin na/ nang ning nas paN chen gcig las gcig che ba nyi shu tsam gdan drangs na'ang 'drongs drongs te/ 'o skol bod kyi sems can gyi spyod gshis rgyus
med dam/ a ti sha ma gtogs sus kyang bod kyi sems can mi thul bas/ da dung a ti sha rang gdan ci 'drongs drongs byed gsung ngo/ gzhan paNDi ta ci 'dra yod zhus pas/
'di ltar/ shAnti pa/ nA ro pa/ Do mi ba/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ a ba dhu tI pa/ byang chub bzang po/ rin chen bzang po/ rin chen sde/ lha'i blo gros/ ngag dbang grags pa/
nag po pa/ dzai tA re dgra las rnam par rgyal ba/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ sa 'gebs pa'i zhabs/ ye shes gsang ba/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ tshul khrims dbang po la sogs pa paNDi ta
bsam gyis mi khyab pa lnga bcu rtsa gnyis tsam yod kyang/ thams cad rang sa rang sa na ngo mtshar che mod kyang/ 'o skol bod la mgon po a ti sha min pas phan med gsung/
'o na a ti sha ston par zhu dang zhus pas/ khyod rang nang par dge 'dun gyi kun dga' ra bar dge 'dun stong phrag mang po 'ong gi/ de'i nang na lhong ba/ lha me ba/ sku lta
bas chog mi shes pa/ gral gang du bzhugs kyang mdzes pa zhig yod kyis/ de a ti sha yin pas/ de la nyin mtshan du gsol ba thob gsung/ de nas rgya brtson seng dpon slob
gnyis kyis gnas brtan ratnA a kA ra'i drung du phyin/ phyag byas gser srang phyed phul te/ rgyas bslabs pa bzhin nag tshos zhus pas/ gnas brtan gyi zhal nas/ shin du legs/
tshe dang ldan pa 'di ltar yin/ nged 'dir mi la tsag pa ma yin te/ 'di na a ti sha med na/ rgya gar sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i 'byung gnas yin pas/ 'dir

nyams na sems can spyi'i bde skyid nyams 'gro ba yin mod/ de'i rgyu mtshan/ rgya gar gyi chos srol dang/ gtsug lag khang thams cad kyi lde mig a ti sha'i phyag na yod pa yin/
de min na nged kyang bod kyi sems can la sems brtse zhing/ khyad par du bod kyi chos rgyal de'i mi nor mang po zad pas ngo mnong ste/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la babs
pa yin pas/ de soms la brtson 'grus drag pos bstan pa rab 'byam la slob gnyer gyis/ ngas kyang tshig su ci 'gro byed/ khyed bod rgya gar ba la 'di ltar sems pa ngo mtshar
che zhes gsung/ de nas gnas brtan gyis khrid de dge 'dun gyi gdugs tshod gral du phyin/ a ti sha gral gyi dbu la bzhugs sam snyam pa la/ shAnti pa bzhugs 'dug pa la/ 'di
a ti sha lags sam byas pas/ tshe dang ldan pa 'di ni shAnti pa zhes bya ba/ mkhas grub chen po a ti sha'i yang bla ma de lags mod zer/ de ltar rje btsun nA ro pa la sogs
pa gral gyi dbu la 'dug pa la re re bzhin 'di a ti sha yin nam zhes dris pas/ 'di nA ro pa zhes pa ding sang 'gran zla dang bral ba a ti sha'i yang bla ma yin zer/ gzhan
du a ti sha ma mthong bas yid zhum pa na/ dus re shig zhig bi kra ma la'i rgyal po khri bshams pa'i steng na 'dug pa/ paNDi ta che chung gang la'ang ldang ba mi byed par
snang ba la/ a ti sha sku bzi brjid che zhing/ zhal 'dzum chags pa/ cam por gshegs pa gcig nang du byon pa dang/ rgyal po des khri las langs pas/ paNDi ta dang dge 'dun
thams cad kyis ldang ba byas/ gral stong du bzhugs pa/ mtho bas 'di a ti sha yin nam dris pas/ ci zer 'ad dpa' bo bzhad pa'i rdo rje zhes pa gnas nges med du

'byon pa'i paNDi ta cig yin zer/ 'di la yon tan ji tsam yod byas pas/ 'di'i yon tan gyi tshod nged kyis mi lon zer nas/ a ti sha yin pa 'chad ma nyan/ de nas nag tshos gtsug
lag khang gi sgo drung du shes rab snying po'i med kyi thad du/ gzugs ha/ tshor ba ha byas pas/ paNDi ta gzhan rnams cang mi gsung ba la/ jo bo zhal 'dzum mdzad de tshe
dang ldan pa de phal skad yin/ gzugs a/ tshor ba a zer ba yin gsung/ nang par de ltar bton pas jo bo'i zhal nas/ de yang gyong po gcig yong bar snang/ spyan ras gzigs kyi
gsung yin/ gzugs med/ tshor ba med gyis gsungs pas/ lhag par dad de rjes su 'brangs pa na/ sprang po'i tshogs la zan gnang ba mthong bas/ byis pa gcig gi skal ba chad de
phyi la brgyug cing/ a ti sha bha la ho/ bha ra 'on zer ba thos pas a ti sha yin nges snyam nas yus kyis dngangs te phyi la phyin pas/ der bzhugs te/ tshe dang ldan pa
bden/ mchi ma ma 'byin/ khyed bod da dung ngas blos btang ba med kyi/ dkon mchog la gsol ba thob gsung/ de nas lan gcig rgya'i gzims khang du tshul khrims rgyal bas jo bo
spyan drangs nas gser srang bdun brgya maNDal dang bcas pa phul/ jo bo spyan 'dren pa la bod kyi mi nor song ba dang chos rgyal khu dbon gyis khyed kyi phyogs su dka' ba
spyad lugs/ bod na log chos yod tshul la sogs pa/ lha btsun pas zhu ba bskur ba rnams rgya brtson 'grus seng ges rgyas par snyan du gsol te/ da de yang tshe dang ldan pa
'di jo bo spyan 'dren pa la btang bar 'dug pa/ mgon po la de gnyis kyis ji tsam pa'i dka' ba spyad kyang 'dod pa'i don ma grub pa de bod kyi sems can rnams snying mi rje
'am/ lhag par yang gung thang

pa 'di rab tu byung nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la thos bsam ma gtogs/ mi 'grub pa'i bya ba ma bab/ da lan cis kyang 'byon par mdzad du gsol lo zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/
khyed lo tsA ba rnams shin du bden/ bod kyi chos rgyal de'i mi nor mang po song bas ngo mnong/ kho bo snying rje chung ba min gyang yang bstan pa'i bya ba ches/ gtsug lag
khang brgya rtsa brgyad kyi lde mig dang chos 'phro mang po yang yod/ na so yang rgas pas thon par dka' mod/ 'on kyang bod kyi chos rgyal khu dbon dang/ lo tsA ba rnams
pa'i dka' spyad chud ma zos cig bya'i/ re shig zhig gser rnams tshags mdzod nged bod du 'ong skad ma zer/ lo tsA mkhas par slobs gsung/ de'i nub mo rje btsun ma sgrol ma
la maNDal phul te/ bod du phyin na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la phan nam/ rgyal po byang chub sems dpa'i thugs dgongs rdzogs sam/ lus srog gi bar chad du mi 'gyur ram zhes
zhus pas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la phan zhing/ rgyal po'i thugs dgongs rdzogs/ khyad par du u pA sa si ka cig la brten nas 'gro ba mang po la phan pas the tshom med
par bod du bzhud/ ces zhes lung bstan/ de nas jo bo'i zhal nas/ rdo rje gdan du 'ong dang gsung bas/ der phyin pa na/ byis pa gzhon nu dar dkar gyi gos gyon pa/ shel dkar
gyi mda' gzhu thogs pa cig byung ste/ phyag 'tshal zhing da mgon po bod du 'byon par zhu/ bod kyi tshe dang ldan pa 'di kun snying rje mod zer te song/ jo bo la bod skad
smra ba'i byis pa de su yin zhus pas/ nang par rdo rje gdan gyi byang phyogs nas rnal 'byor ma cig song bas/ de la dris gsung/ nang par rnal 'byor ma kraShNa skad la dkris
pa Da ma ru dkrol zhing gar stabs ling nge ba cig byung

ba la/ khar kha sang gi lo brgyus rgyus dris pas/ khyed bod kyi mi nged rgya gar ba la 'dri ba zer nas song/ yang jo bo byang chub chen po'i drung na bzhugs pa'i g.yas g.yon
na/ kha sang gi byis pa de dang bu mo sngo ljang ma cig 'dug pas/ lo tsA ba'i rtog pa la 'di gnyis kyi dbus su jo bo bzhugs mi thang ba la snyam pa dang/ bu mo na re/ rgyal
ba'i mdun na rgyal sras bzang po skyong/ rgyal bar gnas kyang ma rgyal lta bur ston/ rgyal ba'i mdzad pa mthar phyin 'gro ba'i mgon/ rgyal ba yas sras gnyis la phyag
'tshal lo/ zeer/ byis pa na re/ gang du rgyal ba'i rnam thar skyong ba na/ bu mo khyod kyang bdag gi khyim 'ong zhing/ bu dang long spyod dpal 'byor spel ba dang/ dga' bar
'grogs shing bar chad bsal 'tshal lo/ he he/ da jo bo yang bod du 'byon ran zer nas/ khong gnyis gzhan du song/ sprul pa cig yin par shes nas/ jo lo nged bod nas 'phags
nas phan 'dogs kyi sprul pa zam ma chad pa cig byung ba de rnams kyang gsung ba dang/ phar gshegs pa'i go cha yang myur du mdzad par zhu zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ bi
kra ma'i pho brang gi lho sgo na bu mo ras 'thag pa cig yod de la dris gsung/ der phyin nas dris pas/ khyed 'dod na dge bsnyen grags che ba ji skad bya ba yod zer bas/ dge
bsnyen chos 'phel bya ba yod dris pas / mo na re/ u pA sa si ka de/ a ti sha yi sras po ma lags sam/ dus rnams rtag tu sprul pa bstan pa yin/ zhes sogs glu blangs pas/
bal po rdzong gi mi ring nas/ kha sang gi byis pa bu mo gnyis kyi bar rnams dge bsnyen chos 'phel gyi sprul par snang ba la snyam nas sems ngal sos par gyur/ de dus jo bo'i
bla ma du ha ra nag po bya bas/ sa dpyad rin chen 'phrul gyi me long bya ba

jo bo la gnang nas/ khyed shod du 'gro bar 'dug/ gdan sa byang skyabs pa/ lho gzhol ba/ rtsi shing nags tshal dang ldan pa zhig 'ong/ khyed kyi bu slob mang pos dge 'dun gyi
sde dang/ gtsug lag khang mang po bzhengs par 'gyur/ de tsa na 'di dgos pa yin gsung/ de nas rim pa ltar bla ma dharma rakShi ta/ rje btsun DomI ba/ bla ma a ba dhU tI
pa/ ku sA li rig pa'i khu byug dang/ yi dam lha'i lung bstan ji snyed cig rnam thar dngos grub kyi 'od zer du 'byung ba las/ rang bzhin gyi rnal 'byor mas lung bstan pa phyogs
tsam zhig 'dir bshad na/ gcig lan gcig dkyil 'khor gcig la zhugs pa na/ rdo rje'i gar dang mchod pa phul ba'i rjes/ ma gcig rang bzhin dbyings kyi rnal 'byor ma/ rus
pa'i rgyan cha gsol nas gar la byon/ hUM zhes rnam dag rdo rje'i glur blangs nas/ mi mngon dbyings na tshogs gnyis dpal 'byor ba'i/ dpa' bo chen po dam tshig rol ba'i lha/
khyab bdag rin chen tshogs kyi bdag po khyod/ ye shes gsang ba'i rdo rje ma lags sam/ khyod kyis rdo rje theg pa'i sgor zhugs nas/ byang phyogs rgyud kyi mtha' mkhob
ma btul na/ las kyi dpa' bo chen por mi rung bas/ myur du ri bo gangs can rgyud du song/ de na rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul pa yod/ gcig ni brum rje sprul pa'i chos 'phel lo/
gcig ni rngog ston legs pa'i shes rab bo/ gcig ni khu ston brtson 'grus g.yung drung ngo/ gzhan yang thub pa mchog gis byin brlabs pa'i/ sprul pa'i dge slong shin du mang
bar yod/ de dag thams cad khyod kyi sras su 'gyur/ gangs can rgyud der bstan pa dar bar byed/ der song chos kyi bya ba 'di ltar mdzod/ rdo rje theg pa nang du dar bar
mdzod/ gzhung lugs rgya mtsho phyi ru dar bar mdzod/ bslab gsum rnam dag rang rang dar bar mdzod/ las can brtags shing

bcud kyis smin par mdzod/ tshig gi spros pa mtha' nas chod par mdzod/ shes rab rtogs pa nang nas rgyas par mdzod/ phrin las bzang po phyogs mthar khyab par mdzod/ gdul bya
yongs la phyogs ris med par mdzod/ sgo gsum thub pa chen por brtan par mdzod/ gnyen po mi g.yo mgon po tshags par mdzod/ 'gro drug thugs rje chen por brtse bar mdzod/ 'gro
ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad sgrol bar mdzod/ bslab pa gsum gyis nyin mtshan phyug par mdzod/ lha chos bdun gyi 'byor pas phyug pa'i tshe/ gsang sngags lhun gyis grub par
mchi 'o ang/ zhes gsungs la/ de ltar bla ma dang/ yi dam rnams kyis bod kha ba can du 'byon par lung bstan na yang/ a ti sha bstan pa'i bya ba la gzhis ches pa dang/ gnas
brtan ratnA a ka ra la sogs pa jo bo bod du 'byon pa la mii dga' ba rnams kyis tshor dgos pa dang/ rdo rje gdan gyi rgyal po la sogs pa mi re re tsam gyis shol btab pas/
gtsug lag khang sogs mchod cing yam yom du lus pa na/ lan gcig jo bo rdo rje gdan du byon pa'i rjes su/ lo tsA gnyis kyis byon nas/ zhabs la gtugs te gdong mchi mas gang
bzhin du gsol ba yang yang btab pas/ jo bos kyang bod du 'byon pa'i thag chod kyi zhal bzhes dang / gtsug lag khang gi gnyer gtad thams cad mdzad de/ gzhan gyi mig brid
pa'i phyir res gar gshegs res gar gshegs pa ltar mdzad nas/ bood du 'byon par chas pa na/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang/ dos rnams/ sprul pa'i mi gnyis kyis g.yag khyu gcig
ded byung ste/ sa thag ring por 'gro ba la zar snga dgos pa yin zer nas drangs song/ nang par jo bos gnas

brtan ratnA a ka ra la/ bod 'di rnams la gnas chen rnams kyi gtsug lag khang ston pa dang/ mchod pa re skyel du 'gro bas bde bar bzhugs pa zhu gsungs pas/ gnas brtan gyi zhal
nas de ltar legs/ nged kyang rjes su 'jug par zhu zer nas/ gnas chen mang du byon pa'i rjes su gnas brtan chen po nged mi tra'i gtsug lag khang du 'gro bas/ khyed bshul
thag ring po la 'o rgyal gsungs pas/ gnas brtan gyi thugs la da bod du 'byon par snang snyam nas/ nag tsho la tshe dang ldan pa khyod slob gnyer la 'ongs zer nas/ nga'i
paNDi ta brkur 'ongs par snang/ 'on kyang bod kyi chos rgyal byang chub sems dpa' de la sems brtse zhing/ de'i mi nor mang po chud zos pa dang/ khyod kyang nga'i slob ma
yin pas lo gsum spyan drongs/ de nas tshur spyan ma drangs na/ rgya gar yang bstan pa nub pa tsam du 'gro ba yod gsungs bas/ nag tshos kyang khas blangs/ der jo bo'i zhal
nas/ gser rnams khyer la shog gsung nas/ cha bzhir bgos te bla ma rnams dang/ dge 'dun spyi dang/ bi kra ma'i rgyal po dang/ gtsug lag khang rnams la bsngos/ gtad gnyer
thams cad gnas brtan ratnA a ka ra la mdzad de phyir ldog go/ de yang jo bo dgung lo nga bdun bzhes pa stag gi lo la rgya gar nas bteg/ kha gcig nga dgu bzhes pa'i lcags
pho 'brug la bteg pa dang/ kha gcig dgung lo re gcig la bteg par 'dod de/ snga ma 'thad par sem mo/ de nas jo bo dpon slob mi tra'i gtsug lag khang nas rgya gar gyi sa'i
mthaX' la byon pa na/ mu stegs kyi gcer bu pa bcu bco brgyad tsam rdzu 'phrul gyis nga rgyal ba/ bod du sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar ba la phra dog gis der rdzu 'phrul gyis
lhags nas

jo bo dpon slob rnams la bar chad byed par brtsams pas/ jo bos sgrol ma'i skyed rim gyis rengs par byed pa'i jag chings mdzad de/ thams cad lter cho bzhin du song/ de nas bal
po'i mthar phebs pa na/ mu stegs bsam pa ngan pas rang phung bar byas pa yin gsung nas/ bye ma la sngar btab te tshong pa la bskur nas/ lam kha na gzer phul 'di 'dra ba
yod pas bye ma 'di gtor/ langs 'ong gi bred mi dgos nged kyis bcings pa yin gsung/ tshong pa rnams kyis de ltar byas pas grol te song ngo/ de nas 'phags pa shing kun du
phyags phebs pa na/ rgya gar nas khyer ba'i dos rnams dang/ lha btsun pa'i bsu ba gtso bo mi bcu drug kyang der sleb/ dkon mchog gi mchod pa dang/ bod lugs kyi gdan gyi
bkod pa bzang po bshams jo bo ta la'i bsil grib la gral gyi gung la spyan drangs/ gtso bo sum pa bya bas dkar yol 'brug rgyab gser srang lnga ri ba ja btso mas bkang ste
phul bas/ 'di la ci zer gsung/ bod kyi rab tubyung btung ba ja zer zhus pas shin du mnyes/ ja bu ram sogs kyis bsnyen bkur/ gtso bo lo drug gis rta mchog dkar po mthong smon
khyung gshog bya ba rin po che sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa zhig dang/ dar dkar po yug re phul/ der dge bsnyen chos 'phel gyi sprul pa 'brog phrug gcig gis li yul nas jo
bo 'jam dpal rde rje/ li'i rgyal po'i zhu yig dang bcas te phebs pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas rten 'brel thams cad legs gsung ste shin du mnyes/ dus der lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng
mnyel ba'i tshul bstan nas/ da ni u pA si ka phod/ nga ni rang bzhin gnas su 'gro/ mi la yid ches mi skye bas/

shi ba skad du dur du skyol/ nga ni 'od gsal sems kyi lus/ 'byung gnas de la thim nas 'gro/ rgya bod gnyis su bya ba byas/ kha ba can du gcig gis chog/ ces gsungs te/ mkha'
spyod du gshegs so/ de nas jo bo dpon slob bal po'i rgyal po grags pa mtha' yas kyis spyan drangs/ jo bo'i chibs glang po che mthong smon bya ba/ rgyal po la gnang ste/
nga thang 'dir bi ha ra zhes pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs pas/ 'byor pa ci dgos pa dang/ rgya gar dang bod kyi rab tu byung ba la sa tra 'dzugs pa'i rgyu byin cig ces gsungs
pas/ rgyal po dad de zhabs spyi bor blangs/ gang bzhed pa thams cad bsgrub par dam bcas/ sras padma'i snying po phul nas rab tu byung/ mtshan lha'i dbang por btags/ mkhas
par gyur nas phyis thang bi ha ra'i mkhan po mdzad do/ de nas a ti sha dpon slob rnams bal po'i rgyal po skyel thung ba rta pa brgyas bskor ba dang bcas te bal po rdzong
la phyags phebs pa na der lha btsun pa'i rta pa sum brgya tsam bsu ba la gos dkar po 'ba' zhig gyon/ rgyan thams cad kyang dkar po 'ba' zhig byas/ blon po chen po lha'i
dbang phyug dang/ lha'i blo gros dang/ lha'i shes rab dang/ lha'i srid 'dzin zhes bya ba bzhi la/ dar mdung dkar po thogs pa bcu drug bcu drug gis bskor/ gzhan thams
cad la yang ba dan chung ngu re dang/ chu dar gyi gdugs nyi shu dang/ pi wang dang gling bu'i sgra snyan po 'khrol ba dang/ dpon g.yog thams cad kyang ngag mthun par dkon
mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro zhing/ bod du sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar 'gyur ro zhes pa'i kha brda bzang po byed pa dang/ a ti sha la gnod pa'i phas rgol thams cad
bdag gis gzhom

par bya'o zhes dpa' bskyed pa dang/ thams cad rta las mi 'babs par gral sgor ram cig byas te/ dbus su a ti sha chibs mthong smon khyung gshog gi steng na bzhugs te/ sku 'khor
paNDi ta gzhan la phan pa bzang po dang/ paNDi ta birya tsantra dang/ paNDi ta ye shes sgron me dang/ lo tsA ba gung thang pa la sogs pa rab tu byung ba'i rta pa sum cu
rtsa lnga lngas bskor ba dbus su bzhugs pa la/ mi rta thams cad kyi mgo nang du 'dud cing/ blon po chen po bzhis dbus su 'ongs te/ sngon rgyal po yon mchod zhal 'dzom pa'i
thog mar/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa'i drung du/ blon po rig pa can rnams kyis zor ma'i glu blangs pa ltar/ blon po rnams kyis glu mdzad pa ni/ lo zhes bya ba grag stong
snyan pa'i glu dbyangs lo/ a zhes bya ba skye ba med pa'i gnas lugs yin/ le zhes bya ba snang stong zung du 'jug pa'i glu/ ma zhes bya ba byams pas 'gro ba yongs la khyab/
lo de zhes pa de tsam thugs la gzhag 'tshal lo/ a lo la zhes bya ba skye ba med kyang gtam 'di gson/ khyed rgya gar yul nas byon pa'i mkhas grub paNDi ta/ yid bsam pa bzhin
du 'grub pa'i nor bu rin chen bzhin/ bod gsol ba 'debs pa'i rten du byon pa bka' drin che/ zhes pa nas/ nged snying stobs chen po'i lha btsun drung nas 'ongs/ lus rkang
pa'i mthil nas tshangs pa man chad 'di/ sems gus dang bcas te bla ma khyed la 'bul/ lha khyed kyi phrin las gang dgos nged kyis bsgrub/ rje rgyal po'i mnga' ris dpal
gyi gtsug lag der/ thugs mi skyo mi mnyel rang yul lags pas 'byon par zhu/ lha btsun pa byang chub 'od de lha dbang brgya byin ltar/ 'khor nye dbang lta bu'i bkur gnas mdzad
cing lha mer bzhugs/ lo a le la

lo de a lo la/ zhes blon po rta pa gsum brgya dang bcas pas/ rje'i snyan du glu dbyangs de phul ba dang/ a ti sha chibs kyi steng na khru gang tsam 'phags te/ sku'i dkyil 'khor
mtshan dpes spras pa/ zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas pas a ti a ti/ pha la pha la/ shin du bkra shis zhes sogs dang/ 'di ltar rgyan dkar ba/ gos dkar ba/ tshig thams cad dam
pa'i chos su 'byung ba/ blon po 'di dag gi lugs kyis chos kyi rgyal po lha btsun pa de/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin dang khyad par med par bzhugs nges shes zhes gsung/ de
nas blon po chen po lha'i dbang phyug gis/ jo bo'i drung du thal mo sbyar nas/ bstan pa'i bdag po bod du byon lags sam/ sems can rnams la brtse bar byon lags sam/ e ma dus
gsum 'doms par byon lags sam/ bshul ring lam la mnyel bar ma gyur tam/ zhes zhus te/ spyan ras gzigs kyi sku rtsa phyag bzhi bcu pa bris ma thag cig phyag rten du phul
ba dang/ mgon po shin du dgyes nas/ de ma thag rab gnas mdzad cing/ spyan ras gzigs dbang 'jig rten gsum gyi mgon/ gzhan la phan phyir brtson pa'i go cha bsnams/ thugs rje'i
rang bzhin dri med dkyil 'khor can/ 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal sel la phyag 'tshal lo/ ding sang kho bo khyed kyi zhing 'dir mchis/ thugs rjes 'gro ba'i don du skyab tu gsol/
zhes gsung/ de nas blon po gzhan rnams kyis kyang ras yug dkar po re phyag rten du phul lo/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ kho bo da gzod zhing 'dir sleb par 'ongs/ 'khor ba'i nags
su bde ba ma mchis na'ang/ bshul rings lam la 'byung bzhi snyoms par byung/ chos rgyal 'khor bcas gzhi la bde lags sam gsung/ de nas thams ngag mthun par/ lha chen po

gdul bya'i dbang gis zhing gzhan du gshegs na'ang/ phyis dkon mchog gi skyabs 'og nas/ lha btsun chen pos dbu bgyis/ blon 'bangs thams cad bkra shis yar yod ces zhus/ de nas
jo bo dpon slob rim gyis mtsho ma pham gyi 'gram du phyags phebs/ der chu sbyin mdzad pa gung thang pas gzigs pas/ mtsho'i dkyil na kha sarpa Na bzhengs pa'i phyag gi mthil
na hri: dkar po gcig las bdud rtsi'i rgyun babs pas mtsho lud pa tsam du gyur pa yi dgas dpag tu med pas 'thungs te tshim pa mthong/ de nas a ti sha mtsho ma pham gyi
'gram du phebs zer ba mnga' ris skor gsum gyis thos/ de'i tshe mnga' ris na rin bzang bal por ha su zhes mnyam par grags pas/ a ti sha bstan pa'i mnga' bdag/ bal po'i rgyal
po la sogs pas zhabs spyi bor blangs pa/ bal po ha sus ma bzod par/ mnga' ris na mar rnal 'byor pa 'khyam po btang nas/ a ti sha'i phyir du mi nor de tsam gtong ba las/
bal po ha su bos na/ da tsam mi nor chos gsum 'dzom pa cig 'ong bar yod de/ ces bsgrags kyang gnod par ma nus/ de nas blon po lha'i blo gros kyis mnga' ris su lha btsun
pa'i drung du sleb nas zhu ba mdzad pa/ thams cad mkhyen pas bal por phebs/ bal po'i rgyal po 'khor dang bcas pas bsnyen bkur zhing / rgyal po yab yum sras rta pa brgya'i
tshogs dang/ a ti sha'i 'khor paNDi ta chen po gsum/ gung thang pa la sogs pa sde snod 'dzin pa sum bcu/ rgyal po sa'i seng gha zhes pa rgya gar nub phyogs thams cad
kyi bdag po rgyal srid spangs nas a ti sha'i thugs dam bskul ba'i rkyen mdzad du byon pa/ mdor na bsu skyel ba rta pa bzhi brgya sum bcu rtsa

lnga tsam/ mtsho ma pham pa'i 'gram na bzhugs nas skye bo'i tshogs dpag tu med pa'i don mdzad de/ ring por mi thogs par yar gling gser gyi lha khang du phebs par yod pas/ thugs
dgyes par zhu zhes zhus pas/ lha btsun chen po dgyes pa'i mthar thug nas/ ngas dad gus ma log par gsol ba rgyun du btab nas yun ring song ste/ da a ti sha dang mjal
ba yin/ mdang rmi lam na nub phyogs nas nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor cig shar byung ba dang/ shar phyogs nas zla ba'i dkyil 'khor nya gang ba cig shar byung ba lhan cig tu 'tshogs
pas/ sprin dang khu rdul thams cad rang sar dengs/ skar tshogs gra ma nyams par 'dud pa rmis pas/ zla ba de nga yin nam snyam yang / shar phyogs nas byung ba gang yin kyang
des go chod par snang/ rmi ltas shin du bzang gsung/ de nas lha btsun pas yang gling gser gyi lha khang du rta pa gtang ste/ lam po che dang/ gnas thams cad la byi dor
dang/ dar zab kyis brgyan te/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang/ mchod pa'i bye brag bsam gyis mi khyab pa bshom du bcug/ gzhan yang phyogs kun du pho nya gtang ste/ jo bo
la bsu ba'i phyir du skye bo'i tshogs dang/ sde dgon gyi rab tu byung ba thams cad bsdus pas/ lha btsun pa khu dbon gyis dka' spyad de tsam byas pa'i paNDi ta de ya mtshan
pa ci 'dra zhig snang ba blta'o zer nas lam ring thung thams cad du skye bo'i tshogs chen po 'dus/ lha btsun pas kyang 'khor rta pa drug brgya dang lhan cig tu byon nas
jo bo dpon slob spyan drangs/ der thams cad kyis jo bo la bltas pa na/ paNDi ta dang/ gung thang pa la sogs sde snod 'dzin pa dang/ bal po'i rgyal po la sogs pa'i dbus
na/ mtshan dang dpe byad

kyis brgyan pa lha mer bzhugs pa mthong bas/ skyabs su mchi'o zhes pa dang/ da ni 'jig rten gyi mgon po bod du byon no/ bdag cag bod kyi sems can rnams la thugs rjes gzigs
shig ces dad pa phyogs gcig tu 'ur ba dang/ lha btsun pas kyang jo bo la/ bla ma rje btsun chen po'i zhal snga nas/ rgya gar yul nas bod kyi yul du byon/ bshul thag rings
pas sku nyon ma mongs sam/ 'du ba rnam bzhi'i sku snyun mi mnga' 'am/ sku khams bde 'am dgyes par spyod lags sam/ sku gsung thugs la gnod pa mi mnga' 'am/ zhes gsol te/
bdag cag bod kyi skye bo phal cher ni/ bla ma dang bral rang gar smra ba ste/ kla klo'i spyod pa ma rungs spyod pa rnams/ a ti sha yis bzod pa mdzad du gsol/ zhes bod spyi'i
bzod gsol dang / de nas lo tsA ba la rje slob dpon tshul khrims rgyal ba'i spyan snga nas/ re ba che bas bdag gis thugs dam zhus/ thugs la btags nas rgya gar yul du byon/
dka' ba mang po spyad pa bzod par gsol/ de nas jo bos bod du 'gro don 'byung bar smon lam btab pa/ e ma ho dge slong byang chub 'od bdag gis/ rtag tu bsams pa'i bla
ma spyan 'drongs drongs pas/ bod kyi yul du skyes bu dam pa 'di'i/ gzhung lugs shin du dar zhing rgyas par shog/ ces zhus pas/ jo bo mnyes nas/ bod kyi sems can rnams kho
bo la 'di ltar dad pa che ba/ phan bde'i 'byung gnas dkon mchog gsum/ nga'i gdul bya theg pa chen po'i rigs can 'di rnams la thugs rjes zung zhig gsung nas/ khrom thams
cad la gzigs shing byin brlabs mdzad/ de nas mtho lhing padmo'i gling du phebs nas/ a ti shas bal po'i rgyal

po la/ khyod kyis thang bi ha ri'i gtsug lag khang dang/ lho'i phyogs su dge 'dun gyi 'du khang/ rgya bod gnyis kyi rab tu byung ba la pa tra legs par tshugs/ de'i sa brtag
pa sogs rten 'brel thams cad kho bo rang gis tshar yod/ de'i nang du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dgung lo brgyad pa'i tshad/ seng ldeng la rje btsun ma sgrol ma'i sku/ rdo
la rje btsun mi g.yo ba'i sku/ tsan dan gyi lde gu la spyan ras gzigs kyi sku/ gtsug tor dre med kyi sku la sogs pa gang grub bzhengs/ de'i bkod pa la paNDi ta gsum po gtong
bas zla ba dgu'i nang du grub pa gyis/ rab tu gnas pa kho bo rang la brda sbyor gsung / de nas bal po'i rgyal po 'khor bcas phyir log pa na/ lha btsun pas bsnyen bkur
te/ rta sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang/ paNDi ta gsum la yang gser srang re phul te/ lnga brgya'i dus 'dir dam chos rnam mang yang/ lam du 'gro ba brgya lam srid pa tsam/ bla mar
bzhugs pa shin du mang na yang/ a ti sha nyid gcig pu nyid du zad/ bal po'i thang nas skyel du byon pa legs/ zhabs gla'i tshul du rta yi tshogs 'di 'bul/ skye rga na 'chi'i
chu bo rab soms la/ rgyal po'i dregs pa spongs la gzhan don bsten/ zhes gsungs pas/ bal po'i rgyal po dgyes bzhin du/ gser srang sum brgya sras lha'i dbang po'i lag
tu gtad de/ lha btsun pa la phul nas/ bal po'i rgyal pos gsol pa/ rgyal rigs lus la rnam dag khrims ldan zhing/ sangs rgyas bstan la dpa' ba'i go gyon nas/ 'jig rten sgron
me bod du spyan drangs te/ thams cad chos la 'god pa ngo mtshar che/ bdag gis bskyed pa'i bu 'di rje la 'bul/ bsam pa bzang po gser dang 'dra ba 'di/

chos rgyal bod du chos grwa 'dzugs pa la/ gser srang sum brgya shig zhig 'degs su 'bul/ slad ma sangs rgyas bstan pa dar ba dang/ a ti sha yang phyogs 'dir yun ring zhing/
bdag kyang 'phreng bas yun du 'grogs par zhu/ zhes zhus te rgyal po paNDi ta gsum dang bcas pa bal por byon/ de nas a ti sha dpon slob lha btsun pas dbu bgyis bsu ba'i rta
ba dgu brgya'i 'khor dang/ rag dung yang lha btsun pa'i thugs shes kyis mdzad de/ lo paN spyen spyan 'dren gyi rgyud bya bar grags gsung ste/ de la sogs pa rol mo'i tshogs
dang bcas te/ rgyal po'i pho brang du spyan drangs bsnyen bkur te/ bod 'dir chos zab zab po las kyang thog mar las rgyu 'bras la brten pa'i chos kyis bskyang bar zhu
zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ chos kyi gnad go ba'i gtam yin/ nan ltar zab pa las rgyu 'bras kho na yin/ yi dam gyi lha zhal mthong ba bas/ las rgyu 'bras la yid ches na de
nyid mchog tu gyur pa yin te/ gshin rje gshed kyi rnal 'byor pa dang / bi kra ma'i gnas brtan gyi lo brgyus rgyus gsungs nas de ltar mdzad pas/ mnga' ris su paNDi ta rgyu
'bras par grags te/ zhi bo'i ming tsam gyis kyang bstan pa la phan par byas gsung nas mnyes/ de'i dus bod dbus gtsang gi mkhas pa phal che ba der 'tshogs te/ lta ba'i gnad
la sogs pa bstan pa rin po che las brtsams pa'i dri ba yang du zhus pas/ rang rang gi the tshom gyi dra ba chod par mdzad do/ de nas lo tsA ba nag tshos/ da ni jo bo
bod du lo gcig las mi bzhugs pa'i chad po yod pas/ chos zhu ba rnams zhus shig ces lha btsun pa sogs la bskul bas/ jo bo la lha btsun pas gser srang sum brgya'i me tog dang
bcas te/ bod kyi yul

'dir theg pa chen po'i lam la log par rtog pa'i gang zag / dge ba'i bshen gnyen gyis ma zin pa dag phan tshun rtsod cing/ rang rang gi rtog ges zab pa dang rgya che ba'i don
la dpyod cing/ so sor mi mthun pa dag mchis pas/ de dag gi the tshom bsal du gsol zhes pa dang/ gzhan yang theg pa thun mong ba'i dri ba gnyis/ pha rol du phyin pa'i dri
ba gnyis/ gsang sngags la dri ba gsum la sogs pa mang du zhus nas/ byams pa dang klu sgrub nas brgyud pa'i gdam ngag bla ma nyid kyis thugs nyams su bzhes pa tshig nyung
la don rgyas pa cig mdzad par zhu zhus pas/ mdo sngags gnyis ka'i gnad bsdus nas ston pas brjod bya yongs su rdzogs pa dang/ sems 'dul ba'i rim pa gtso bor mdzad pas lag
tu blang bde ba dang/ shing rta chen po gnyis kyi lugs la mkhas pa'i bla ma gnyis kyi gdams pas brgyan pa lugs gzhan las khyad par du 'phags pa byang chub lam gyi sgron
ma mdzad/ yang lha btsun pas/ rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa/ man ngag ye shes zhabs lugs dang/ gtso bo spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs zhus pas/ gsang 'dus 'jig rten
dbang phyug gi lha bcu dgu'i bsgrub thabs mdzad de gnang ngo/ de'i tshe lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos/ rgyal pos spyan drangs lugs/ dka' spyad du ma'i mthar spyan 'drongs
tshul dang/ paNDi ta'i yon tan gyi khyad par mtha' yas pa/ sngar nas kyang thos shing/ rang phyogs su byon tshul rnams gsan pas/ dus deng sang nga las yon tan che ba med
dam/ paNDi ta byon kyang zhu rgyu tsam ma mchis/ lhag par yang paNDi ta de 'dul khrims dang mdo sde la rtsal du 'don pa gcig 'dug zer/ de'i rigs la theg pa chen po gasngags
kyi lugs 'byung ba shin du dka'/ lar gang zag  bzang po cig

yin par shes/ rmii ltas la sogs pa'ang bzang / cung zad cig bsus nas bsnyen bkur bya ba bab snyam du sems pa'i de nub rmi lam na mi reng dkar po cig byung nas/ kho bo sems
can gyi don la byas yus che/ 'on kyang rgyal ba spyan 'dren pa la dka' spyad du ma byas da dung mi shes pa zhu rgyu mang du mchis/ lo tsA ba thos rtags zhi zhing dul ba bya
ba yin/ rgya bod kyi lo paN thams cad kyi yon tan dril kyang/ paNDi ta'i gzhung gi yon tan mi rdzogs/ bod 'di kun man ngag gi sna rtses 'dul ba yin/ man ngag thams cad
bod kyi mi lon zer nas gtam 'dri long med par yal nas song/ lo tsA ba gnyid sad pa dang/ paNDi ta de snying rje che ba cig yod par 'dug/ sna la thugs rje chen po 'ong ba
de bzang snyam/ de nas nang par thag ring po nas bsus te/ sku'i spyod pa la bltas pas chog ma shes/ rim gyis rang gi khang par spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur bar bzhed pa la/
paNDi ta dang khong rang stan mnyam pa tsam bshams/ de nas paNDi tas nang du byon pa dang/ lha khang thog na theg pa thun mong gi lha bod lugs su bzhengs nas yod pa la/
phyag la sogs pa saM skr-i ta'i skad kyis yan lag bdun pa mdzad de/ lha re la bstod pa tshig bzhi pa re mdzad cing 'dug/ de bzhin du bar khang na theg pa chen po'i lha
sku mang po yod pa dang/ sum thog na gasngags bla med kyi lha sku mang po yod pa la'ang yan lag bdun pa phul nas lha re re la rang rang gi rgyud dang mthun pa'i bstod pa
tshigs su bcad pa tshig bzhi pa re mdzad der lo tsA bas saM skr-i ta'i skad snyan po de thos pas/ snyan ngag phul du phyin pa 'dug pa dang/ sngar ma gzigs pa'i lha rigs rnams
la'ang bstod pa mdzad pas/ theg pa chen po la'ang de 'dra na

dang tshugs nye bar 'khor yin nam snyam pa la brten nas rang gi stan la 'brid thebs gsum byas/ mthar stan med pa tsam du nga rgyal skyungs/ de nas bsnyen bkur te/ lo tsA bas
rgya gar gyi lo brgyus rgyus mang po dris pas/ sgro skur med par tshang ba lan du byung/ de nas yoon tan gang la mkhas zhus pas/ khyed thun mong ba la zer ram/ thun mong
ma yin pa la zer gsung/ lo tsA bas thun mong ba la shin tu mkhas thun mong ma yin pa la 'dri ba yin gsung bar go nas/ thun mong ma yin pa la lags mod zhus pas/ kho bo 'di
dang 'di la'ang mkhas gsung nas/ lo tsA bas rna bar ma thos pa'ang mang po bton nas byung/ der lo tsA ba'i nga rgyal thams cad zhi/ de nas paNDi ta'i zhal nas/ 'dul ba/
mdo sde/ mngon pa/ gasngags la sogs pa du ma las brtsams te/ 'di shes sam/ 'di shes sam zhes dris pas/ kho bo de la'ang mkhas zer ba min pa ma byung / paNDi ta de la shin
du mnyes nas/ khyod lta bu yod pa la kho bo bod du 'ong mi 'tshal bar 'dug pa la zhes pa'ang gsung/ yang lo tsA ba de dag thams cad gdan thog gcig tu hril te hril nas
nyams su len na ji ltar byed gsungs pas/ lo tsA ba na re/ theg pa ma 'dres so sor gsal/ bya ba phyed la ma 'dres par/ rang sar nyams su len lags mod/ zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal
nas/ lo tsA ba ngan par thal/ bod la kho bo dgos par 'dug gsung nas lan gzhan mi smra bar bzhugs/ de'i nub mo lo tsA bas/ nam thun gsum du bgos nas/ gnas gsum du rim gyi
theg pa'i mtho dman dang bstun te bsgoms pas/ khong gi spyod pa thams cad paNDi tas mkhyen nas/ nang par lo tsA ba/ tsab ta tsob ta mang pos ci bgyid/ gang gi dam pa rdo
rje'i gdan gnon dgos pa yin gsung /

der lo tsA bas theg pa'i nyams su len lugs zhus pas/ lo tsA ba des mi 'ong gsung/ 'o na khyed rang ji ltar mdzad lags zhus pas ci zer gnas gar sdod/ grogs su dang 'grogs/ spyod
lam ci byed kyang 'dul khrims la gzhi byas la/ sems can thams cad ma yin pas der bsgom dgos/ ma lhar dag snang sbyong / lha skye med yin pas der bsgom 'dril ma shes
na snying po mi lon zhes gsung nas/ 'di skad du  khrims ni yon tan kun gyi gzhir/ rang gi ston pas legs par gsungs/ snying rje chen po dang 'brel ba'i/ byang chub sems ni
mchog tu bsngags/ bzang rtog mtshan mas ma bcings pa'i/ skyed rdzogs zung 'brel nges 'tshang rgya/ skyes bu chung dang cher gyur pa'i/ bya ba 'di yin 'bring po la'ang/ mi
rtag brtson pas bskul ba gces/ rang dga' spangs nas rgyal ba'i bka'/ rgyas par byed pa mkhas pa yin/ snying por bsdus nas nyams len pa'i/ skyes bu de ni bzang por grags/
las 'bras khyad du mi gsod pa'i/ bag yod can de btsun por bzhed/ kun shes gcig brdugs mkhas pa'i skyon/ lag len mi byed 'chal pa yin/ blang dor mi byed btsun po'i gsob/
shes par mdzod cig rin chen bzang/ thugs rje chen pos bskul bar zad/ ces gsung/ lo tsA bas dam par shes nas/ lha yi lhar gyur paNDi ta/ rnam dag sku mchog khrims kyis spras/
don gnyis 'byor pa'i nor gyis phyug/grol nas 'dren par kho bos 'tshal/ kho bo'i lung rigs sgron me yis/ sbas pa khyod kyi yon tan mthong/ sngan sngon chad tshig dang
'gal na yang/ da ni khyed bzhin nyams su blang/ zhes bstod do/ gzhan yang mdo sngags kyi chos rang rang gi skal ba dang 'tsham par gnang ste/ bod log

par lta ba lung rigs kyis tshar bcad/ the tshoom za ba spang blang gi mig phye nas/ bstan pa ches gsal bar mdzad do/ 'dir smras pa/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab nyin mor byed pa yis/
log smra'i mun pa mtha' dag drungs phyung nas/ yang dag lam bzang ches cher gsal mdzad pa/ bstan pa'i nyi ma gnyis pa deng 'dir shar/ de ltar lha btsun pa sogs kyi thugs
dgongs rdzogs par mdzad nas/ bal po'i rgyal por/ paNDi ta dang bcas pas gtsug lag khang bzhengs 'tshar ba'i zhu byung ste/ 'byon du nye ba na/ jo bo chen po dgung lo re
gcig bzhes pa'i dus/ bla ma dang yi dam gyis lung bstan pa'i dge bshes ston pa rang lo so dgu bzhes pa/ dang por yang gling gser gyi lha khang du mjal nas byin gyis brlabs
pa'i tshul ston pa'i rnam thar gyi skabs su 'byung la/ de nas bshes gnyen ston pa dang/ lha btsun pas jo bo rgya gar du 'byon du ma ster/ dbus kyi rgyal khams su bsu
ba gnad la dgar ba'i spring yig tshigs su bcad pa bcu dgu pa gtang/ bod ston rnams ma sleb ring la/ thabs du mas jo bo'i thugs ngang bsrings te rgya dpe rten gsum la sogs
pa'i gzhi thams cad bal por ma skur/ de'i dus jo bo'i phyags phyir gung thang pa/ sa'i saM gha/ u pA sa si ka/ e la dha ri la sogs pa dpon slob nyi shus bal por byon nas/
mu stegs bcing ba'i mchod rten nag po bzhi mdzad/ u pA sa si kas bkra shis pa'i mchod rten dkar chen zhes pa che ba cig bzhengs/ gung thang pas jo bo yab sras zhal sprod
kyi ras bris che ba cig/ u pA sa si kas jo bo'i sku la lha btsun pa dang/ gung thang pa ldem du byas pa gyang ris la bkod de/ rab gnas la sogs pa zhag nyi shu rtsa gnyis
la tshar bar mdzad do/ de nas

jo bo rgya gar du 'byon par bzhed kyang/ u pA sa si ka dang/ bod kyi bsod nams kyi mthus/ slar yang mang yul du byon nas/ lha khang ke ru bya ba bzhengs/ de nas lha btsun pas
dbus su spyan drangs te/ las stod du phebs/ bod ston rnams kyang der byon/ gtsang gi sa rnams su sa skya dang/ snar thang la sogs pa'i lung bstan mang du mdzad de lo phyed
bzhugs/ de nas bsam yas/ thang po che/ lha sa rnams su/ lha btsun bo dhi rA dza/ khu ston/ rngog legs shes rnams kyis rim gyis spyan drangs nas/ chos mang du gsungs/
gsang phu la sogs pa lung bstan/ khyad par lha sar ka ba bum pa can gyi nye 'khor nas rgyal rabs ka khol ma mkha' gros lung bstan nas bton/ de nas rtog byang chub 'byung
gnas kyis yer par spyan drangs/ bka' gdams glegs bam gyi zhu lan phal che ba rngog gis der mdzad/ de nas bang ston gyis snye thang du spyan drangs/ lo ngo dgu bzhugs pa'i
drug la 'gyur mang po dang/ rgyud sgrub thabs/ man ngag sogs gang la gang 'dul gyi chos gsungs/ rin po che sna lnga'i me tog gi char bab/ lo gsum mam/ lo ngo bzhir mkha'
'gro'i dbus su rdo rje'i glu rnams gsungs/ de rnams su yang yi dam dpag tu med pa'i zhal gzigs pa sogs rgyas par lam yig tu gsal lo/ mdor na gangs ri'i khrod du bstan pa
snga dar la mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho/ slob dpon padma sam bha ba/ slob dpon ka ma la shI la rnams bka' drin ches shin du che la/ bstan pa phyi dar pa/ lta spyod log par
smra ba 'ba' zhig shing rta chen po'i gzhung rnams la nyams len gyi gnad med pa'i bshad chos su bsams shing/ nyams len snying po'i don ston pa'i man ngag zur du med par 'dod
pas/ bshad

pa dang sgrub pa'i chos/ don tha dad du 'dzin pa dang/ sdom pa gsum 'gal bar bsams nas tshul khrims kyi bslab pa khyad du gsod pa dang/ lam phyogs re pas thar pa thob par 'dod
pa rnams 'gog pa la/ dpal ldan a ti sha nyid kha ba can pa thams cad la bka' drin che ba yin te/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab thams cad kyi gnad bsdus pa/ shing rta chen po klu
sgrub dang/ thogs med gnyis kyi lam srol/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i sar 'gro ba'i skye bo mchog gi chos lugs/ skyes bu gsum gyis nyams su blang ba'i rim pa ma tshang
ba med par bsdus pa/ byang chub lam gyi sgron me'i sgo nas skal ba dang ldan pa rnams rim gyis sangs rgyas kyi sar 'khrid pa'i lam ma nor ba gsal bar mdzad pas bka' drin
che ba yin / de yang spyir rgyal ba'i lung gi bstan pa thams cad sde snod gsum du 'du bas/ rtogs pa'i bstan pa yang bslab pa gsum du 'du la/ tshul khrims kyi bslab pa
ni ting nge 'dzin gyi bslab pa sogs yon tan thams cad kyi rten du gsungs shing/ ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi bslab pa ni/ byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed nas pha rol
du phyin pa drug la gtso bor bslab pa thun mong ba'i lam dngos yin zhing/ rdo rje theg pa nyams su len pa rnams kyis kyang/ dbang bskur rnam dag thob nas dam tshig dang sdom
pa bsrung ba/ skyed rdzogs nyams su len pa rnams thabs kyi cha nas khyad che ba yang/ bslab pa gsum du ma 'dus pa med pas/ bstan pa thams cad 'gal med du gsal bar mdzad
do/ de lta bu'i lam gyi rnam gzhag dang mi ldan na/ lam gyi go rim/ grangs nges/ ngo bo rnams/ shing rta chen po rnams kyis gsungs pa dang mi mthun cing/ rgyal bas gsungs
pa'i lam du mi 'gyur bas/ 'bras bu rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang 'byung dka' bar gsungs so/ de lta bu'i bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho lta bu mnga' ba de'i rnam thar

sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yul du gyur pa/ bdag lta bu blo dman pa dag gi yul ma yin zhing/ ye ge nyung ngu dag gis rtogs par dka' la/ mthong tshad tsam
zhig bris na'ang mang bas/ rnam thar rgyas pa don du gnyer na gdul bya thun mong ba'i blo dang bstun pa lam yig tu gsungs pa dang/ de las blo mtho ba la braM ze be tA ri/
byang chub bzang po/ rig pa'i khu byug/ a ba dhU tI pa/ rA hu la gupta rnams bsten tshul la bla ma lnga pa dang/ de'i steng du thar par gshegs nas bla ma gser gling pa/
shAnti la sogs bdun bsten tshul dang/ bla ma bcu gnyis pa dang/ yi dam gyi lhas lung bstan pa dngos grub kyi 'od zer dang/ dam pa chos kyi 'byung gnas chung ba dang/ chos
kyi 'byung gnas che ba gsang skor du grags pa rnams ston pas mdzad pa dang/ de rnams dang phyogs mthun pa lo tsA bas bstod pa brgyad bcu pa dang/ thun mong ma yin pa rnams
bka' gdams glegs bam du skyes rabs nyi shu rtsa gnyis gsungs pa/ jo bo yab sras gnyis ka'i rnam thar shugs la rgyas par 'byung ba rnams su shes par bya'o/ de ltar skal
ba dang ldan pa rnams la mdo sngags kyi gzhung gdams ngag ma lus pa bstan nas/ bstan pa'i srol nub pa rnams gsar du gtsugs/ srol cung zad yod pa rnams 'phel bar mdzad/
log par rtog pa'i dri mas sbags pa rnams legs par bsal te/ bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas par mdzad nas/ dgung lo don gsum pa shing pho rta'i dbyug gu zla ba'i tshes
nyi shur lam yig las gsungs kyang/ ston pa'i gsung gi gral tshes bcu bco brgyad la byon par bzhed de/ dga'

ldan du rje btsun byams pa'i drung du lha'i bu nam mkha' dri ma med pa zhes bya bar gyur te/ bka' gdams glegs bam las/ bskal bzang 'di la rje btsun byams pa'i rjes su rgyal
ba seng ge 'byon par gsungs pa de/ jo bo rje yin par bzhed do/ lnga pa de'i rjes su slob pa'i bshes gnyen byon tshul la gnyis/ rgya gar du byon tshul dang/ bod du byon tshul
lo/ dang po ni/ rgya gar/ kha che/ o rgyan / gser gling/ mi yul/ bal po rnams su dngos slob paNDi ta dang/ grub thob dang/ nying slob bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byon
la/ bi kra ma la shI lar yang slob ma paNDi ta ratnA kIrti/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ su ma ti kirti/ bai ro tsa na rakShi ta/ bal po ka na ka shrI la sogs pa sum bcu tsam
yod kyang/ thun mong ma yin pa'i slob ma lnga ni/ paNDi ta chen po pi to pa/ dharma a ka ra ma ti/ dbu ma'i ser ge/ bshes gnyen gsang ba/ sa'i snying po rnams ni jo bo dang
rtogs pa byin brlabs mi mnyam yang/ mkhyen pa mnyam pa tsam du grags so/ gnyis pa bod du byon tshul ni/ gangs ri'i khrod 'dir rab tu byung ba dang/ skye bo phal che bas
chos thob cing bka' drin gyis khyab pa las/ de rnams kyi nang nas/ chos brgyud 'dzin pa la/ slob ma grags che ba byon tshul dang/ slob ma mchog byon tshul lo/ dang po
ni/ mnga' ris skor gsum nas/ lha byang chub 'od/ lha pho brang zhi ba 'od/ lo chen rin bzang/ rgya brtson 'grus seng ge/ nag tsho lo tsA ba/ lo chung legs she/ mang yul lo
tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab/ 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab 'od/ lo tsA ba dge blo/ lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros/ gi mi sgom chen/

'dul 'dzin gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gnas brtan gser bso rnams byon pa las/ lha btsun pas jo bo chen po'i chos mang du mkhyen/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi zhal gzigs/ mngon shes
lnga thob/ lo chen rin bzang rigs kha che'i g.yu ri g.yu sgra bya ba/ yab gzhon nu dbang phyug/ yum cog ro shes rab brtan ma/ lcam sring bzhi yod pa'i gcen shes rab dbang
phyug gis gcung rin chen dbang phyug tu sku skye ba bzhes/ dgung lo bcu gsum la mkhan po legs pa bzang po las rab tu byung ste/ mtshan rin chen bzang por gsol lo/ de'i
mod la 'dul ba rgya cher 'grel thugs su chud/ de nas rgyal po'i bkas kha cher byon/ lo tsA mkhas par bslabs/ paNDi ta kA ra rnam gsum sogs rgya gar gyi paN grub du ma
la gtugs/ theg pa mtha' dag gi chos la sbyangs/ bstan pa la bya ba rgya cher mdzad/ a ti sha dang pu rang du mjal te/ gu ge khri thang pas mdzad pa'i lo chen gyi rnam thar
las/ dgung lo brgyad bcu rtsa bdun la mjal bar gsungs/ ji ltar mjal ba'i tshul gong du bshad la/ gzhan yang yo ga/gsang 'dus/ bde mchog sogs kyi dbang dang/ rgyud kyi bshad
pa/ man ngag sogs theg pa gong 'og gi chos mtha' dag gis thugs tshim par mdzad/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin brlabs gnang bas rtogs pa khyad par can 'khrungs pas lhag
par dad de/ lha rten dang dpe ma gtogs pa gang yod phul/ jo bos dbus su lo tsA la 'gro dgos gsungs pas/ nga rgas pas mi nus zhus/ 'o na sgrub pa gyis gsungs pas mnyes te/
lo tsA ba chen po la paNDi ta'i bla ma drug bcu yod kyang/ jo bo nyid ma gtogs pa gzhan rnams kyis sgrub pa la

ma chud/ de nas lo tsA bas sgo gsum rim du byas pa la/ dam bca' ba'i yi ge gsum bris te sgrub pa mdzad pas/ gsang 'dus dang/ bde mchog gis zhal gzigs/ dgung lo dgu bcu rtsa
brgyad pa dgun zla tha chung gi tshes bcu bdun skar ma nya pa mod pa'i nyin mkha' spyod du gshegs par gu ge khri thang pas gsungs so/ rgya brtson seng ni/ gtsang stag tshal
du 'khrungs/ rten dge gnyen/ phyis rab tu byung ba mdzad/ rgya gar du jo bo la chos mang du gsan/ 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul par chos kyi 'byung gnas su bshad cing/ bal por
sku gshegs/ lo tsA ba nag tsho ni/ yul gung thang gdung nag tsho/ mtshan tshul khrims rgyal ba/ 'dul ba 'dzin par grags/ rgya brtson seng la mngon pa mkhas par bslabs/
dgung lo nyer bdun la rgya gar du jo bo chen po spyan 'dren du byon/ lo bcu dgu'i bar du tshul bzhin bsten/ thun mong gi yon tan rnams rdzogs par mdzad/ nag tshos snye thang
nas mnga' ris su 'byon khar/ jo bos bslab bya mang du mdzad de/ dam tshigs gsum bkod kyi sku phyag tu bzung nas byin brlabs mdzad/ 'dul ba mdo rtsa dang/ gsang ba 'dus
pa'i rgya dpe dang/ 'gro chos su thun mong ma yin pa'i spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub skor sogs sbas chos nyi shu gnang ste lung bstan mang du mdzad/ jo bo rang gi sku 'the
bong tsam seng ldeng la bris te ga 'ur bcug nas/ gung thang pa'i dpung pa la btags/ mnyes mnyes rgya chen mdzad/ jo bo la gung thang pas kyang lan gsol te/ phyi gzhag rnams
'brom la gzhag/ rnal 'byor pas kyang nag tsho la bslab bya ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul rnams snye thang du mdzad pa'i zhu lan dang/ rnal 'byor pa'i

gtod yig tu grags par gsal lo/ de nas mnga' ris su byon nas/ lung bstan pa bzhin sgrub pa mdzad pas/ 'jam dpal rdo rje/ sgrol ma yi ge drug pa rnams zhal gzigs/ mngon shes
kyang mnga' la/ de las slob brgyud phyag ser ba sogs byon tshul 'og tu 'chad do/ lo chung legs she ni/ 'khrungs yul mnga' ris pu rangs pa/ bal por thang bi ha ra bya ba rgyal
pos bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang du/ rngog rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis zhu sna byas te jo bo dang mjal/ rdo rje 'byung ba/ gtsug dgu khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dkyil mchog/
stod 'grel dang bzhi'i rgya dpe/ gsang 'dus kyi chos skor zhu ba'i rten du phul nas/ jo bo dang lo tsA bas bsgyur/ de nas yo ga rnam gsum gsungs te/ bod du jo bo'i
yo ga'i 'khor 'dus pa dang po lo chung legs she yin gsung/ lo tsA ba dge blo ni/ lo chen gyi slob ma rig pa can gyi khye'u lnga'i nang nas/ gnyis kha cher tshad pas grongs/
gsum pa ni rma lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros/ mang wer gyi lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo/ ljang lo tsA ba rin chen gzhon nu las dang po ste/ lo chen la mkhas par sbyangs/
jo bo chen po'i drung du chos mang du zhus/ yun ring du bsten cing lam sgron sogs 'gyur mang du mdzad do/ go mi sgom chen ni/ jo bo la lo chen gyis rnal 'byor rgyud kyi
skor gsan pa'i dus su sbyong rgyud dang/ gtsug dgu'i dbang dang/ rgyud kyi bshad pa sogs gsan te/ da lta yang go mi nas brgyud pa ma chad par bzhugs te/ kun rig sogs sgur
lugs su grags pa rnams so/ gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ dang por klu mes can du byon te/ mdo rtsa 'grel pa dang bcas pa sogs 'dul ba'i gzhung rnams

la mkhas par sbyangs/ de nas jo bo'i drung du theg pa che chung gi chos mang du gsan te/ ngas bslabs pa'i chos thams cad kyang lam du song gsung/ 'di la bu chen bzhi ste/ stod
du zhang zhung pa rgyal ba'i shes rab/ 'jims su gzhon tshul/ dbus su 'brom seng dkar/ stod pa ye shes bla ma/ de rnams kyi slob ma rgya 'dul 'dzin yin la/ 'dis dgung
lo brgyad bcu rtsa lnga bzhugs/ gra grwa pa 'dul ba'i bshad nyan pher ba stong lhag byung ste/ bod du 'dul ba'i bshad gra grwa rnams dang/ 'dul 'dzin gser ri'i phreng ba
lta bu byon pa rnams phal cher 'di las 'ched cing/ a ti sha nas brgyud pa'i chos skor la nyams len mdzad pas slob brgyud du gyur pa yin no/ glo bo'i yul nas ston pa yang
rab sogs dang/ gtsang stod nas brag ston che chung gnyis/ leng 'brog che chung gnyis byon/ gtsang smad nas 'gar 'gos yol gsum zhes grags che bas cung zad bshad na/ dang po
'gar dge ba gsal gyis jo bo la mdo sngags kyi chos mang du zhus/ khyad par du lu yi pa'i dbang bka'/ lha sbas kyi 'grel pa la brten pa'i bshad bka'/ chos tshan dgu la sogs
pa'i rdzogs rim yongs su rdzogs par gsan nas/ des lha rje stod pa stengs pa zla gsal sogs la brgyud pa da lta yang ma chad par 'dug go/ rje 'gos ni/ rus 'gos/ yab yum
rus gcig pas khug pa/ lhas phug tu 'khrungs pas lha btsas te/ gyi co zla ba'i 'od zer dang 'grogs te rgya gar du byon/ spyir paNDi ta bdun bcu/ mkha' 'gro'i bla ma gnyis
rnams la chos gsan/ de'i tshe paNDi ta mnyam po la'ang 'dus pa la kha zin che bar snang bas/ thog mar gsang 'dus la

slob gnyer mdzad de/ 'dus pa la mkhas pa'i paNDi ta bcu tsam bsten pa'i yul bhaM ga la'i mkhas pa chen po dI pam kA ra zhes pa/ rgya gar du 'dus pa gsan pa'i dpon slob yin
la/ jo bo'i gsang 'dus 'phags skor thams cad mnga' zhing/ bod du yang chos mang du gsan te/ rtsa ba'i slob ma yin/ spyir sngags thams cad/ khyad par du gsang ba 'dus pa la
mkhas par grags/ 'di la slob ma rgyud kyi ka ba gtsugs pa bzhi/ man ngag gi gdung theg pa brgyad/ las tshogs dang phrin las la mkhas pa lcam dang dral ma ltar dpag tu med
pa byon no/ yol dbang ni/ sku mched gsum ste/ yol drang song/ yol thog 'bebs dang gsum ka jo bo'i dngos slob yin yang/ 'dir dang po ste/ jo bo gtsang nyang tshe gnas su
phebs dus/ jo bo'i zhal nas da nang tho rangs nam mkha' la hrIHdkar po sgra dang bcas pa zhig byung/ bcu gcig zhal gyi sku li ma 'di la phog/ de las 'od 'phros bod thams
cad 'od kyis khyab nas/ 'od de ban chung gzhon nu gcig la phog pas/ de'i sgyu lus 'od gsal du shar ba rmis gsung/ nyi ma rtse shar yol chos dbang btsun chung lo bcu drug
lon pa cig gis dar dang gser phul/ bdag la thugs rje chen po'i gdams ngag cig zhu zer bas/ jo bo dgyes nas bcu gcig zhal gyi sku de yang gnang/ spyan ras gzigs dang/ rta
mgrin sogs kyi chos skor rnams snga phyir rdzogs par gnang/ thugs rje chen po zhi khro mang du zhal gzigs te dngos grub brnyes so/ gzhan yang stod lung pa gnam gyi rdzing
kha ba mal shes rab sems dpas/ jo bo la yun ring du bsten te bsgoms nas smin mtshams nas 'od zer byung/ de'i rjes su

sems bcug nas bsgoms pas/ zhing khams mang po mthong ba byung ste/ jo bo la lam du 'gyur ram zhus pas/ zhi gnas kyi cha mthun yin/ bla ma mtshan nyid dang ldan pas zin na lam
du 'gyur gsung/ yang lan gcig snye thang na jo bo'i gzims chung du khong rtogs pa 'bul ba la/ khu ston gyis lkog nyan byas pas/ sa thob pa tsam du mngon te/ khong phyir
byung ba'i rjes/ khu ston gyis jo bo la/ de su lags/ rtogs pa ji tsam du 'dug zhus pas/ mal shes rab sems dpa' bya ba theg pa chen po'i sbyor lam drod la nye bar 'dug gsung/
de gar song zhus pas/ kho rkang mgyogs kyi dngos grub thob pas klung shod ngar gyi la la sleb song/ ra sgreng la 'gro bar 'dug gsung/ 'dis stod lungs tsha thog gi dgon
pa btab ste/ spyan snga'i rab byung mdzad pa'i mkhan po yin no/ dbus nas khu rngog 'brom gsum grags che bas 'og tu 'chad do/ gzhan yang rtog byang chub 'byung gnas/ glan
ye shes shes rab/ zhang sna nam rdo rje dbyug gsum la/ theg chen gdung rgyud brtan mdzad gsum du grags/ ka bha ya shAkya dbang phyug/ rag shi ston pa tshul khrims 'byung
gnas/ rma ston pa shAkya byang chub/ dar ston pa byang chub gsal/ rba ston pa g.yung drung rin chen/ gar li ston pa yon tan g.yung drung / rgyus ston pa chos kyi rgyal
po/ bang ston byang chub rgyal mtshan/ 'dang ljang ston pa/ zhang sna chung ston pa/ lhab mi ston pa shes rab 'od zer te dbus kyi ston chen bcu gcig go zhang btsun yer
pa ba ye shes 'bar/ sa phug pa zhu sgom/ mkha' ru ba chen por grags pa snga ma ste/ sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pa gsum mo/ gzhan yang rngog sgom yon tan rgyal po/ sgom pa
dad pa bla ma

rnal 'byor pa g.yung drung rgyal mtshan/ sum pa mthu chen/ sgro Arya byang chub/ khu seng ge rgyal mtshan rnams byon/ zhang btsun yer pa ba ye shes 'bar ni/ rje btsun byams
pa la chos gsan par gsungs shing/ spo to ba'i gnas kyii slob dpon yin la/ phyis kyi zhang yer pa ba bstan kya'o/ bla ma zhang gi bla ma dang mi gcig la/ de rnams jo bo chen
po'i thun mong ma yin pa'i slob ma yin no/ gzhan yang mar pa lo tsA la dbang rin chen phreng ba gnang/ khyung po rnal 'byor la sems skyed/ byams chos/ bde mchog/ gsang
'dus/ gshed skor dang bcas pa gnang/ mar pa do pa dang/ pu rangs lo chung la bde mchog gi skor rnams gnang/ ba ri lo tsA ba la sgra'i skor rnams gnang ste/ mdor na gangs
ri'i khrod 'dir kun la bka' drin gyis khyab par mdzad do/ khams nas rnal 'byor pa chen po/ dpal ldan dgon pa ba/ rnal 'byor pa shes rab rdo rje/ phyag dar ston pa dang
bzhi la khams la sku mched bzhi zhes grags pa cung zad bshad na/ rnal 'byor pa chen po 'khrungs yul mdo smad tsong kha/ yos bu lo pa/ gdung rus lung/ mtshan byang chub rin
chen/ lo sum bcu rtsa gnyis la dbus su byon/ jo bo dang thog mar mang yul bzoo gnas su mjal/ lo dgu bsten no/ dpal ldan dgon pa ba mdo khams stod kyi 'dan ma/ sga pa'i
sgrol ma lha khang pa/ gdung rus 'jeng/ 'brug lo pa/ mtshan dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ mdo khams nas dang po skam po ri pa bya ba'i grub thob cig la gtad nas byon/ mnga' ris
na paNDi ta byon 'dug bya ba gsan pas/ jo bo dang nyan tsho gnas rnying du mjal/ rnal 'byor pa dang gnyis la/ jo bos thun mong gi chos bzhis snod rung du mdzad nas/ lha
'di dang las 'brel 'dug gsung ste/ dam tshig gsum bkod kyi sgrub thabs gnang nas bsgrubs pas/ bzlas pa

stong phrag brgyad brgyad song nas zhal gzigs/ jo bo lo dgu bsten/ rnal 'byor pa shes rab rdo rjes/ jo bo lo lnga bsten cing/ rngog legs she dang lhan du bzhugs te gsang phur
sku gshegs so/ phyag dar ston pas kyang jo bo lo lnga bsten te/ snye thang du bod ston rnams kyis phar phyin gsung bar zhus pas/ thog mar paNDi ta'i lugs dang/ de nas
jo bo nyid kyi bzhed pa ston pa bzhi'i sgo nas 'khrid tshul gsungs pa/ phyag dar ston pas zin bris su btab pas shin du legs pa cig byung/ phar phyin khams lugs mar grags
te/ khong phar phyin la rtsal thon par gsungs/ gnyis pa chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i slob ma mchog byon tshul la gsum/ bshes gnyen ston pa byon tshul/ dge bshes gsang phu ba byon
tshul/ nag tsho'i rjes slob byon tshul lo/ dang po ni/ de rnams kyi nang nas jo bo chen po'i chos kyi brgyud pa 'dzin pa'i mchog 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas yin
te/ 'khrungs yul byang rtsa sgye mo phyogs su mdzad/ gdung rus 'brom gyi nang tshan brag gsum/ yab stag gsum sku gzher/ yum khu lde bza' gnyis kyi sras su shing pho 'brug
la 'khrungs/ gzhur zhang po'i sar g.yung chos mgon la klog bslabs/ slob gnyer mdzad kyi yod pa'i dus/ rgyal gyi zhang chen po la dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa blangs/ de nas
dgung lo bcu bdun bzhes pa la/ se btsun dbang phyug gzhon nu khams nas yar byon/ rgya gar du 'byon par bzhed de/ bal yul bar byon/ lo gcig na slar log pa dang mjal/ 'khrid
par zhus pas sang red shog gsung bas/ tshong pa dang 'grogs te byon/ khams 'dan ma'i yul du lo hril po

bcu dgu se btsun la bsten/ mdo sngags kyi chos mang du gsan/ mkhas par gyur te dge bsnyen chos 'phel du grags/ snying rje pad dkar du/ byang phyogs su bstan pa la dad pa lhar
skye zhing/ rab byung chos bzhin mi spyod pa log par lhung/ der dge bsnyen chos 'phel zhes pa rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa 'byung zhes pa dang/ sangs rgyas phal po cher/ byang
phyogs su dge bsnyen chos 'phel bya ba 'byung zhes 'brom ston pa lung bstan/ 'brom gyi dgongs pa la/ dal 'byor mi lus thob par dka' ba rnyed pa'i dus 'dir/ chos rnal
ma cig byed na 'di tsam gyis chog gam mi chog/rgya gar mkhas pa cig la 'dri ba la/ bar du lo tsA ba mi dgos pa byed dgongs te/ paNDi ta rgya'i tsher ma bya ba la bi brta
la sogs pa bslabs/ kha gcig smr-i ti dznyA na dang gcig par 'dod/ de la lo tsA mkhas par bslabs/ der se btsun gyi zhal nas/ pha dang 'phrad par song gsung ste/ dgung lo
so brgyad 'gro ba la yar byon/ byang 'phrang kha sog chu khar phebs/ 'phrang kha ber chung gis ra sgreng gi dgon pa phul/ mnga' ris lha bla ma bas paNDi ta spyan drangs te
phebs pa sngar nas gsan kyang/ de'i tshe ring po mi thogs par rgya gar du 'byon par 'dug zer bas/ mtshan thos pa tsam gyis lhag par dad pa skyes te yar byon/ jo bo dpon
slob pu rangs na bzhugs pa la/ sgrol ma'i zhal nas/ da ni zhag gsum dro dang bzhi na bod kyi u pA sa ka 'byon pas byin gyis rlobs shig gsung/ jo bos kyang de'i sta gon mdzad/
u pA nye ba/ a sa ka gnas pa ste

mtshams sbyar bas/ u pA sa ka nye bar gnas pa'am/ dge bsnyen la 'jug la/ pa'i ring po chad pa dang/ si ka ces pa ma dag ste/ u pa si ka dge bsnyen ma la 'jug go/ de nas rta'i
lo rang lo so dgur pa la jo bo dang mjal/ byin gyis brlabs/ dbang bskur/ 'jam dpal rdo rje'i sku yang gnang/ khyod bla ma rnams dang sgrol mas lung bstan pa'i slob ma
yin pas nga'i rtsar sdod/ nga'i bka' brgyud 'di la gsol ba thob dang byin brlabs yod kyi/ byin brlabs 'byung gi gsung/ de'i tshe jo bo nyid kyang rgya gar du ldog par bzhed/
lo tsA ba yang sngar gyi chad yod pas phar gdan 'dren bzhed pa la/ ston pas kyang bzhugs par zhu ma nus/ 'on kyang thabs mkhas pas/ dbus na rgyal blon gyi gtsug lag khang
yod tshul dang/ dge 'dun gyi sde mang du bzhugs pa rnams jo bo phebs par mos tshul dang/ bod ston rnams la yang chad pa yod pa bzhin phrin yig btang ba sogs gong du
bshad pa ltar/ dka' ba du mas bod du spyan drangs te/ ston pas lo bcu gsum tshul bzhin du bsten cing/ bshes gnyen ston pa la bla ma lnga yod pa ni/ dang por klog bslabs pa'i
slob dpon gzhu'i kun dga' ra ba'i g.yung chos mgon rgyal gyi zhang chen po/ se btsun dbang phyug gzhon nu/ paNDi ta sgra'i tsher ma/ jo bo ni 'gran gyi do med yin la/
spyir jo bo'i chos thams cad thugs la mnga' ste/ mi 'chug bsdams pa las kyang jo bo'i zhal nas/ gzhung bzang khyod ni tshangs spyod sdom pas phyug/ smon 'jug sems bskyed
lag len snying rjes mdzad/ dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs gsang ba phyir mi ldog/

sdom gsum khyod kyi rgyud la rdzogs par gnas/ de dag kun gyi lam rim lag len rnams/ rim pa bzhin du khrid du bskyangs pa las/ kun la thogs med khyod kyi blo la rdzogs/ gzhan
yang bslab btus spyod 'jug la sogs pa/ don yod go ste sems la phan pa'i chos/ brgya dang bcu gsum dag par khyod kyis bslabs/ gsang ba gzhan la bstan par dka' ba yang/ sbas
pa'i chos rnams khyod kyis lon par mdzad/ khyod ni zhu mkhas kho bo snod la rtog/ lha rnams kun la bag chags gzhag pa'i phyir/ sgrub thabs stong phrag nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i
khrid/ kho bo phyogs 'dir bos pa'i dgos pa dang/ sdom gsum don du gnyer bar 'dod pa la/ so sor lag len rim par bkrol ba lags/ shes zhes sogs mang du gsungs so/ khyad
par du rgyal bas lung bstan pa shing rta chen po gnyis kyi gdams pa'i bcud/ rgyal ba'i bka' bstan pa thams cad 'gal med du nyams su len pa'i lam ma nor ba'i gdams ngag a
ti sha la mnga' ba de/ gtso bor ston pas thob par mdzad cing/ bshes gnyen ston pa'i rjes 'jug sku mched gsum la sogs pa rnams la yang/ bka' gdams pa zhes mtshan du grags
la/ ston pas mdzad pa'i lha chos bdun ldan chung ba las/ ngo mtshar bka' ni sde snod gsum po ste/ gdams pa skyes bu gsum gyis phyug pa yin/ bka' gdams rin chen gser gyi
phreng ba la/ 'gro ba gang gis bgrangs kyang don yod 'gyur/ zhes pa nas/ bdag gi bla ma 'gran gyi do med 'di/ tshul khrims gos can lta ba'i rnal 'byor pa/ ye shes lus can
mtshan dang dpe byad ldan/ log pa'i chos las nges par 'das pa yin/ e ma ya mtshan bsam gyis mi khyab

pa'i/ bde bar gshegs pa rgyal ba gnyis pa 'di'i/ brgyud par bcas pa'i rjes su 'brang du byung/ de yis kho bo bod du lus blangs kyang/ bsod nams mi chung shin du skal ba bzang/
zhes pa'i bar du gsungs so/ de ltar mjal ba'i dus dang / bsten pa'i lo grangs 'di las gzhan du 'dod pa ma dag par mngon no/ jo bo dga' ldan du gshegs nas ka ba shAkya
dbang phyug sogs bod ston rnams kyis/ jo bo'i 'das mchod snye thang du gtang/ ston pas jo bo'i gdung dang rten gsum sogs spyan drangs te/ shing mo lug gi lo la ra sgreng
du byon/ dgon pa'i sa dpyad gzigs pas shin du legs par dgongs te/ brag seng ge'i zhol du rnal lam brtags pas/ dbu rtse'i sa na gser gyi mchod rten 'dug pa'i 'od zer las/
dbu rtse gandhi ra ser lhag ge ba mang po byung nas/ bod yul thams cad 'od kyis gang bar byas te/ tshur 'dus shug pa'i gseb thams cad gang ba dang/ gzhan yang rtse 'phying
dkar ba mar gyi phung po dang/ pha bong thang rin po che'i phung por song ba la sogs pa'i ltas khyad par can mang po rmis te/ nang par sum pa mthu chen dang/ rnal 'byor
pa/ dgon pa ba gsum gyis ltas bzang zhus pas/ bzang gsung nas/ dgon pa 'debs par thag bcad/ sa 'dul la brgyad stong pa 'grel pa dang bcas pa gsungs/ me pho spre'u lo la
dgon pa gong dang/ gzims khang rnams btab/ me mo bya'i lo sa ga zla ba'i tshes gnyis la sa chog mdzad/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa lha bcu dgu'i thig btab ste/ ka gnyis ma'i rmang
bting/ gur dkar phib/ jo bo'i gdung dang/ dngul gdugs can/ 'jam dpal rdo rje la sogs pa bzhugs/ zo bo bi ri rnal 'byor bya bas

ka gnyis ma rgya phibs/ khyams stod ka ba bcu gnyis rnams bya lo rang la grub par mdzad/ de nas na ning chu mo yos yan la 'das lo bzhi brgya dang nyi shu rtsa bdun song/ rten
gsar du bzhengs pa rnams kyi rab gnas sogs/ rnal 'byor pa gong 'og gis grogs mdzad de phun sum tshogs par grub nas/ jo bo'i gdung bzhugs pa'i khyung mgo can grub/ 'di
man chad la byed pa po cig 'ong gi gsung nas/ 'dzin rdo yon tan 'bar pa khyod 'jig rten gyi shes che ba yin gyis/ kho bos tshe 'di'i rnam rtog spong blo cig bgyi gsung ste/
'jig rten mkhyen pa rnyed dang ma rnyed dang/ zhes sogs gsungs shing/ 'jig rten chos brgyad mgo snyoms mdzad do/ de dus rnal 'byor pa phyag khri mchog jo bo lo lnga bsten
pa de ra sgreng na bzhugs pa/ kho bo mtshams shig byed pa yin gsung nas/ 'jig rten gyi rnam par rtog pa la mtshams po che mdzad de/ shug gseb na gang dgar bzhugs nas
rtse gcig tu sgrub pa mdzad/ dgung lo zhe gnyis 'gro ba'i dus/ dge bshes ston pas 'khor gcig la bdud rtsi ka pA la gang bskur te/ phyag khri mchog la gtad pa gsol nas mkha'
spyod du gshegs so/ de ltar bshes gnyen ston pa thugs zab la bkyel che ba/ mkhyen pa rgya mtsho lta bu mnga' ba des/ mdo rgyud du ma nas lung bstan pa'i ra sgreng de bod
kyi sde pa gang gi yang phyogs su ma chad pa/ bi kra ma la shi la'i gnas chung/ jo bo'i gdan sa/ rnal 'byor pa gong 'og rnams kyi sgrub gnas/ bod kyi spyi mchod cig byung
gsung/ de yang sngon gyi yi ge las/ chos kyi rgyal po srong brtsan bgam btsan sgam po byang du mi rgod 'dul ba la byonadus/ ra sgreng du phebs te dbu skra gtor nas/ 'di
spos shing rgyas par gyur pa'i tshe

gnas 'dir nga'i sprul pa 'byung zhes gsung ba/ bshes gnyen ston pa yin par bzhed do/ 'dir smras pa/ spyan ras gzigs dbang sngon tshe chos rgyal tshul/ ding sang rgyal ba'i
'byung gnas skur bstan cing/ 'jig rten dbang phyug srid mtha'i bar du ni/ 'gro ba'i don mdzad su yis dpag par nus/ der sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa a ti sha'i chos srol dri ma
med pa rnams gtsugs te/ spyir las dang skal ldan gyi slob ma brgyad bcu tsam smin par mdzad cing/ khyad par du sku mched rin po che gsum jo bo nyid kyis snye thang du lung
bstan te/ 'brom rje thub pa'i bstan pa lnga stong gnas/ 'on kyang bod du chos spyod ji ltar dar/ bdag gis bstan pa dkrongs bskyed byas pa yin/ da ni legs par gzhi bzhengs
tshar ba yin/ chos 'di legs par bskyongs skyongs shig rgyal ba 'brom/ mtha' rgya byang nas bkyed cig snying stobs can/ lo rgyus rnam thar zung zhig khrel gzhung can/
pha gcig bu gcig yin no snying la soms/ shes zhes dang/ bdag gi bstan pa 'di ni khyod la gtad/ lo skor gcig gi bar du byang phyogs su/ tshon gyi char pa phob la gzhan don
mdzod/ de nas khyod kyi yon tan ma lus pa/ gang zag gcig gis blang bar mi nus kyi/ las can brgyad bcur bgos la mtha' rgya bkyed/ gtso bor sprul pa'i sku mched gsum po la/
gzhung dang man ngag thun mong gsum byin la/ lhag chad med par rang gi gdan sa gtod/ gnas kyi gdan sar a mes chen po bskos/ de nas zhen cing chags pa ma byed par/ dga'
ldan gnas su bdag gi drung du shog/ ces bshes gnyen ston pa bstan pa'i bdag por byin gyis brlabs shing/ chos kyi gdan sa sku mched gsum dang/ gnas kyi gdan sa rnal 'byor
pa dang/

bcas pa lung bstan cing/ las can brgyad bcu'i nang nas grags che ba gong du bshad pa'i khams pa sku mched bzhi dang/ gzhan yang khams nas rnal 'byor pa byams pa'i blo gros/
yongs rdzogs rnal 'byor pa/ lho brag nas rnal 'byor pa phyag khri mchog/ btsun pa dge skyong/ bi ri rnal 'byor pa/ stong btsan na mgo kyu ra gzhon nu 'od zer/ lhab mi shes
rab g.yung drung/ sgom pa rin chen bla ma/ gtsang pa jo pad/ ka ba rgya dkar/ mar pa jo legs/ bran ka jo btsun/ sum sgom dbang phyug 'od zer/ rnal 'byor pa g.yung drung
rgyal mtshan te 'di rnams jo bo dang ston pa thun mong ba'i slob ma yi dam gyi lha zhal gzigs pa/ skyes bu chen po'i lam la zhugs pa sha stag go sras kyi thu bo sku mched
gsum yin la/ kha cig kham pa lung pa dang sku mched bzhir yang 'dod de/ 'dis yung ba'i kham lung du/ dgon pa btab 'gro don mdzad cing lo dgu bcu rtsa gcig bzhugs/ gzhan
yang zhang ye shes rgyal mtshan/ brag rgyab pa gnyan ston shaka 'byung/ mnga' ris 'dul 'dzin/ rgyug pa'i zhang chen po/ rnam thar gtsang ma'i ka kyog pa chen po/ 'dzin
sgom yon tan 'bar/ sgro byang chub tshul khrims/ a mi thar pa rgyal mtshan/ a mes sman rgan la sogs pa de rnams bshes gnyen ston pa'i slob ma thun mong ma yin pa grags che
ba rnams yin no/ de ltar slob ma rnams smin par mdzad de lo dgur bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mdzad nas/ drug bcu rtsa gcig sa 'brug lo tshul zhugs zla ba'i tshes nyi shu la ra
sgreng nas/ rje btsun byams pa'i drung na/ jo bo lha'i bu nam mkha' dri ma med pa zhes pa'i drung du gshegs/ bka' gdams glegs bam las/ ston pa lha'i bu rgyal ba rgya mtsho/
ka ba shAkya dbang phyug/ lha'i bu shAkya dri med/ rngog legs she/ lha'i bu shes rab sgron ma/ lo tsA ba nag tsho

lha'i bu tshul khrims ldan zhes 'gyur bar gsungs so/ de'i srol 'dzin byon tshul la gsum/ ra sgreng du byon tshul/ sku mched gsum byon tshul/ de las 'phros pa byon tshul lo/
dang po ni/ rnal 'byor pa chen po ston pa yang lo dgu bsten/ ra sgreng gi gdan sa lo bcu gnyis mdzad pa'i ring dgon pa gong nas phyir byon/ da lta dbu rtse ka ba bcu drug
ma'i sa der gzims chung mdzad/ de dus zhang 'phrang kha ber chung gi sras/ dgra bcom/ de'i sras dar ma ye shes kyis/ ka gnyis ma'i khyams smad/ khyams chung nag tshang
gsum mdzad de/ rab gnas rnal 'byor pa chen pos mdzad/ sa tra mang du gtsugs/ gdul bya du ma smin par mdzad de/ dge 'dun sum brgya tsam 'dus/ drug bcu rtsa gnyis pa 'brug
lo rgyal zla ba'i tshes brgyad la ra sgreng nas thegs/ dpe la lar/ rta lo sa yos la thegs pas bdun bcu tham pa bzhugs zer ba yang snang ngo/ de nas dpal ldan dgon pa ba gdan
sar bskos/ ston pa lo dgu bsten/ rnal 'byor pa dang 'dra/ ra sgreng gi gdan sa lo bcu mdzad/ dgon pa gong ma rang du bzhugs nas sne'u zur pa la sogs pa'i slob ma mang
du smin par mdzad de/ drug bcu rtsa bdun pa khyi lo'i mngon bar byang chub pa'i nya la ra sgreng nas thegs/ dgon pa ba la slob ma mang du byon pa'i mchog bu chen/ rgyu ni
rlung shod rgyug pa'i zhang ka ma ba shes rab 'od/ kha rag sgom chung/ rog phyor phu ba smra ba'i seng ge/ mtha' bzhi sgom pa/ 'phan yul rgyal du gnyan sna mo ba dang/
'bre ko te lung pa tshul khrims rgyal/ dar yul du chu sgom gzhon nu snying po dang/ 'tshur sgom ye shes rgyal mtshan gnyis/ 'phan yul snya ra dben mor 'gar 'dul 'dzin/ spras
thong pa sar sne'u zur pa rnams so/ de rnams kyi nang nas

chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i mchog sne'u zur pa yin te cung zad 'og tu 'chad do/ de rnams rnal 'byor pa dang thun mong ba'i slob ma yin kyang dgon pa ba'i bu chen du drangs song
kha rag sgom chung ni gtsang du sku 'khrungs/ lam po gnas su mkhan po mar sgom la rab tu byung ste/ mtshan dbang phyug blo gros su btags/ dang por sbas sgom bsod nams rgyal
mtshan ye shes yang zer bya ba jo bo'i slob ma gcig la chos gsan/ de nas ra sgreng du byon loo drug bzhugs nas rnal 'byor pa dang/ dgon pa ba gnyis la chos mang du gsan/
gtsang bu'i thugs dgongs la da ni rang gis kyang chig kya thub zer 'ong snyam ste/ nyung ma'i sa bon phul gang khyer nas sprags kyi sme'u ke rur byon/ dbyar lo thug gsol/
dgun nyung thug la phyed thun re btab nas gsol kyin lo bcu gcig tu sgrub pa rtse gcig mdzad/ de nas kha rag tu byon nas sgrub pa mdzad pas kha rag sgom chung du grags/
kha gcig mtho chos dang ang yig bdun bcu rnams sprags su mdzad zeer te/ rnam thar na kha rag shar du mdzad gsung ngo/ 'dis rnal 'byor pa gong 'og gi gsung la brten te/
lam rim don tshan bcu gnyis su bsdus pa mdzad de/ kha rag skor gsum du grags pa'i gcig gi rtsa ba yin no/ bdun bcu rtsa lnga pa la gtsang gi phug nag po bya bar sku gshegs
khar/ lo pa la/ skyes pa'i yul spongs/ nye du dang thag bsrings/ bshes gnyen rtag tu bsten/ khrul hrul po'i gos gyon/ dman pa'i sa bzung/ ngan pa'i zas zo/ rgya skad chu
bzhin du 'thung la sgrub pa gyis gsung ba'i gdams ngag gnang ste/ rus pa lhag rol bsdus la/ byang ra sgreng na dpal ldan dgon pa ba'i sku 'bum yod pas/ de'i grib ma dang
ser bu 'phog sar bskyol zhig gsung ste/ de ltar byas so/

de nas ra sgreng du dpal ldan dgon pa ba'i rjes su spo to bas gdan sa lo gsum mam gcig mdzad kyang zer te zhang chos rgyal la sogs pa khams pa ma rungs pa 'ga' zhig gis bzhugs
dbang ma byung ba dang/ spo to ba rang gi rnal lam du yang zhing pa ma dul ba sogs byung bas/ der ma bzhugs par sku mched gsum pos dka' thub kyi ri sul rnams su drang
srong gi spyod tshul gyis/ gnas nges med du thugs dam dang gzhan phan gang 'phel mdzad pas/ ra sgreng du gdan sa la bar stongs lo sum bcu tsam dang/ chos tshugs la yang
dar rgud cher byung/ de nas sku mched gsum gshegs nas lo gcig gnyis na mtha' bzhi sgom pa bya ba ston pa la yang thug cing/ sku mched gsum gyi slob ma yin pa yi dam gyi lha
mang po zhal gzigs shing/ gzhan don phrin las la dbang 'byor ba des/ bla ma'i gdan sa nyams pa'i gtam gsan pas/ ra sgreng du byon gnas tshul rnams gzigs te/ shar ba pa
bzho'i khang pa gnas na bzhugs pa dang/ bya yul ba chen po/ glang ri thang pa/ ka ma ba/ lor sdings po ba rnams kyi drung du byon nas/ khyed rnams bla ma'i gdan sa la phyi
mig blta na dus la bab nas 'dug gsung ste bskul bas/ de rnams kyis grogs mdzad/ 'bul ba chen po byung ste pa tra yang mang du gtsugs/ bud med dang ra lug rnams phud/ chos
khrims shin du dam pa dang/ dge 'dun mang po yang bzhugs par mdzad de/ chos srol cher gtsugs/ tshogs dpon bshes gnyen mtha' bzhis lo shas su mdzad do/ khyad par shar
ba pas ka gnyis ma'i nub tu dbu rtse ka dgu ma gcig dang por bzhengs pa/ phyis dpon gyad pa dang/ zi gu chos grags gnyis kyis mgo byas bzang 'dus bcu drug bya bas bdag rkyen
byas nas/ ka chen

bcu drug yod pa/ sgo lhor bstan/ nyis thog gser 'bru gser bya gnyis dang bcas pa bzhengs/ de'i khyams smad sgang phyug po bya bas byas so/ spo to ba bzhud nas lo mang po'i
bar du mtha' bzhi la sogs pa bgres pa res gral dbu tsam ma gtogs/ gdan sar ming btags pa dang/ 'chad nyan sogs cher med la/ skabs shig tu rngog blo ldan shes rab la phul
bas/ gsang phu dang sbrel te lo kha yar du chos bar zla ba gcig gnyis tsam du bzhugs pa yang mdzad do/ de nas ka gnyis ma bzhengs nas lo dgu bcu rtsa gsum lon pa sa pho 'brug
gi lo la ka pa nyi shu rtsa bzhi ma bzhengs pa'i sbyin bdag 'phreng kha ber chung gi sras/ chos grags/ dgra bcom/ lhun po gsum/ lhun po'i bu spyan ras skyabs/ shAkya
skyabs/ ye shes skyabs/ padma skyabs dang bzhi 'ong / padma skyabs kyi bu jo yis/ jo rgyal gnyis/ jo yis kyi bu zhang ye/ se'o gzhon tshul/ thang po/ khams pa grags dang
bzhi'i nang nas/ se'o gzhon tshul des spyir ra sgreng gi skor du zhabs tog cher mdzad/ khyad par dbu rtse ka ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ ka gnyis ma'i shar phyogs su bzhengs par
'dood pa la/ rin chen sgang du sangs rgyas dben ston la sa dpyad zhus pas/ shar nub nas rdo gnyis khyer shog gsung ste/ de la gzigs pas/ shar phyogs klu'i rgyal po'i pho
brang la gnod par 'dug pas/ nub phyogs su gyis gsungs pas/ zhang 'od 'jo bas ra sgreng du lo bcu gnyis bzhugs pa'i bcu pa'i thog tu sa chog mdzad/ rmang bting/ de nas
lo gnyis pa lcags pho rta'i lo bdun bcu rtsa gsum pa bya zla'i tshes bcu bco lnga la thegs/ 'di 'phan yul 'jog po 'chad khar byon pa bshes gnyen nam mkha' 'bum gyi bla ma
de yin no/ de nas gzhon tshul gyis ka ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi nyis thog sgo lhor bstan/ spen bad gser 'brus mdzes pa byas/ de'i

khyams smad tsong kha shAka 'byung gis bzhengs/ de rnams kyi rab tu gnas pa sangs rgyas dbon ston gyis mdzad do/ zhang 'od 'jo bo gshegs kar/ dgon pa dang gdan sa 'od 'jo la
gtad kyang/ ra sgreng pa bshags rnams kyis ma phul bas/ sgang thang dkar bas/ thang dkar dang / ra sgreng sbrel nas lo nyi shu rtsa dgu gdan sa mdzad de/ chu pho bya la
thegs/ de rjes sngar gyi 'brel pos zhang 'od 'jo ba'i slob ma dgon 'od 'jo ba yang zer/ zhogs pa chen por grags pa des gdan sa lo bcu drug mdzad/ de nas sgang thang dkar
ba'i rjes la gnyis su gyes pas/ dgon gong 'og gnyis su grags par 'dug la/ phyis brgyud pas 'dzin pa 'di gnyis gong du smos pa rnams dang/ gdung rus gcig par mi 'dug cing/
dgon 'og ma ba'i brgyud pas bzung nas mkhan chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan sogs rim pa gsum tsam song la/ dgon gong ma ba'i brgyud pa ni ma thos so/ phyis ka gnyis ma la 'byung
ba'i gnod pa byung nas/ bya btang rin chen bzang po dang/ bdag gi bla ma 'jam dbyangs rin chen grags pa gnyis kyis legs par bsabs pa'i tshul thos mod 'dir ma spros
so/ gnyis pa sku mched rin po che gsum byon tshul ni/ de ltar bshes gnyen ston pas ra sgreng du bka' gdams kyi chos srol rnam par dag pa gtsugs te bzhugs pa'i dus su/ 'phags
pa sku mched gsum gyis byon/ tshul bzhin du bsten te yon tan rnams rdzogs par mdzad do/ de yang bshes gnyen phu chung pa ni/ rgyal gyi kyi ra'i phu chung du lcags mo
lug la 'khrungs/ rus zur tshangs/ yab yum 'byor pa chung yang gser zho do bsnams nas/ rgyal lha khang du zhang chen po la rab tu byung ste/ mtshan gzhon nu rgyal mtshan du
