btags/ khu ston la phar phyin 'grel pa don gsal tshar bcu bco lnga dang/ 'dul mngon la sogs pa

mang du gsan te thos pa cher mdzad/ snye thang du jo bo la chos kyi 'brel pa zhus pas/ btig pa dang 'khrungs su byung ste/ gang la lo bcu gcig yin zer yang zhen chags med pa'i
blo skyes gsung/ de nas ra sgreng du byon pas/ sku mched gzhan gnyis kyang byon te/ rten 'brel dang/ pha rol du phyin pa'i gdams ngag/bslab phyogs/ spyod phyogs kyi skor
rnams zhus/ lo bdun bsten/ khong rang la chos zhu mang du byung yang/ sha zug bzang po rang za ba'i dus yin/ gzhan la ster ba'i dus min gsung nas sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad
pas/ bdag las gzhan gces pa'i byang chub kyi sems dang/ chos thams cad bdag med par rtogs pa'i shes rab khyad par can 'khrungs/ yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs/ nyams len
byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa'i bka' gtso bor babs/ de nas sku mched gsum 'bral med du sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad cing bzhugs/ phyis yung ba'i phu chung du bzhugs nas kyang sgrub
pa gtso bor mdzad de/ brag gi dkyil na gser bre yod pa mngon bar mkhyen nas phyag mkhar gyis reg pas rang bye ste/ bton pa'i rjes dang/ gzims khang gi nub na brag la phyag
'dzub gtsugs par sgrub chu dang/ zhabs rjes dang/ dbu zhwa'i rjes yin zer ba yang 'dug go 'di la slob ma grags che ba/ sha bo sgang pa dang/ 'ban tshul khrims rgyal ba
sku lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du gshegs par grags pa dang/ zhogs su 'khrungs pa sdings pa shes Rab rgya mtsho dang/ zhogs phu'i karma brag pas rgyun du bzang spyod
la zhal 'don mdzad pa la/ chu len dus bde ba can gyi zhing der rab tu 'gro zhes pa'i skabs su mkha' spyod du gshegs pa sogs sgrub pa snying por mdzad pa nyi shu tsam byon
no/ spyir sku mched gsum gra grwa pa la ris su chad pa med pas/ chos kyis

'brel ba la khyad par med do/ de nas spo to ba gshegs pa'i gdung cha lngar bgos te/ cha gcig dang/ thugs bzhugs pa'i dngul gyi mchod rten khru bzhi pa gcig byas pa phu chung
bas gsan pas/ dngul las byas na nga'i grogs po'i gdung ma 'ongs pa na mi ngan gyis grogs mor spung nge 'ong dogs 'dug ste/ da byas rting rab gnas nga la bab pas/ dbyar
rgyal gyi do bo dgon par 'gro ba'i zhor la bya gsung nas/ tshul khar rab gnas mdzad/ tshul zhugs do bo dgon par bzhugs nas/ khyi lo'i ston yung ba'i phu chung du byon/ bdun
bcu rtsa drug bzhes pa rgyal zla'i nyi shu gsum la thegs/ la lar do bo dgon par sku gshegs zer ba'ang 'dug go/ bshes gnyen spo to ba ni/ 'khrungs yul spras bra bo thang/
gdung rus gnyos/ yab sku gshen srid la dbang phyug/ yum le mo bya ba'i sras su me mo yos la 'khrungs/ byis pa'i dus su yab kyi mchod gnas sba sgom bya ba la sgom bslab
par zhus pas/ khong gi zhal nas thos pa en re ma byas pa'i sgom mchan khung bas phu thag thung gsung/ byis pa'i dus nas byang chub kyi sems skyes thob tu mnga' bar shar
ba pa'i bstod pa las gsungs/ de nas yer par rdog byang chub 'byung gnas dang/ glan tshul khrims byang chub la mkhan slob zhus nas rab tu byung/ mtshan rin chen gsal du btags/
jo bo chen po dang yang de dus yer par mjal/ dge bshes ston pa byang du 'bul ba'i gser bsgrub pa la bzhud 'dug pas/ nag tshos lo tsA mdzad/ sgom rim tshar gcig gsan/
de nas khu ston gyi drung du byon mtshan nyid kyi chos mang du gsan/ yer pa'i zhang btsun la gnas kyi slob dpon zhus/ de nas ra sgreng du bshes gnyen

ston pa'i drung du dbyar de gdams ngag gcig zhus nas/ ston khams su 'byon dgongs pa la/ sku mched gsum lhig tu thog mar lam rim dang/ spyod 'jug gsan pas/ bdag ni grol ba don
gnyer la/ rnyed dang bkur stis 'ching mi dgos/ shes zhes pa'i skabs kyi man ngag gsungs pa'i thad du thugs snang 'gyur te/ tshe 'di'i rnam rtog skyur nas bshes gnyen bsten
pa yin gsung/ ston pa lo bdun bsten yon tan thams cad rdzogs par thob/ thugs rab che bas shin du mnyes/ ston pa gshegs khar sku mched gsum gyi thugs la 'jigs sar skyel
mas bor ba 'dra ba zhig yong bar 'dug na/ da su la brten snyam ste spyan chab byung bas/ mngon shes kyis mkhyen nas/ ngas khyed gsum gyi brten sa su yang ma mthong bas/
da phyin gsum yan/ lnga man dpung gdang 'chos la/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen mdo sde la gyis/ sems bzang por gyis dang/ khyad par can gcig dang 'phrad de 'ong cig gsung/ mdun
na jo bo legs yod pas sems bzang po bya ba byang chub kyi sems la zer ba ma lags sam zhus pas/ yin mod gsung bas/ de snga nas ma go rgyu med pa la/ des gsal btab pa 'dra
ba zhig byung nas/ de'i thabs lkog tu man ngag tu yang gsungs/ tshogs su lung dang sbyar nas kyang gsungs/ tha na bka' bkyon tshun chod kyis kyang/ de'i thabs gsungs nas
yod pas/ lo bcu gnyis tsam du mya ngan sangs pa 'dra ba cig byung/ phyis sems bzang po byed pa la/ khong rang dgos par song bas mya ngan la sangs dus ma byung gsung/ ra
sgreng nas byon te sku mched gsum dang po klu shod na mgor bzhugs/ de nas gnas nges med du sgrub pa mdzad/ thugs gting zab pas

yon tan 'di yod cher mi gsung yang/ byang chub kyi thugs rang 'khrungs kyi tshul du mnga'/ yi dam dpag tu med pa'i zhal gzigs/ mngon bar shes pa rgya chen po dang ldan pa'i
tshul bsam gyis mi khyab bo/ gzhan phan mdzad pa'i thog mar lam sgron/ yon tan mthas par bstod pa/ bslab btus sogs gsungs pas/ gra grwa pa sum brgya tsam byung/ de nas rim
gyis 'phel te gra grwa pa nyis stong tsam 'dus/ de thams cad kyang tshe 'di blos thongs pa sha stag yod par grags/ ram sding ma ba drung na bzhugs dus/ chas rkyen med
pas zas gos cung zad gnang ba la/ 'di ye mi gnang bar zhu/ bdag gi blo chud zos nas/ zad dus dge bshes kyis gnang ste 'ong snyam nas/ brnab sems skye zhus pas/ khyed ma 'dzom
snyam nas yi chad mi dgos/ nga gnas brtan bcu drug gi ma ba gcig yin pas/ nga dang mjal ba bsod nams che gsung/ phyis gnas brtan yan lag 'byung gi sprul par zhal gyis
bzhes/ zang zing gi dngos po bre gang yang 'dzin chags mi mdzad/ phyis spo tor bzhugs nas gzims chung ka gnyis ma dpe khang du grags pa sogs la brten nas bzhugs/ gzhan
phan mchog tu gyur te/ dgung lo don dgu bzhes pa shing mo bya la spo tor tshul zhugs zla ba'i nyer dgu la yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ shar phyogs kyi nam mkha' la lhas rol
mo dang bcas te spyan drangs pa snang ba dag pa rnams kyis mthong/ de nas phyag thal mo sbyar te/ sems can thams cad kyi gnas dang skyabs dang mgon du gyur cig gsung ste
thegs/ gdung bzhu bas thugs ljags dang ring srel kha dog sna lnga mang du byon/ de nas sras chen brgyad kyis ka ba der gtsugs pa'i dbu rtse ka ba brgyad ma dang/ zhang ston
shar ba pas

sngar gyi chos ra'i sa la khyams ka ba nyi shu rtsa lnga yod pa bzhengs so/ sngon gyi gtam brgyud la/ spo to'i sgo la sus 'dzul rgyal/ sding ma'i chu la sus 'thung rgyal/ zer
ba la/ kha gcig spo to'i sgo stengs su sdings ma ba'i gzims sa mdzad pas zer kyang/ spo to ba chos gsung ba'i sgo nang du su tshud rgyal zer ba'i don yin gsung/ rgyas
par don du gnyer na rnam thar che chung gnyis 'dug par blta'o/ 'di la slob ma'i mchog bka' babs brgyad la sogs pa bka' gdams gzhung pa'i srol 'dzin byon tshul 'og tu 'chad
do/ grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po spyan snga pa ni/ 'khrungs yul nyan gyi snang ra sgang / gdung rus dbas/ yab shAkya rdo rje/ yum li mo ye shes sgron gyi sras su lcags
mo bya la 'khrungs/ mtshan stag tshab 'bar zer/ byis pa'i dus su yum gyis dpang du khyer nas/ grong 'dul ba bya ba la phung po lnga'i rab byed gsan pas/ phung po 'di lngar
'byed tshod kyis mthar stong pa nyid du 'dug snyam du/ rang bzhin med pa'i don thugs su chud/ dgung lo bcu gnyis la gong mo sgang pa bya ba rang bzhin gyi rnal 'byor ma
gcig byon/ rdzogs rim zab pa gcig gnang nas/ 'di bsgoms gsung ste mi snang bar gyur/ phyis de'i steng du sleb pa dpal ldan dgon pa bas gnang ba de min pa ma byung gsung/
bcu bco brgyad pa la stod lungs tsha thog dgon par mal shes rab sems dpa' la rab byung zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims 'bar du btags der yum gyi rmi lam du dung dkar gcig bus
pas dzam 'dzam bu gling pa byin gyis thos pa gcig byung bas/ nga'i bu de rab tu byung nas grags pa yang che ba gcig 'ong bar 'dug zer/ slob gnyer mdzad dus

tsha thog dgon par byon pa'i zhor la/ jo bo snye thang na mo cher bzhugs pa dang mjal te/ sems skyed gsung pa gsan/ de'i dus spyi bor phyag gzhag/ saMskr-i ta'i skad du bkra
shis kyi tshig bcad mang po mdzad/ gser gling pa'i bum pa padma'i mchu can gnang/ nga'i chos brgyud 'dzin pa zhig 'ong gsung/ de nas lan tsha rab dang/ rgyug par sde snod
kyi gsan sbyong mang du mdzad/ rgya gar rdo rje gdan chos kyi 'byung khungs yin pas der 'byon dgos dgongs te/ lo tsA dang rgya yig mang du bslabs/ de'i tshe yum rgyug
par byon nas/ 'di rnams phal cher dgra 'dres gtser ba dang/ lto don du gnyer ba sha stag yin/ chos bya sams bsams nas rab tu byung ba ni khyod dang zha btsun gnyis yin/ snying
nas chos byed na ra sgreng du 'deng zer nas/ yum gyis khrid de dgung lo nyer drug la 'brom ston pa dang mjal/ spyan snga'i zhal nas/ nga'i ma rang bzhin gyi rnal 'byor
ma yin pas/ 'dir bskyal ba yin gsung/ rgya gar du 'gro ba'i chos 'dra zhus pas/ ston pa'i zhal nas/ khyod rdo rje gdan du ma 'gro/ ngas rjes su 'dzin pa yin/ tshes grangs
'di la lam rim gyi dbu 'dzugs gsung ste byon/ nyi ma shar ba dang 'dzom pas rten 'brel bzang gsung ste/ lam rim khrid pas ji ltar ba bzhin thugs la 'khrungs/ sku mched
gzhan gnyis dang dpe gcig la phu chung ba dbus su byas te gzhung gi bshad pa gsan/ spyan snga'i zhal nas/ zin nges pa re la'ang lan gsum gsum ston pa'i spyan sngar bskyar
nas shog gu dmar po la bris yod gsung/ nub gcig rnal lam du rdo rje gdan du byon pa

rmis te/ jo bo shes rab dbang phyug bya ba rdo rje gdan lan gsum bskor pa zhig dang zhu thug byas pas gcig par byung/ rgya gar du mi thon pa la blta bar 'dug/ de'i dam bca'
ma grub pa'i sdig sbyongs su ngas sA tsha bsags na ri de'u tsam 'ong ba btab gsung/ lo bdun lo dgu yin tshul bzhin du bsten gzims g.yog mdzad/ rgyun du spyan sngar bzhugs
pas mtshan yang de ltar du grags/ yon tan thams cad rdzogs par mdzad/ de dus ston pas theg pa chen po gasngags la 'o kol pha phad gnyis tsam yin gsung pa'i yong rdzong
rnal 'byor pas zhu sna mdzad de gasngags kyi chos mang po sku mched gzhan gnyis la thugs rgyus med par klog chos su gnang bas/ yong rdzong rnal 'byor pa de nga la drin che
gsung/ ston pa gshegs nas zang zing gi bgo skal med de/ chos kyi bgo skal nged gsum gyis thob gsung/ de nas jo bo'i dngos slob grags che ba rnams la bsten pa'i dam bca'
mdzad de/ rnal 'byor/ dgon pa ba/ shes rab rdo rje/ phyag dar ston pa sogs dang/ gsang phu ba rngog legs she yang zla ba bcu bco brgyad bsten/ ra sgreng du zla ba rer nas
bre lnga lnga la brten te sgrub pa mdzad dus rang la rigs kyi bu/ dal 'byor mi lus thob pa dran nam gsung nas/ rnal bsangs te nyin mtshan g.yel med du thugs dam mdzad pas/
rnal 'byor pa'i zhal nas/ bu khams bag re gsengs gsungs pas/ dal 'byor rnyed par dka' ba 'di bsams na/ skad cig kyang g.yel ma nus gsung/ skye rim la brtan pa thob pas
rang lus mi g.yo ba'i skur gzigs/ mi g.yo ba'i bsnyen pa dung phyur dgu song/ spyan ras gzigs padma gar dbang dang/ 'jam dpal brtan pa'i 'khor lo la sogs pa zhal gzigs/
pha bong thang du glen klu'i byang chub dang mjal/ chos zhu

dgongs pa na mi snang bar gyur/ rang dad gus chungs chung pas yin nam dgongs te/ bdag byin brlabs kyi sgor zhugs nas gsol ba btab pas/ dngos su byon nas byin gyis brlabs/ chos
bzhi tshan bzhi la sogs pa gsungs pa ni/ gnyid dang rmi lam gyi dpes/ snang ba 'di 'khrul par shes pa'i rnal 'byor/ chab dang chab rol gyi dpes/ snang stong dbyer med
du shes pa'i rnal 'byor/ bu ram gyi ming gzugs kyi dpes/ snang grags kyi chos thams cad ro gcig tu shes pa'i rnal 'byor/ spyod pa pha rol du phyin pa drug la bslab gsung/
thams cad sems su rtogs pas chos thams cad la skur pa mi gdab/ sems sangs rgyas su rtogs kyang dge ba'i bshes gnyen mi spang/ rang la 'khor ba dang ngan song gi dogs pa
med kyang/ sdig pa mi dge ba phra mo tsam yang spang/ rang dang sems can tha dad med par rtogs kyang/ sems can thams cad la snying rje chen po mi spang gsung/ ting nge 'dzin
sems la zhog/ yang dag don la bltos/ byams dang snying rje bsgoms/ lha sku 'ja' tshon lta bur sbyongs gsung/ a skye ba med pa/ rlung mtshan ma med pa/ sems rang bzhin
med pa/ re zhig lus la brten pa yin zhes sogs mang du gsungs so/ de nas sku mched gsum po so sor byon nas/ klu shod phyor ba sogs gnas nges med du gzhan don rgya cher mdzad/
dgung lo drug bcu la nyan du phebs/ ra sgreng btab nas lo ngo so bdun 'gro ba chu mo bya lo la/ jo bo yab sras kyis lung bstan pa'i lo'i gtsug lag khang/ gsang ba 'dus
pa'i thig btab nas rmang bting/ dbu rtse khyams stod dang bcas pa/ 'gran gyi do med lnga la sogs pa bzhengs nas chu mo yos yan la 'das lo sum brgya dang go gcig song/
de'i dus glang ri thang pa nyan gyi tshan sar dpon slob stong tsam

chos gsan zhor la/ lo'i grog mdo yan rdo kyags leb rgyang bdun tsam dang/ bkra shis mched lnga'i bla g.yel dpangs sum thog tsam la shar nub tu 'dom nyi shu rtsa drug yod pa
dang/ shar ba pa slob ma mang po dang bcas te chos gsan cing/ mkhar las kyi grogs mdzad pas/ dgon pa myur du grub/ dbu rtse'i rgyab tu sgrub chu dang/ bkra shis mched lnga'i
rab gnas la nA ga ba dhi dngos su spyan drangs tshul sogs kyang 'byung/ lor lo brgyad bzhugs/ dge 'dun sum brgya tsam 'dus/ lo nas smyug tum dgon par byon pa'i lam du
pha bong dkar leb bya ba'i steng nas/ bya yul gyi rgyab ri gzigs bas/ ri de rgyal ba'i gtsug tor 'dra/ yan lag brgyad ldan chu bo 'bab/ de yi shar lho'i phyogs mtshams
na/ tshe dang ldan pa'i dgon gnas yod/ ri bya yul yu pa ba pha gi thad du gtsug lag khang bzhengs la/ sems can la phan pa rgya chen po gyis shes zhes lung bstan/ der zhabs
rjes kyang byon/ de nas smyug tum du lo gsum bzhugs/ bla ma dang yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ nga ni tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa'i gang zag zhig yin/ nga'i rdo rje'i gdan 'di
yin gsung ngo / gtsang pa rin po che'i zhal nas/ bar dor mchog gi dngos grub brnyes pa'i gsung yin gsung/ dgung lo don gcig bzhes pa lug lo'i smin drug zla ba'i nyer gnyis
la smyug tam du thegs/ 'di la slob ma'i mchog sgom nga/ 'gran gyi do med gsum la sogs pa bka' gdams gdams ngag pa'i srol 'dzin byon tshul 'og tu 'chad do/ de yang sku
mched gsum rang gi gsung ltar na/ gnas brtan chen po bcu drug gi rnam 'phrul du byed/ rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul par byed pa ni lam yig las/ bal yul gyi 'phags pa shing
kun la

nam gyi gung mi ma yin rnams skor ba byed pa'i khrod du/ rdo rje phag mo'i grub pa thob pa gcig gis skor ba byas pas/ gling bu'i skad 'dra ba'i glu las/ sngon dang sngon gyi
dus tsa na/ thugs dgongs bla na med pa de/ jo bo a ti sha la yod/ rtogs pa bla na med pa de/ jo bo a ti sha la yod/ da lta ma rig mun par 'khyam/ zer ba dang/ yang/ a ti
sha yi gdung 'tshob pa/ 'phags pa sku mched gsum po yin/ gcig tsam lho bal mtshams na yod/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal dang gnyis su med/ gcig tsam bal po'i yul na yod/ 'phags
pa wa ti dang gnyis su med/ gcig tsam mang yul grong na yod/ 'phags pa bhu ga dang gnyis su med/ zer ba gsan pas/ rten de rnams rigs gsum mgon po dngos dang khyad med pas/
de rnams kyi sprul pa yin par byed ces gsung/ rgyal bu chags pa med pa'i skyes rabs las/ bla ma chags pa med pa'i zhal nas/ sras kyi snying po chags pa med/ bdag gi rab
'byin mgon par gyur/ de bzhin khye'u stong phrag dag/ lnga bdo snyigs ma ma rung tshe/ khyod kyi srid 'dzin 'gro ba bskyong/ mtha' mkhob yul gyi dbus su byed/ rin chen phreng
ba bstan pa'i dpal/ nor bu brtsegs pa bzhin du skyong/ sa bcu'i mgon po 'jam pa'i dpal/ bstan pa rin chen gsal bar byed/ sa bcu'i dbang phyug spyan ras gzigs/ ston
pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin par byed/ sa bcu'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'dzin/ tshul khrims me lce rab 'bar te/ 'chal pa'i bud shing bsreg par byed/ ces gsungs so/ de ltar bshes gnyen
ston pa la las can gyi slob ma brgyad bcu tsam mtsho la padmas brgyan pa ltar byon pa las/ chos kyi brgyud pa 'dzin pa'i mchog 'phags pa sku mched gsum yin no/ gsum
pa de las 'phros pa byon

tshul la gnyis/ spo to ba nas brgyud pa bka' gdams gzhung pa'i slob ma byon tshul/ spyan snga ba nas brgyud pa bka' gdams gdams ngag pa'i slob ma byon tshul lo/ dang po ni/
spo to ba la spyir slob ma mang du byon kyang grags che ba mtha'i ka chen brgyad / dbus kyi nyi zla zung gcig ces pa ltar na/ gtsang du ram snang gnyis/ gnyal du glang gnyos
gnyis/ dol du 'be dog gnyis/ khams su bya phag gnyis/ dbus su glang shar gnyis rnams yin la/ bka' babs brgyad du byed na/ bya phag gnyis mi 'dren par/ byams snying rje
byang chub kyi sems bdag gzhan brje nus pa'i bka'/ glang ri thang pa rdo rje seng ge la babs/ bka' 'gyur ro cog la gzhung bshad byed pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la
mnga' brnyes pa 'dra ba yod pa'i bka'/ shar ba pa yon tan grags la babs/ gsung rab thams cad skyes bu gsum gyi gdams ngag tu dril nas sman pa mkhas pas nad brtags te nad
thog tu sman gtong ba 'dra ba yod pa'i bka'/ snang rde'u lhas pa ye shes rgyal mtshan la babs/ stong nyid kyi lta bas dngos po dang mtshan mar 'dzin pa thams cad 'jig nus
pa yod pa'i bka'/ ram sding ma ba 'byung gnas rdo rje la babs/ rtsod pa paNDi ta'i rgol ba yang bzlog nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ dol pa shes rab rgya mtsho la babs/ bla ma
la sangs rgyas dngos kyi mos gus rgyun chad med pa yod pa'i bka'/ gnyal pa chos 'bar la babs/ dang tshugs mchog zung gcig la 'gran nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ gras pa gzhon nu
'od gras pa yon tan 'od yang zer la babs/ rgyun du dkon mchog gi drung du mchod pa bkra lam me ba 'bul ba yod pa'i bka'/ dge bshes brag dkar ba la babs so/ de yang glang
ri thang pa ni/ 'khrungs sa 'phan yul gnya' gong gser ma bshongs/

yab jo bo dar ma mdo bzang gi sras su shing pho rta la 'khrungs/ rus zhugs tshang/ kho rang gi zhang po bshes gnyen grog mo mkhar pa la rab tu byung/ mtshan rdo rje seng ger
btags/ rgyal ba 'od dpag tu med pa'i sprul par byed la/ sngon lo tsA ba ka ba dpal brtsegs su sprul nas bstan pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad cing/ 'dir gdul bya blo dman pa
rnams kyi ngor/ dang po shin du bkren pa'i tshul mdzad de lo na spyan snga la chos gsan dus yos sbar ba res gdan gnon mdzad kyi bzhugs/ de nas bsod snyoms mdzad pa'i rnyed
pa gang byung/ spyir dge 'dun dang/ khyad par spo to ba dpon slob la drangs pas sku bsod skyes pa ltar mdzad de/ gra grwa pa nyis stong tsam 'tshogs pa'i rgyags khong
rang gis gnang/ gnas nges med du bshad sgrub zung 'brel du mdzad/ gtso bor spo to ba yun ring du bsten/ phu chung ba dang/ kham pa lung pa chen po sogs la yang chos gsan/
spo to ba gshegs nas thang grong ltag tu gtor ma mdzad dus/ gtor sder bya rog gis khyer te/ glang thang gi shar ri de'u de'i khar gzhag pas/ dpon shAka bya bas zhabs tog
byas te der lo gsum sgrub pa mdzad/ zhol du sgrub chu yang byung/ nyin mtshan dbyer med du byang chub kyi sems kyi ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pa'i mdangs la/ klu mo spun gsum
gyis glang thang gi gnas phul/ dge 'dun gyi sde 'dzugs par zhus/ phyis ri de'i steng nas yar 'phur te thugs phreng skyur sar khron pa brus/ dbu zhwa skyur sar bla brang
byas te dgon pa btab/ slob ma mang du 'dus/ bka' gdams gzhung drug lam sgron sogs la 'chad nyan mdzad cing/ bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub

kyi sems kho na la gtso bor mdzad de/ kho bos rlung tha mal du gtong ma myong gsung/ zhal bzhugs rin ring glang thang gi lcags ri'i nang du srog chags rnams gcig la gcig mi
'tshe bar grags/ dgung lo bdun bcu pa chu mo yos kyi sa ga zla ba la dpe'i chos lung du sku gshegs/ rgya lcags ri gong kha ba byang chub dpal ni/ khams su glang ri thang
pa'i snyan pa thos pas/ dbus su chos la 'byon pa'i 'dun pa yod pa/ srin mo zhig gi gnod pas/ lo ngo drug 'das/ khong rang yang sngags kyis bcings te khyi'i lus su bsgyur
yang/ glang ri thang pa dang mjal bar 'gron po'i phyi la yongs/ srin mos mnan du slebs pa na/ glang ri thang pas mkhyen pas der byon bgegs bskrad/ gtor mas byin gyis brlabs
pas mi'i lus su gyur/ stong nyid snying rje thugs su chud de slob ma'i mchog tu gyur/ jo bo'i slob ma bshes gnyen bal bo bas btab pa'i lcags ri gong khar bzhugs pas rgya
lcags ri bar grags so/ gzhan yang slob ma che ba dge bshes lcags zhing pa/ khyung po rnal 'byor/ ra lo tsA ba/ gnyan chen po zhang zhung/ mdo sde la sogs byon la/ gdan
sa sha bas glang thang dang shar ba sbrel nas/ dge 'dun sum stong tsam 'dus/ de nas gdan sa zhang zhung pas mdzad/ mchod rten chen mo drang srong gis bskul te bzhengs te
bzhengs tshul dang / bar du rin chen sgang pas bdag byas pa sogs rgyas par ma spros so/ zhang shar ba pa chen po ni/ pa tshab dom po'i rgyud du lcags khyi la/ yum phyugs
bskyong ba'i dus/ rdo leb steng du 'khrungs te/ de la zhabs rjes kyang byon/ dgung lo bcu bco brgyad pa la klu shod phyor bar bros te rab tu byung/ mtshan yon tan grags
su btags/ de nas spyan snga ba phyor phur sku mtshams

mdzad pa'i sar mjal/ zla ba bzhi mtshams khrod du bzhugs te chos gsan/ da nga'i grogs po'i rtsar brgyugs gsung bas stag lung du spo to ba'i spyan sngar byon/ gra grwa pa lo
dgu/ nang mi lo dgu ste bcu bco brgyad bsten/ zhar la phu chung pa dang/ spyan snga ba la yang 'dod chos rdzogs par gsan/ spo to ba gshegs nas yon tan gyi rjes su 'brang
ba'i 'khor rnams dang lhan cig klung shod du byon te tshogs pa bsdus/ de nas gnas nges med du 'chad nyan mdzad pas/ gra grwa pa nyis stong brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ de rnams
phal cher chos don gnyer sha stag go/ de yang bshes gnyen ston pa/ rnal 'byor pa/ dgon pa ba/ sku mched gsum/ sne'u zur pa/ shar ba pa rnams la bka' gdams zhal brgyad
du grags so/ snang dren lhas pa'i rnam thar ma mthong zhing/ ram sding ma ba 'byung gnas rdo rje'i rnam thar che chung gsum 'dug pa'i skye ba bcu drug pa'i rnam thar du/
bdag nyid ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par ga tsa na/ bskal pa stong gi skye ba dran te/ yab yum bla ma dang/ chos gang la zhus pa/ rus dang rigs dang/ gnas dang phyogs thams
cad kyang dran/ dus rgyun du sa le ba ni skye ba bcu drug dran no zhes gsung la/ gtsang smad du ram sdiing ma'i chos sde btab/ gzhi bdag gis mdzo mo dkar mo gcig phul ba
sa la thim pas/ chu mig khyad par can zhig byung ste/ rgya gar gyi mda' chu khron pa skyes dang khyad med/ sus 'thungs kyang rgyal gsung/ gra grwa pa stong tsam byung/ slob
ma gcig la khyod lho brag tu song/ 'di kho na 'dra ba'i sa cha yod/ der dgon pa thob/ bla ma dang dgon pa'i ming yang gcig pa thogs gsung ste/ lho brag sding ma de las
brgyud do/ dol pa shes rab rgya mtsho ni/ jo bo dol du phebs dus/ yul 'di nas byang chub sems dpa' rtags mtshan can zhig

'byung/ zhes lung bstan te/ sa pho 'brug la 'khrungs/ yang zhogs gad kyi dgon pa btab/ spo to ba'i gsung la zin bris su mdzad pa phyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa la/ be'u bum
sngon por grags pa mdzad/ rog dmar zhur du grags te 'khor stong tsam 'dus/ dgung lo bdun bcu rtsa gsum pa phag lo rgyal zla'i tshes bcu gsum la thegs/ slob ma che ba bde
legs phag mo gru pa sogs byon kyang/ chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i mchog don stengs pa chos skyabs bzang po dang/ lha 'bri sgang pa chen po sogs byon/ don stengs pas blo'i phur
don stengs btab nas gra thang dang sbrags nas bzung/ lha 'bri sgang pas be'u bum sngon po la 'grel pa legs pa gcig la de phris che zhing/ 'on gyi phur 'bri sgang gi dgon
pa btab/ tshogs pa'ang mang du 'dus bar skabs su 'bri sgang gi dgon bdag bya yul bas mdzad nas mkhan po'i bko gzhag kyang mang du mdzad snang ngo/ 'be se dkar bas gzhung
gi mdar ra brags kyi gtsug lag khang btab/ mkhan brgyud shin du 'phel bar byung ngo / grab pa yon tan 'od yang zer gzhon nu 'od ni/ 'phan yul grab tu 'khrungs / bzhugs
gnas grab phu'i phrong sdings te/ khong rang gzhon nu nas thos pa che bas/ dang por spo to ba la chos kyi tshod bltar byon kyang/ phyis mi phyed pa'i dad pa skyes te/ klog
chos lo bcu drug gsan/ spo to ba'i gsung sgros bsgrigs pa'i dpe chos rtsa 'grel mdzad de/ dge bshes brag dkar ba spre'u lo pa/ 'khor bzhi brgya tsam 'dus/ dpe chos gsan
pa'i ched du grab pa'i slob ma mdzad/ dgung lo brgyad bcu pa yos lo'i dgun zla tha chung gi nyer gnyis la thegs/ de'i slob ma slob dpon byang chub

snang ba/ de'i slob ma don grub lce sgom/ de'i slob ma skyer sgang pa la sogs byon no/ bka' babs kyi nang nas zhang ston shar ba pa spo to ba'i chos srol 'dzin pa'i mchog ste/
'di la slob ma'i mchog bka' babs lngar grags pa ni/ byang chub thugs kyi bka' babs mchad kha ba/ byin brlabs kyi bka' babs gtum ston blo gros grags/ gzhung bshad kyi
bka' babs dam pa stabs ka ba/ rnam thar bka' babs nye mal 'dul 'dzin/ 'dis klungs shod mdar dgon pa btab/ longs spyod kyi bka' babs rnal 'byor shes rdor/ 'dis shar ba pa'i
gdan sa lo gsum mdzad do/ dang po bya mchad kha ba ni/ 'khrungs yul lo ro/ gdung rus bya/ yab 'phags pa skyabs/ yum bsod nams skyid kyi sras su lcags sbrul la 'khrungs/
dwags po gtsang 'dul la rab tu byung zhus/ mtshan ye shes rdo rje btags/ gnyal du ngor rje brtsan btsan po'i chos 'khor la byon pas/ ba ri lo tsA ba rngog lo tsA ba sogs
sde snod 'dzin pa mang po grub mtha'i rnam dbye 'byed pa gzigs pas/ chos tshol ba la mos te byon/ g.ye chung gi sgre dgon pa na spyan snga ba'i slob ma sgre pa chen po bzhugs
pa dang mjal/ bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po zhus pas ma gnang/ sgre pa la jo gdan tsha rong pa dang/ dwags po gtsang 'dul mjal du byon pa la/ mkhan slob zhus nas bsnyen
rdzogs mdzad de sha mi la 'dul ba gsan/ de nas lar lungs su byon te bshes gnyen mang po bsten/ khyad par glang ri thang pa'i slob ma lcags zhing pa la blo sbyong tshig
rkang brgyad ma gsan pas dad nas/ spo to ba'i slob ma dol pa dang/ lugs smad pa gnyis lo bzhi bsten/ dol pa la be'u bum sngon po yang gsan

de nas dgung lo sum bcu la/ glang ri thang pa la gtad nas byon kyang ma mjal bar/ shar ba pa bzho'i khang pa gnas na bzhugs pa dang mjal/ dang por tshogs chos gsan/ de nas
blo sbyong rtsa chod de nyams khrid du lo dgu bskyangs pas/ bdag gces 'dzin gyi 'khri pa chod pa cig byung gsung/ ston chos la bya yul du byon/ sprul sku bya yul ba la gdams
ngag gi skor rnams rdzogs par gsan/ 'phan yul du byon nas kyang shar ba pa yung ring du bsten/ de nas gnas nges med du thugs dam gyi gtso bo blo sbyong la mdzad cing/
bka' dgo pa la/ phyis 'gres phu sgom chen sdings su nye gnas la khyod kyis slob ma 'di rnams la mar khu'i skyog 'dren gyis/ ming ston byed gsung nas/ don bdun gyi sa bcad
mdzad de tshogs chos su gsungs/ de nas mal gror byon/ mchad kha rnying ma btab/ lo bcu gcig tu chos gsungs pas/ slob ma stong tsam 'dus/ de nas mtha' phur zla ba brgyad
bzhugs/ khyad par gyi sras se spyil phu ba/ dan tsha rab kyi rnal 'byor byang seng/ rong po bo dhi satA/ dwags po nyang sogs dang yab sras gnyis ka'i slob ma rnal 'byor
byang seng gis dro pa btab/ gzhan yang lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa sogs mang du byon/ bdun bcu rtsa lnga pa shing lug zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes lnga la mtha' phur thegs/
gdung bzhu bas thugs ljags sogs byon/ gser gyi me tog gi char babs par grags te/ rgyas par blo sbyong gi byung tshul dang/ rnam par che chung du blta'o/ de'i khyad par gyi
sras seng spyil phu ba ni/ 'khrungs yul ldo stod zer gnyal stod dar ma sgang/ gdung rus se/ dgung sding lcags mo glang/ rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs gnyis ka'i mkhan po
phya pas mdzad/ mtshan chos kyi rgyal mtshan du btags/ bya mchad kha

ba dang mjal yung ring du bsten cing yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mdzad sngar bya mchad kyis lung bstan pa bzhin mchad kha gsar ma btab/ mchad kha ba chen po'i nang rten
du sku lder rin po che dang phyi rten gyi mchod rten la sogs pa bzhengs nas klungs shod du byon/ spyil phu'i dgon pa btab ste/ rnam g.yeng spangs nas stod du mkhar gong
la kha/ smad du nyung zhing sgang du mtshams mtho brgyab nas lo bdun du mtshams mi 'da' mdzad/ de nas brag dkar gnas brtan sogs kyis spyan drangs nas/ mchad khar dgun
chos la byon pas/ ding sang gi bar dbyar gyi tshul zhugs spyil phur mdzad/ dgun chos mchad khar gsung ba'i srol byung la/ gdul bya du ma smin par mdzad nas/ drug bcu rtsa
dgu pa sa mo bya'i lo dbyar zla ra ba'i tshes bcu gsum la spyil phur gshegs/ 'di la slob ma'i mchog lha chen po rgya spang pa thang pa/ nyan lha sdings pa sogs mang du byon
pa las/ lha chen po ni/ yab jo bo rnal 'byor/ yum sna nam gza'i sras su stag lo la pho brang khang dmar du 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu bco lnga la rgya dur gyi mkhan po klubs
dkar dang/ gtsang pa khyung po la mkhan slob zhus/ bya sar rab tu byung ste mtshan byang chub rin chen du btags/ de nas bya mchad kha ba'i sku 'dra gzigs pas dad pa'i
rkyen byas te/ dge bshes se dang mjal/ chos mang du zhus/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi la rgya sar sgang nas mkhan po glan spyan drangs te bsnyen par rdzogs/ gzhan yang kha che paN
chen la sogs pa bla ma mang du bsten/ se spyil bu ba gshegs nas/ mchad kha spyil bu'i gdan sa mdzad/ bka' 'gyur gyi lung bzhugs pas lha lung gi dbang phyug gi tu grags/
sangs rgyas sman bla sogs yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs pa rnam thar du

gsal/ 'brug lo bdun bcu rtsa lnga pa la mchad khar thegs/ lha 'gro ba'i mgon po ni/ yab jo 'bag gi sras su rta lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu drug pa la mchad khar khu bo'i drung du
dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa zhus/ de nas skyor mo lung du sbal ti la rab tu byung ste/ mtshan dbang phyug 'od du btags/ de nas spo tor dge bshes gnas brtan la mkhan po zhus
te bsnyen par rdzogs/ lha chen po gshegs nas gdan sa mdzad/ mi g.yo ba'i grub pa brnyes pas stag sham can du yang grags/ gdul bya mang po smin par mdzad nas/ bdun bcu rtsa
bzhi pa lug lo zla ba dgu pa'i nyer gcig la spyil phur thegs/ lha brag kha ba ni/ jo bo shAkya bkra shis kyi sras su khyi lo la 'khrungs/ lha 'gro mgon dang mjal te rab
tu byung/ mtshan ye shes blo gros su btags/ sbas pa ston gzhon sogs la chos rnams rdzogs par gsan/ mchan kha spyil gu'i gdan sa mdzad/ sum cu rtsa bdun la thegs/ de nas
jo 'phel gyi sras lha dbang phyug ye shes 'brug lo pa/ zur khang pa snga mar grags pas gdan sa mdzad de/ drug bcu la thegs/ de nas grags pa rin chen gyi sras lha blo gros
'od bya lo pa/ gdan sa lo bzhi bcu mdzad de/ lha rin chen seng ge/ mkhan ches seng ge rgyal mtshan sogs smin par mdzad/ drug bcu rtsa bzhi la thegs/ gdan sa zur khang pa
rin chen seng ges mdzad/ de nas lha shAkya bsod nams/ de rjes lha zur khang pa bsod nams lhun grub/ lha dpal ldan bzang po/ da lta gdan sar bzhugs pa lha bsod nams rgyal
mtshan pa rnams byon no/ mkhan chen seng ge rgyal mtshan pa'i sku che ba'i yon tan rnams jo stan sgom dpal gyis byas pa'i rnam thar du gsal la/

de la slob ma rje btsun ye mgon pa/ byang sems ra sgreng pa shAkya bsod nams sogs mang du byon no/ rgya spang sa thang pa ni/ gdung rus rgya/ mtshan nyi ma dbang phyug/ spang
sa'i dgon pa btab/ dgung po lnga bcu bzhugs/ de nas gdan sar bzang bskos drug bdun dang/ lha'i brgyud pas gzung nas kyang gdan sa bdun brgyad tsam song ngo/ lha sdings
pas nyan gyi lha sdings btab/ blo sbyong bla ma brgyud par ram pa lha sdings pa zhes 'byung la/ stod lungs mdar ram pa lha sdings zhes pa'i dgon pa yod pas/ 'di dang bla
ma gcig mi gcig brtags par bya'o/ ram pa lha sdings pa nas sangs rgyas dbon slob dpon yon tan dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen ram pa lha sdings gnam 'bar bas btab
zer bas mi cig gam snyam/ dka' bzhi pa/ rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa ste/ de rnams kyi rnam thar chos rjes 'tshal min pa bsod nams bzang pos
mdzad par gsol lo/ byin rlabs kyi bka' babs/ gtum ston blo gros grags ni/ gdung rus gtum/ 'khrungs yul shab sgo lnga'i lcags mkhar te shar ba pa sogs bka' gdams kyi bla ma
mang du bsten/ de nas snar gyi mda'i thang la lo ra yod sar spyil po mdzad de/ chu mo bya'i lo la gzhi gtsugs/ snar thang gi dgon pa btab ste lo bcu bzhi bzhugs/ grwa pa
stong tsam 'dus pa'i grags che ba/ rdo ston shes rab grags rdo rje grags yang zer grwa ston bdud rtsi grags/ zhang btsun rdo rje 'od/ rga ston shes rab grags rnams las/
rdo ston shes rab grags la nyid kyis dgon pa 'di bzung la 'gro don bskyongs gsung nas/ khong rang byang rta sde'i chos lung du thugs dam la bzhugs te/ dgung lo brgyad bcu
rtsa gcig po me pho khyi'i lo rgyal gyi zla ba'i nyi shu gsum la chos lung du

gshegs pas chos lung sku gshegs su grags/ de rjes rdo ston gyis gdan sa lo nyi shu mdzad/ de nas zhang btsun rdo rje 'od kyis gdan sa lo brgyad mdzad/ de nas dpal ldan gro
mo che pa/ gdung rus gro/ 'khrungs yul chu sgo ba/ bya'i lo la sku 'khrungs/ rtsis pa gzhon nu seng ge la bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan bdud rtsi grags/ yi dam mang po dang/
gnas brtan bcu drug zhal gzigs/ snar thang gi dbu rtse rnying ma bzhengs/ lam mchog gi rtsa tshig mdzad/ gdan sa lo sum bcu rtsa dgu mdzad de/ 'brug lo brgyad bcu pa la gshegs/
de nas zhang ston chos kyi bla mas gdan sa lo bcu mdzad/ de ni shab sgo lnga'i sna ring du 'brug la 'khrungs/ gdams pa rnams bshes gnyen gong ma nyid la gsan/ mkhyen
pa che bas zhang thams cad mkhyen par grags/ 'dis gdan sa lo bcu mdzad de glang la gshegs/ de nas sangs rgyas sgom pas gdan sa mdzad/ de ni lcags kyi skyo lung dro'i phur/
sa mo phag la 'khrungs/ gro mo che la bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan seng ge skyabs/ mkhan po gong ma gnyis la gdams pa rnams gsan/ blo sbyong tshogs chos chen mor grags
pa dang/ lam sgron gyi TIkka sogs mdzad/ gdan sar lo bcu bzhugs te/ don gnyis pa lcags khyi'i dpyid zla tha chung gi tshes lnga la dben gnas byang chen du gshegs/ de nas
mchims nam mkha' grags ni/ gdung rus mchims/ nyang stod smon gro'i phu kha'ur rta'i lo la sku 'khrungs/ gnas brtan bcu drug gi gcig tu grags/ mkhyen rab che bas spyir brtsams
chos mang du mdzad cing/ khyad par lam mchog gi 'grel pa phul du byung ba zhig kyang mdzad/ gdan sa lo sum bcu rtsa drug mdzad/ chos rgyal 'phags pa'i bla ma yang

mdzad nas/ chu mig chos 'khor gyi gral dbu yang zhus/ 'di'i ring la gnyal zhig gi slob ma grags pa seng ge spyan drangs te/ mtshan nyid kyi bshad grwa'ang gtsugs/ de nas skyo
ston pa ni/ rta nag yang yul du byi ba lo la sku 'khrungs/ mtshan smon lam tshul khrims/ phyag rdor gyi grub pa thob/ snar thang gi gtsug lag khang che ba dang/ lcags
ri sogs mdzad nas gdan sar lo bcu bco lnga bzhugs/ de nas chos rje nyi ma rgyal mtshan pa snar phu'i steng khar ma kha rir bya lo la 'khrungs/ gdan sar lo bdun bzhugs/ stag
brgyad bskos/ chos khrims dam par mdzad/ bla ma 'brom ston la glegs bam cha lag dang bcas pa gsan/ de rjes mkhan chen 'dul ba 'dzin pa ni/ nyang stod rgya bra dpe stod
du glang lo la ze'u'i rigs su sku 'khrungs/ mtshan grags pa brtson 'grus/ rgya yul du byon te se chen dang/ ol bya ru rgyal bu'i bla mchod mdzad/ de nas yar byon te gdan
sa lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du mdzad pas snar thang du longs spyod che zhing/ 'gro don phrin las che bar grags/ de'i rjes mkhan chen grags pa shes rab kyis lug la gdan sar byon
te/ lo bcu gcig gi bar mdzad/ de nas mchims blo bzang grags pas lo sum bcu rtsa dgu'i bar gdan sar bzhugs te/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa rgyas par mdzad
cing/ grwa sar sha khrims dang/ khams pa mi sten pa la sogs pa'i khrims dam par mdzad do/ de nas mkhen dbang rgyal mtshan pa gdan sar byon te/ lo nyi shu rtsa bdun bzhugs/
bslab btus la TIkka'ang mdzad/ 'di'i ring la chen po snyan grags pas kar phugs la gso nam dang nang du gnas brtan lha khang dang/ mkhan chen blo bzang grags pa'i phyi
rten

gyi mchod rten sgo mangs/ phyi'i lcags ri chen mo mdzad de/ de'i rjes su mkhen grub pa shes rab pas gdan sa lo sum bcur mdzad cing/ bka' gdams gzhung drug dang/ lam sgron lab
mchog la sogs pa'i gdams pas 'gro ba mtho dman rnams yang dag pa'i lam la bkod de/ rang lo re bdun pa chu mo yos la zhi bar gshegs/ de nas mkhen bsod nams mchog grub pas
gdan sar lo bcu drug bzhugasate 'gro don bskyangs/ de nas mkhen grags pa donagrub pas gdan sa lo sum bcur mdzad nas go gcig pa phag la gshegs/ de nas mkhen bzod pa dpal
grub gyis kyis gdan sa lo gsum mdzad nas/ rang lo bdun bcu pa la gshegs/ de nas mkhen 'dul ba 'dzin pa dpal ldan bzang pos gdan sa lo gsum mdzad nas rang lo don gnyis pa
chu sbrul la gshegs/ de nas mkhen shes rab rgyal mtshan pa nga gnyis pa chu 'brug la gdan sar byon nas chu yos yan la lo bcu gnyis song ngo/ de ltar na gtum ston gyis snar
thang chu bya la btab nas chu yos yan la 'das lo sum brgya dang sum bcu song bar shes par bya'o/ gzhung bshad kyi bka' babs dam pa stabs ka bas/ stabs ka grwa pa'i sgang
/ 'od 'jo chos kyi sgang/ khra phu longs spyod kyi sgang zhes pa gsum btab grwa pa brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ grags che ba'i slob ma zhang bzhi ni/ zhang ston 'od 'jo ba
dar ma g.yung drung/ zhang ston khang mo che pa/ zhang ston sho ma ra pa/ zhang ston bcom thang pa chen po'o/ thugs kyi sras bzhi ni/ sgang thang dkar ba rdo rje rin chen/
gu ra ba tshul khrims rdo rje/ stabs ka'i rnal 'byor pa nam mkha' rin chen/ khra phu ba 'dul ba 'dzin pa'o/ 'od 'jo zhang ston dar ma g.yung drung la gtad/ de nas rong
ston kha bo ches bskyangs/ khra phu 'dul ba 'dzin pas bskyangs te/ de las 'phros

pa zhang ston dang khra phu ba chen po/ de'i slob ma gtsan dgon pa sogs byon te rgyas par ma spros so/ gnyis pa spyan snga rin po che nas brgyud pa/ bka' gdams gdam ngag pa
byon tshul ni/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug spyan snga ba la slob ma'i mchog sgom bzhi/ 'gran gyi do med gsum dang/ gzhan yang mkha' ru ba/ rom po rdo rje/ g.ye nas sgre pa
chen po/ zhang ston dpal brtsegs/ rgya rtse sgra bo/ 'phan yul gyi sgro lag pa chen po/ zhang ka ma ba shes rab 'od/ ku ma ra shAkya/ sku srung ston pa/ 'dul 'dzin la khur
ston pa/ mchad 'u ba chen po/ dgag dbye shes rin sogs mi chen nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam byon pa'i/ dgag dbye shes rin gyis nyan tshar gyes kyi mchod khang bzhengs/ spyier
grwa pa bdun brgya tsam 'tshogs sgom bzhi ni zar pa phag sgom rdo rje ye shes kyis mal gro zar gyi mchod khang bzhengs/ rgyug pa ston sgom gyis klu shod rgyug pa'i mchod
khang sogs mazhengs/ mang ra sgom pa brtson 'grus 'bar gyis thang skya'i dgon pa btab/ dbu rtse gsar ma bzhengs/ ral pa seng sgom gyis klu shod ngar gyi mchod khang bzhengs
so/ 'gran gyi do med gsum ni/ stod lungs pa chen po/ bya yul ba chen po/ smyug rum pa chen po'o/ smyug rum pas klu shod mdar myug rum gyi dgon pa btab/ stod lungs pa
chen po ni/ 'khrungs yul stod lungs gser phug/ dgung snying spre'u lo pa/ rab tu byung ba khyung po jo bsod la mdzad/ mtshan rin chen snying por btags/ gtsang phyogs la
gzhon nu nas mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer la byon nas/ bla ma seng ge sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po dang/ paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa sogs mkhas pa mang po la mdo sngags kyi gsan
sbyong rgya cher mdzad/ rtsod pa yang bzang/ de nas stod lungs thag mar

dbus gtsang gi ston chen thams cad 'tshogs nas/ chos kyi bgro glengs 'ba' zhig mdzad pas/ khong gis kyang grwa skor la byon/ rtsod pa mdzad pas/ glog skya gtso rgan bya bas
nyan nas/ bod dbus gtsang gi ston chen 'di tsam zhig nyin re bzhin 'tshogs nas/ mar 'khor ba na ngo lugs/ yar thar pa bsgrub lugs kyi chos tshig bzhi pa gcig med par/ klad
pa gas gas ba glang dkar zal la 'tshi ba 'di byung re che zer ba gsan pas/ khos kyang de tsam zhig go 'dug na/ da rgya gar du chos 'tshol ba la 'gro dgongs nas byon pa
dang/ mkha' ru ba'i grwa pa dge slong snam sbyar 'phrag par gzhag pa tshul khrims kyi dri bro ba cig dang mjal te/ tshe ni yun thung shes bya'i rnam pa mang / tshe yi tshad
kyang ji tsam mi shes pas/ ngang mtsho la 'o ma len pa ltar/ rang gi 'dod pa dang du blang bar gyis/ shes zhes gsungs/ de sus mdzad byas pas/ jo bo'i gsung yin zer/ gang
nas byon byas pas/ mkha' ru dgon pa nas 'ongs zer bas/ mkha' rur byon/ skyabs 'gro'i chos skor gsung ba gsan/ de nas mkha' ru bas lung bstan nas/ ra sgreng du rnal 'byor
pa chen po'i spyan sngar byon/ lta ba'i dri ba mang po mdzad pas/ ston pa sngon du thabs goms pas rgyud smin dgos pa yin gsung nas/ thog mar skyabs 'gro dang byams snying
rje nas rim gyis khrid de chos mang du gsan no/ de dus spyan snga ba sku mtshams la bzhugs pas/ rnal 'byor pas mjal sna mdzad de chos gsan/ rtsa ba'i bla ma zhus/ de
nas rnal 'byor pa lo dgu/ dgon pa ba lo lnga bsten/ spyan snga ba lo bdun 'bral med du bsten te/ bka' gdams kyi chos thams cad rdzogs par gsan/ gser srang brgyad brgya 'bul
bar dam bcas te/ phyed phyag tu phyin pa la

spyan snga ba gshegs pas/ bzhi brgya'i tshab tu dgung lo don gsum pa la lam pa'i gtsug lag khang gi rmang bting ste rdzogs par grub/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten snga phyir dpag
tu med pa bzhengs pa'i grags che ba/ rab gnas kyi dus su spyan snga ba la chos gsungs pa'i/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo'i sku la sogs pa rgyud sbyangs ma bdun dang/ rnal 'byor pas
rab gnas mdzad pa spo to'i gsung 'byon/ mkha' ru'i ljang skyes/ btsan gro'i chu khol zhes rten rtags thon gsum du grags pa'i thub pa chu khol sogs mang du bzhengs/ spyan
dang mngon bar shes pa mnga'/ yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ bden gnyis kyi rtogs pa thugs la 'khrungs/ 'gro don rgya cher mdzad de/ slob ma rtogs ldan sdings mo ba gnubs chos
'bar/ dge bshes lha bzo khyung khams po che/ glog skya/ dge bshes zar pa/ bya 'dul 'dzin/ dge bshes gnas brtan la sogs pa rtogs pa dang/ gzhan phan la mnga' brnyes pa
mang du byon te/ lo brgyus rgyus cung zad 'og tu 'chad do/ de nas stod lungs pa dge bshes lha bzo la gdan sa gtod dgongs pa la/ lha bzos mngon shes kyis rig nas gram rda
chad skad sar bzhugs pas glen pa lha bzo de byung na bslab bya 'dra bya rgyu yod pa yin te ma byung/ da dge bshes glog skya dang/ zar pa gnyis kyis 'di dang mal gro zar
gnyis spyi la bskyongs gsung/ der yod pa rnams kyis rjes su rten bzhengs sogs ji ltar byed zhus pas/ spur 'di g.ya' phu rgyu'i rtse la bskyol/ rten ma bzhengs gsung/ 'o na
sprul sku bya yul ba rten bzhengs pa 'dug na/ ji ltar byed zhus pas/ nga khong la drin che ba yin/ lo bdun 'gro ba nas bskyangs/ bla ma spyan snga rnal 'byor pa lta bu
la sprad/

khong rang ji ltar dgongs pa mdzad du chugs gsung/ de nas sku gshegs kar ngas don khyad par can grub pa yin/ zhes lan gsum gsung / drung na yod pas pa'i yi dam gyi lha zhal
mjal ba yin nam zhus pas/ yi dam gyi lha zer nas mig hur re rna ba co bo yod pa min/ chos thams cad don dam par skye pa med cing/ kun rdzob tu rmi lam sgyu ma lta bur rtogs
gsung ste/ brgyad bcu rtsa lnga pa me pho spre'u lo mngon bar byang chub pa'i zla ba'i tshes brgyad la lam pa dgon par sku gshegs/ sang lha bzo dpon slob kyis kyang phebs/
nya ga mo pas mdang ma gir bzhugs pas ma byung zhus pas/ tshe dang ldan pa mi theg pa'i khur chen po cig bskur bar 'dug pas bsdad pa yin/ bla ma dang mdang mjal/ bzod
gsol kyang tshar gsung/ der glog skya'i zhal nas/ nga rgas pas ya gir mi thon/ khyod kyis zar bskyongs gsung/ zar pa'i zhal nas/ nga yang bla ma'i gdan sa dga' ste/ da
ngas zar bskyangs shig gsung/ de nas bya yul ba chen pos kyang phebs/ sngar gyi zhal bkod rnams snyan du gsol bas/ gzhi 'di la gzan gyis dogs pa'i dgongs pa yin yong gsung
ste/ chas rkyen thams cad dang/ sol ba tshun dbur stod nas drangs te gdung khang chen mo bzhengs so/ sprul pa'i sku bya yul ba ni/ mdo ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po las/
phyi ma'i dus na ting 'dzin 'dzin pa dag/ lnga brgya las ni mi nyung der 'byung ste/ mdo sde mchog 'di rgya cher bzung ba la/ de dag sngon du 'dren pa gzhon nu yin/ zhes
lung bstan te/ 'khrungs yul stod lungs go go lung gi grong mkha' rog

gdung rus gnyos/ yab g.yung drung 'bar/ yum stod lungs pa'i lcam sring ljang bza' lcam bu ste/ shing mo yos la 'khrungs/ dgung lo bdun la stod lungs pa chen po dang mjal/ lo
bcu gnyis la stod lungs tsha thog dgon par/ rnal 'byor pa'i slob ma sgom pa byang grags dang/ spyan snga ba'i slob ma sgom pa ye shes rgyal mtshan gnyis la mkhan slob zhus
te/ dge tshul mdzad/ mtshan gzhon nu 'od du btags/ de nas stod lungs pa mal gro zar du 'byon pa'i phyags phyir byon/ lo bcu zhabs tog tshul bzhin mdzad/ thugs 'dzin yangs
pas bslab spyod sogs gzhung che chung rnams tshegs med par thugs su chud par mdzad/ de nas spyan snga ba phyor ba na bzhugs pa/ stod lungs pa dang dpon slob gnyis kyis
mjal du byon pas/ mngon shes kyis gzigs nas/ stod lungs pa la jo bo ston pa re skyid na/ 'khor 'di lta bu yod pa ces yang yang gsung bas/ bla ma mnyes par dgongs te phul/
lo bcu gsum zhabs tog tshul bzhin du mdzad pas/ spyan snga ba mnyes pa'i gsung mang po dang/ byin brlabs zhugs ste nang ma gcig la sde snod gsum dang/ rgyud sde bzhi'i
tshig don ma lus pa thugs la 'khrungs/ spyan snga pa la slob dpon nA ga bo dhi dang mjal ba bde'am zhus pas/ btsun chung 'di 'drir bcug pa'i chos mi 'dra ba gsung/ phyis
gshegs kar ngas slob dpon nA ga bo dhi dang dngos su mjal/ chos mang du zhus rtsa ba'i bla mar byed pa yin/ khyed rang yang gsol ba thob dang rjes su 'dzin par 'dug gsung/
mdor na spyan snga ba'i yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mnga' zhing/ spyan snga ba smyug ram du gshegs nas sku gdung bzhu ba'i dus/ thugs nam mkha' la 'od dang

bcas te/ sprul sku chen po'i dpang par babs pa phyis bya yul gyi gdung khang du bzhugs so/ smyug ram du sku mtshams lo dgu mdzad/ de nas tshogs bsdus te/ thog mar brul gyi
ra ba dkar por dgon pa btab/ dge 'dun lnga brgya tsam 'dus/ de'i tshe rje btsun ma sgrol ma la sogs yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs/ nA ga bo dhi la dngos su chos gsan/ de nas
gdun bya bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang/ dgon pa 'bul ba yang mang du byung ba la/ bla ma dang sgrol mas lung bstan pa'i gnas bya yul du dgon pa 'debs dgongs kyang/ yon bdag
rnams the tshom bsal ba'i phyir/ bshes gnyen mtha' bzhi spyan drangs nas dgon pa thams cad nas rdo re blangs pa la sa dpyad mdzad nas/ se gsal ba'i g.yung drung gis phul
ba/ bya yul nas blangs pa'i rdo la sa'i dpyad bzang bar lung bstan pas/ gzhan rnams kyang ma dga' ba med par mdzad de/ lo dgon pa btab nas/ lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa shing
pho rta'i lo la gtsug lag khang gi rmang bting nas/ lo bcu gsum pa rta lo'i nang tshun la dgon pa gtor tshugs yan rdzogs par grub/ rmang bting nas na ning chu mo yos yan
la 'das lo sum brgya dang bdun bcu song ngo / de'i tshe spyan snga ba rnal lam du byon nas snam sbyar gser mdog can bkon pa rmis pas/ bla mas gnang ba byung gsung nas/
mkhan po rtog chos dbang bya 'dul 'dzin zer las slob mang ra sgom pa/ gsang ston rgya shes rab 'bar gyis mdzad de/ bsnyen par rdzogs/ bya yul du dge 'dun nyis stong lnga
brgya tsam 'dus/ de dus bya yul/ klung shod/ mal gro gsum du dus gcig la gral dbu mdzad pa dang/ mdo smad du ngang tshang ba'i gtsug lag khang gi rab gnas dang/ dwags por
sha ba gling pa'i mchod rten gyi

rab gnas zhus pas dus tshod tshes grangs 'di la mchod pa rgya chen po bshoms/ gsol ba thob/ ngas gzims chung 'di'i steng nas rab gnas byed pa yin gsung ste/ kun gyis mthong
bar gtsug lag khang dang/ mchod rten stengs su phyag nas babs pas/ de nas sprul skur grags/ mi ma yin mang po la chos gsungs pa dang / skyed rdzogs kyi rtogs pa mnga' ba/
mngon shes mang du gsungs pa sogs don du gnyeer na rnam thar che chung dang/ gtsug lag bzhengs tshul rten bshad du gsol/ de ltar slob ma mang du smin grol la bkod/ 'gro
don rgya cher mdzad de dgung lo drug bcu rtsa bzhi bzhes pa sa pho rta'i lo'i nya drug zla ba'i tshes bcu bco brgyad la bya yul du thegs/ de nas gzhi byes kyi grwa pa mangs/
sku gdung bzhu ba dang bzhugs pa la ma 'tsham pas/ sku stod rdo rus kyi dpang khebs kyis dril nas/ sku smad zhugs phul bas spur dud kyis gar khyab tu ring srel 'byung
ba dang / dung g.yas 'khyil/ sgrol dkar/ rnam rgyal mchod rten rnams byon no/ sprul sku chen po la slob ma nyis stong re 'dus pa'i nang nas/ ting nge 'dzin skyes pa lnga
brgya/ dge bshes jag tse 'cha' ba brgya dang bcu/ de'i nang nas grags che ba phyi'i chen po brgyad/ nang gi chen po brgyad/ thugs kyi sras bzhi rje sgam po par grags pa
dwags po lha rje la sogs pa byon/ phyi'i chen po brgyad ni/ mdo smad nas ngang tshang ba chen po/ brag dmar ba chen po/ dwags por sha pa gling pa chen po/ lhor lha rgya
ri ba dang/ dge g.ye ba chen po/ stod lungs su gnam par ba dang/ nya ga mo pa chen po dkon mchog 'od zer/ gtsang du mu sman pa chen po dang brgyad do/ nang gi chen po brgyad
la/ khrom gzher chen po 'brug lo pa/ mtshan rin chen 'od/ skam skam/ bar bar sogs dgon pa mang du

btab/ don gcig bzhugs/ smyug rum pa chen po ni/ snga phyi gnyis byung ba'i phyi ma yin no/ mal gror brul ba chen po ni/ rus glog skya/ dgung snying yos/ mtshan dbang phyug
rgyal mtshan dbang phyug rin chen yang zer/bya yul ba chen po dang thog mar 'brom du mjal/ rgyal steng gi dgon pa btab/ don drug bzhugs/ sku jol ba chen po/ ba ngar ba chen
pos ba ngar gyi mchod khang bzhengs/ 'phan yul du rta pa zhang sgom chen pos rta phu'i dgon pa btab/ 'brom du bkra shis sgang pa chen pos smon grong gi dgon pa btab/ rgya
mig mangs pa chen po dang brgyad do/ thugs kyi sras bzhi'am lnga ni/ rgya chen pos rgya sa sgang gi mchod khang gsar rnying gnyis bzhengs/ 'phan yul phyar rje nas gnubs
mchod gnas/ dgon mkha' ru ba la gsum byon pa'i bar pa dang/ gtsang pa rin po che dang bzhi/ sras lngar byed na dgyer sgom chen po yin la/ dpe kha gcig tu nang gi chen
por drangs pa yang snang bas/ mi 'dra ba cung zad 'dug kyang rnam thar gtso bor byas so/ dgas dwags po lha rje ni/ snying rje pad dkar du/ dge slong 'tsho byed ces bya ba
theg chen pa 'byung zhes lung bstan te/ 'khrungs yul gnya' bod snyi/ rus snyi ba/ dbu gtso rgyal 'bar gyi sras su sa mo lug la 'khrungs/ dgung lo nyer drug la daDa dwags
por mar yul blo ldan dang/ sha pa gling pa la mkhan slob zhus nas chig rdzogs mdzad/ mtshan bsod nams rin chen du btags/ de nas bya yul ba/ rgya yon bdagsha pa gling pa
yang zer// dge bshes sgre pa/ smyug rum pa  rgya lcags ri gong kha ba dang lnga la bka' gdams kyi chos rnams cha tshang bar gsan/ de nas sgrub pa bya dgongs nas/ khong rang
gi yab mes kyis brtsigs pa'i gser kha bya ba'i gtsug lag khang yod par brang khang brtsigs/

pha zhing la yon bdag byas te sgrub pa byed pa'i dus nyin gcig lcags ri'i lho phyogs su skyo sangs la byon pa na/ sprang po gsum las rje btsun mi la'i snyan pa gsan pas dad
pa'i rkyen byas te pha zhing gser zho bzhi dang/ ja zho gang la btsongs nas/ rgya lcags ri ba dang/ bya yul ba/ smyug rum pa rnams la phyi phyag mdzad pas/ bya yul ba'i
zhal nas/ khyed rnal 'byor pa khyi thul can gyi spyan sngar ma 'gro/ cis kyang 'gro na nged kyi rtags rnam thar ma dor bar shog cig/ lar ser kha la phan na khyi tshil yang
sman yin/ zangs nged kyis brdungs nas za pa skad mis 'don pa gcig 'ong bar 'dug ste thabs med gsung/ smyug rum pa'i zhal nas/ khyod kyis nga rgas kar ma bor bar shog cig
gsung/ de nas mi la dang mjal/ gdams ngag gis thugs tshim par mdzad/ phrin las mtha' yas shing/ dgas dwags lha sgam po btab te rang lo bdun bcu rtsa lnga pa chu mo bya
la sku gshegs/ rgyas par ni bka' brgyud kyi rnam thar rnams su gsal lo/ 'di dag bka' gdams kyi brgyud pa dngos su mi 'dzin kyang/ bka' phyag chu bo gnyis 'dres su grags pas/
slob ma'i mchog tu bgrangs ya yin no/ de nas lo bya yul gyi gdan sa rin par byon pa'i tshul ni/ spyan snga rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug smyug rum du thegs nas/ lor gnas
brtan gyi bu gzhon nu smon lam gyis gdan sa lo dgu/ de nas rtogs ldan sdings po ba gnubs chos 'bar sbrul pos gdan sa lo gsum/ de nas gnas brtan smon lam blo gros kyis zla
ba bcu bco brgyad byas/ yang sdings po bas lo drug dril bas lo dgu mdzad de/ bdun bcu rtsa brgyad la lor thegs/ de nas

gtsang pa rin po che byon nas gdan sa mdzad de/ bya yul du sprul sku chen po thegs nas/ dge bshes rgya spre'u lo pa gdan sa lo lnga mdzad/ drug bcu rtsa bzhi pa rta'i zla ba'i
nyer brgyad la bya yul du thegs/ de nas gnubs mchod gnas gzhon nu rgyal mtshan khyi lo pa/ gdan sa lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi mdzad/ klung shod khra ba kha'i dgon ba btab/
brgyad bcu rtsa drug pa mngon bar byang chub pa'i zla ba'i nyer brgyad la bya yul du thegs/ de nas lo brgyad gdan sa ba med pa'i rjes la/ lor gtsang pa rin po che'i rjes
la/ rin po che glang lung pa bzhugs pa/ mal gro mdar ston mo'i gral dbu nas bya yul du gdan drangs/ de nas lo bya yul gyi gdan sa sbrel ba'i srol byung ngo / gtsang pa rin
po che ni/ 'khrungs yul gtsang gi gnubs yul rong/ gdung rus gnubs/ yab gnubs a la la/ yum ral rgyags bza' lcam gyi sras su me pho 'brug la 'khrungs/ mtshan nam mkha' rdo
rjer btags/ dpe kha gcig tu rdo rje rgyal mtshan yang zer/ rten tshangs spyod kyi dge bsnyen mdzad/ gzhon nu'i dus nas chos thams cad rmi lam sgyu mi'i nyams dang / mkha'
'gro ma mang po'i zhal gzigs/ de nas gnyan lo tsA ba rgya gar nas byon pa dang mjal te/ mdo sngags kyi thos pa rgya chen dang/ khyad par sngags la mkhas par sbyangs/ bod
kyi mkhas pa mang po la ngas thug da rgya gar du 'gro dgongs te/ ding rir dam pa mjal du byon pas/ chos mi gsung bar brda chos bzhi mdzad pa'i gcig/ rdo dkar po shar phyogs
su 'phangs song ba dam pa kun dga' la dris pas/ khyod kyi yongs 'dzin shar na yod zer ba'i brda yin zer bas/ lha sar jo bo mjal ba dang/ yer par sgrub

pa la byon pas/ bya yul ba chen po 'brom smon grong du chos bar la byon pa'i chos nyan mang po dang phrad de sprul sku bya yul ba la chos nyan du 'gro zer/ de la yon tan ci
yod byas pas/ gzhan mi shes bla mas byin gyis brlabs pa gcig yin par 'dug zer/ khong gis kyang tshod blta ba'i phyir chos grwa'i mthar bzhugs pas/ sems la phan pa mang du
byung ste/ mjal nas mi phyed pa'i dad pa 'khrungs/ phyags phyir bya yul du byon nas/ lo bcu bzhi bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos thams cad rdzogs par gsan yi dam mang po'i zhal
gzigs/ chos nyid kyi bden pa mngon sum du gzigs te/ phyis lor byon pa la/ mkha' 'gro ma dung phreng can mang pos bsu ba mdzad de/ rdo rje gdan gyi chos skyong dang gcig
par snang gsung/ dgung lo re gcig la dga' ldan du 'byon pa'i rnal lam byung bas/ sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub pa mdzad/ lo'i gdan sar lo bcu bco lnga bzhugs te/ brgyad bcu
rtsa lnga pa lcags 'brug zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad la lor thegs/ 'di la slob ma dge bshes 'gar la sogs pa bu bzhi dang/ tshe blos thengs pa sdings po ba sogs bcu bzhi
byon te ma spros so/ de'i slob ma rin po che glang lung pa ni/ 'khrungs yul stod lungs nga tshur yab rdo rje grags dang/ yum hor bza' mgon mo'i sras su chu yos la 'khrungs/
lo bcu dgu la pa tshab lo tsA ba la rab tu byung ste/ mtshan brtson 'grus gzhon nur btags/ zur chos pa gcig la 'dul ba mkhas par bslabs/ nya ga mo pa la lo bdun lam
rim tshar gcig tu basbyangs pas/ ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du blo bkol du btub pa byung gsung/ nyer bdun pa la

snon gyi gyad par bya 'dul 'dzin/ phya pa chos seng/ btsun pa chos mchog gsum la bsnyen par rdzogs/ de nas lor gtsang pa rin po che lo lnga bsten te chos mang du gsan/ dad
gus tshad med pa 'khrungs pas/ rtogs pa 'khrungs tshul sogs mang du 'byung la/ sngon du lo'i gdan sa lo bcu gnyis dang/ de nas lo bya yul sbrel nas lo drug ste bcu bco brgyad
mdzad/ bdun bcu rtsa lnga la nya drug zla ba'i tshes brgyad la bya yul du thegs/ glang lung pa'i dus su chos rje 'jig rten mgon po bya yul du byon te/ khrom gzhor dang
gnyis la bka' gdams kyi chos gsan pa'i dus su/ de gnyis kyi slob ma skyo rin po che la nged dben gnas byed pa'i sa cig dgos gsungs pas/ gzho'i phu na 'bri phyugs 'jog
pa'i se nags yod pa phul/ dgon pa btab ste phrin las rgyas pa'i tshul gzhan du gsal lo/ glang lung pa'i rjes su se rnal 'byor pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de ni 'khrungs yul
gzhung/ yab se shes rdor dang/ yum rje mo 'od zer gyi sras su 'khrungs/ glang lung pa'i phyags phyir yun ring du bzhugs/ bla mchod pa lo 'ga' dang/ lo bya yul gyi gdan
sa lo dgu mdzad nas/ khrog gi dbyi phu dgon pa btab po/ sangs rgyas sgom pa ni/ 'khrungs yul gzhung/ yab 'be spyan ras gzigs dang/ yum byi za rgyas chung gi sras su lcags
'brug la 'khrungs/ lo bcu bzhi la 'dul ba 'dzin pa sbal ti'i sar rab byung mdzad/ mtshan rdo rje gzhon nur btags/ de nas lo brgyad pa la glang lung pa stod lungs su byon
pa dang mjal/ lo bcu bzhi bsten rtogs pa khyad par can 'khrungs/ de nas la mo lha khang

du lo drug sku mtshams mdzad/ so brgyad pa la ra mo cher mkhan po sbal ti la bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ 'dul ba mkhas par bslab/ lor byon nas/ zhe bzhi la lo bya yul gyi gdan sar
byon/ glang lo bar bdun bcu bzhugs/ zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bzhi la lor thegs/ de nas gtsang pa jo sras kyis lo dgu gdan sa mdzad/ lo'i dbu rtse gsar ma bzhengs/ zem rin po
che ni/ yul ham mdo'i de'u gong bya bar phag lo la/ yab pa yags rtse mo'i sras su 'khrungs/ lo bcu bdun pa la lor sangs rgyas sgom pa'i spyan sngar byon pas/ sngon la dro
par song gsung nas rnal 'byor byang seng la rab byung zhus/ mtshan grags pa seng ger btags/ 'dul ba dang/ jo bo nas brgyud pa'i chos mang du gsan/ lo lnga bzhugs/ yar
lam rin chen sgang du sangs rgyas dbon la chos zhus/ de nas ham mdor lo bzhi sgrub pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas padma gar dbang dang zhal mjal/ de nas lo bya yul du sangs rgyas
sgom pa la tshogs chos/ klog chos thams cad rdzogs par mdzad/ thugs dam bum pa dbu thog tu gzhag pas ting nge 'dzin khyad par can 'khrungs/ ra sgreng du byon dus jo bo
'jam dpal rdo rjes chos gsungs/ lo bya yul gyi gdan sa lo bcu bco brgyad mdzad/ drug bcu rtsa drug pa 'brug lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes nyi shu la glang lung du thegs/ 'di
la slob ma'i mchog bzang po drug tu grags pa'i re mer ba chen pos lho ri mer gyi dgon pa btab/ 'od gsal sgang pa ni/ 'khrungs yul 'on bra ma thang/ don stengs pa la rab
byung zhus/ dro sar rnal 'byor bya seng la 'dul ba sogs bslabs/ phar 'byon par chas pa la/ snya re sman rtsar zem phebs pa dang mjal bas/ mi phyed

pa'i dad pa skyes/ lo dgu bsten/ 'dis zhogs kyi 'od gsal dgon pa btab so bo / gzhan yang dum bu ri pa chen po'i dbon po zla ba grags pa/ smad kyi byang chub sems dpa' zla ba
rgyal mtshan/ 'dis dum ri'i dgon pa btab  dgas dwags po spyi ther ba/ 'bri sgangs sangs rgyas lha ston pa/ chos rgyal kham pa lung pa rnams byon/ kham pa lung pa ni/ 'khrungs
yul nyan ka ka pa/ gdung rus dbas/ yab rnal 'byor mgon po'i sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/ byis pa nas zem rin po che lor yar 'byon mar 'byon mdzad pa dang mjal res
kyis sems phrogs pa bzhin byung/ lo bcu gnyis la zem bya yul du bzhugs pa la rab byung zhus/ mtshan rin chen seng ger btags/ de nas phyags phyir lo bdun bzhugs/ tshogs chos
rnams rdzogs par gsan/ zem gyi zhal nas khyed nga'i yon tan 'di rnams rtsad chod/ bsnyen rdzogs gyis gsung bas/ zem lam dgon du phebs pa la skyor mo lung gi mkhan po
zhig po bya ba mjal du byon dus bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ 'dul ba yang gsan/ de nas zem la klog chos rnams zhus ma 'ongs pa na 'di ltar gyis kyi bslab bya mang po rnams mdzad
de/ zem gshegs nas/ ri mer ba gdan sar spyan drangs kyang/ khyod rang gi pha gi na 'os pa cig chos skyong gis bdag tu bzung 'dug gsung nas/ lung bstan mdzad de sa byon/ khong
yung ba'i khams lung du bros te de nas spyan drangs pas/ mtshan kyang de ltar grags/ nyi shu rtsa lnga pa la gdan sar bskos/ lo nyi shu rtsa bdun mdzad/ lo'i mchod khang
gi khyams smad gling rgya bkyed pa/ gser thog sogs bka' drin che zhing/ lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa rta lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer lnga la ka phug tu thegs/ yar lungs jo bo'i
chos 'byung du 'di'i dus su bka'

gdams kyi bshes gnyen grags che ba thus chen brgyad du grags pa byung zer ro/ sangs rgyas jo bo ni/ 'khrungs yul rgya sa sgang/ yab lha'i brgyud pa jo bo bsod nams mgon gyi
sras su sbrul lo 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nas sangs rgyas sgom pa shar phyogs dang ba'i 'od kyi 'jig rten na bzhugs zer ba'i dbyangs 'then pa gsan pas/ mtshan thos pa tsam gyis
dad gus skyes/ lo bcu gnyis la zem glang lung du bzhugs pa la rab byung zhus/ mtshan dbang phyug gzhon nur btags/ nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa la zem la mkhan po zhus te bsnyen
par rdzogs/ bka' gdams kyi chos la sogs pa mang du gsan sbyong mdzad/ lnga bcu rtsa gnyis la lam dgon gyi gdan sar byon/ lo dgu mdzad/ drug bcu la lo bya yul gyi gdan sar
byon pa'i dus mngon shes mang du gsungs/ bya yul gyi gtsug lag khang dang/ gling gi zhig gsos sogs mdzad de/ bka' drin lhag par che zhing/ bla ma yi dam chos skyong mang
po zhal gzigs/ gdan sa lo bcu bco brgyad mdzad/ bdun bcu don gsum pa bya lo dbyug gu zla ba'i tshes bcu bar du bzhugs/ sangs rgyas ston pa ni/ 'khrungs yul lho brag gla
shul sgo/ yab sum pa bkra shis kyi sras su byi ba lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu bzhi la khams pa lung pa'i drung du rab byung zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims seng ger btags/ nyi shu
la mkhan po dge ye ba la bsnyen par rdzogs/ 'dul ba mkhas par mkhyen/ de nas lo bya yul gyi chos skyong rnams kyis bsu ba byas pa'i snang ba dang dus mtshungs par sangs
rgyas jo bos shog gsung ste/ bya yul steng khang du bskos/ jo bo chen po zhal gzigs/ de nas gdan sar byon te lo bcu drug mdzad/ lo bya yul du chos khrims shin du dam pa dang

bka' gdams kyi srol bzang po gtsugs/ glang lo bar drug bcu rtsa gnyis bzhugs/ sangs rgyas sgom pa gsar ma ni/ 'khrungs yul lo ro gla shul/ yab sum pa brgyad stong dpal gyi
sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/ gzhon nu'i dus mtsho sna pa la dge tshul zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims shes rab tu btags/ de nas bya yul du byon nas sangs rgyas jo bo dang/ ston
pa la bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ bka' gdams kyi chos rdzogs par gsan/ khyad par du sangs rgyas ston pa la sngags kyi rdzogs rim gsan pas/ 'od gsal gyi rtogs pa 'khrungs/ de nas
lam dgon gyi gdan sa lo gsum mdzad dus/ thugs skyo ba cung zad skyes te sham po gangs la bzhugs pa/ lo bya yul gyi gdan sar spyan drangs/ lo bcu gsum gdan sa mdzad/ nga
lnga pa stag lo bre phul zla ba'i tshes bzhi la bya yul du thegs/ sangs rgyas dbon po gzhon nu smon lam/ dgas dwags por spre'u lo la 'khrungs/ dgas dwags po spyi ther gyi
dbon por grags/ rgyal steng gi gdan sa lo mang rab dang/ de nas gdan sa gong lo gsum mdzad/ bdun bcu rtsa gnyis pa lug lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad la lor thegs/ rin
po che bcu bzhi pa/ klungs shod sho nag thang bya bar yab seng ge'i sras su yos la 'khrungs/ gdung rus rtsi/ lo bcu bco lnga la lug rgyur sangs rgyas jo bo la rab tu byung/
mtshan tshul khrims mgon por btags/ lo bzhi bsten/ tshogs chos rdzogs par gsan/ bcu dgu la brag gsab tu bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ de nas skyor mo lung dang/ thang sag tu
'dul ba dang dbu ma mkhas par sbyangs/ sangs rgyas ston pa lo bcu gnyis bsten/ lkog chos rdzogs par gsan/ yi dam zhal gzigs pa

mngon shes mnga' ba sogs rnam thar du gsal/ 'khor rnams la nged yan chad du bka' brgyud 'di la dam tshig dang lta spyod la lhad dang zel med/ byin brlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams/
nyams rtogs rgyun chad med pa yin pas/ khyed zhabs tog byed pa don dang ldan pa yin gsung/ bya yul gyi mkhan po lo gsum/ lam dgon gyi gdan sa lo brgyad/ gdan sa che
ba lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis mdzad de/ bdun bcu rtsa gcig pa glang lo zla ba dgu pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la lor thegs/ 'di stod lungs pa rin chen snying po'i sprul par grags so/
rin po che gnam gang pa/ 'khrungs yul 'ol kha ba/ gdung rus byen/ yab chos skyong bsam me'i sras su khyi lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu gcig pa la rgyal stengs su sangs rgyas dbon
po la rab tu byung/ mtshan gzhon nu ye shes su btags/ mkhen phya ru ba la/ 'dul ba/ spyod 'jug/ gdams ngag skor mang du gsan/ bcu dgu la rin po che tshul khrims mgon po
la bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ nged kyi gzims g.yog gyis zin bris thob gsung bas/ de ltar mdzad de tshogs lkog gi chos rdzogs par gsan pas thugs rab la mnyes te/ blo gros rnam
dag ces gsung/ lo nyer drug la rgyal stengs su bskos te lo bcu bco lnga gdan sa mdzad/ de nas rin po che bcu bzhi pas/ thub pa'i gser sku dbu zhwa/ bstan rim sogs gnang nas
byin gyis brlabs/ bzhi bcu pa la gdan sar byon/ lo so bzhi mdzad/ don gsum pa khyi lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i gnam gang bar du bzhugs/ rin po che tshes bcu pa/ 'khrungs
yul 'ol kha ba/ gdung rus ljang/ yab dpon dkar gyi sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu bzhi la rin po che bcu bzhi pa

la rab byung zhus mtshan chos kyi rdo rjer btags/ nyer gcig la rin po che sa de nyid kyi drung du bya yul du bsnyen rdzogs mdzad de/ dal dang 'byor pa rnyed dka' bas/ 'di dag
ji lta bzhin du bsgrubs/ gsung ba'i skabs su thugs la nges shes skyes te/ tshul khrims mi 'bras bzhin du bsrungs gsung/ bcu bzhi pa lo dgu bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos rdzogs
par gsan/ gsang sngags nod do/ 'dul mngon spyod 'jug sogs la mkhas par sbyangs/ byes kyi mkhan po lo gsum/ rgyal stengs su lo nyi shu rtsa brgyad/ gdan sa gong lo brgyad/
spyan g.yas su mkhan po gzhon nu dpal gyis gdan drangs nas chos kyi 'khor lo yun ring du bskor/ bde mchog sogs zhal gzigs/ mgon po lho nub pa bran bzhin du 'khol ba
sogs rnam thar du gsal/ bdun bcu rtsa gsum pa 'brug gi dgun zla tha chung gi tshes bcu bar du bzhugs/ rin po che bcu bcu brgyad pa/ dgung snying yos/ zhogs su 'khrungs/
rin po che gnam gang ba la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ mtshan blo gros rin chen du btags/ 'od gsal gyi gdan sa lo bdun/ gdan sa gong lo brgyad mdzad do/ bzhi bcu rtsa
drug pa byi ba lo dpyid zla ra ba'i tshes bcu bco brgyad bar du bzhugs/ rin po che rin chen rgyal mtshan/ yab lhas pa dpon rdor gyi sras su gru bzhir byi ba lo la 'khrungs/
rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs rin po che gnam gang ba la zhus/ mgon po gri gug zhal gzigs rje rin po che blo bzang grags pa sogs bla ma bcu bco lnga bsten/ gdan sa lo nyi
shu rtsa gsum mdzad/ lnga bcu rtsa dgu pa khyi lo zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu bco lnga bar du bzhugs/ yongs 'dzin chen po tshul khrims dar gyi zhal snga nas yab dpon bsam

grub dar/ yum sog mo rdo rje sgron gyi sras su shing pho stag la lcas par 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gsum la gug rdzong du slob dpon tshul rgyal ba la rab tu byung/ mtshan tshul
khrims dar du btags/ nyi shu rtsa lnga la rin po che chos kyi rdo rje'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs/ skyur mo lung du slob dpon bsam gtan don grub dang/ dro sar dmar ston
dbu ma pa sogs la 'dul ba'i sde snod mtha' dag la mkhas par sbyangs/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal ba dang/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa sogs las/ sher phyogs dang byams
chos mtha' dag thugs su chud par mdzad/ thang sag tu zla grags gsar ma dang/ slob dpon tshul dpal pa la dbu ma'i gzhung che chung mtha' dag gsan/ rin po che rin chen rgyal
mtshan pa sogs bla ma lnga'i drung du bka' gdams kyi chos skor rnams dang/ chos rje kun bkras pa sogs la/ sa lugs kyi chos skor dang/ zha lu grags pa rgyal mtshan pa la
bu lugs kyi chos skor dang/ gdan sa thel du chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la phyag rgya ba'i chos skor dang/ rtogs ldan sngo nyal ma dang/ drung rin rgyal ba la dus
'khor rgyud 'grel sogs la mkhas par mdzad/ mdor na mkhas grub kyi bla ma sum bcu tsam bsten te/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag gi tshig don la mnga' brnyes par
mdzad de/ mkhas pa'i grags pas phyogs kun du khyab/ 'chad nyan sogs gzhan phan rgya cher mdzad de/ slob ma'i mchog chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ bzad pa blo rgyam/ bzad pa
padma bzang po/ chos rje blo brtan pa/ khams su lha 'bri ston pa sogs mang du byon/ sher phyogs gsung ba'i tshe me tog gi char 'bab pa yi dam dang chos

skyong zhal gzigs pa sogs rgyas par rnam thar du gsal la/ lor byes pa mkhan po lo lnga/ gzims 'og lo gsum/ gdan sa gong lo bcu bdun mdzad/ bdun bcu don lnga pa 'brug lo zla
ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer drug bar du bzhugs/ 'dir smras pa/ nges 'byung tshul khrims gsum gyis bag yod phyug/ rab 'byam sde snod gsum la mkhyen pa rgyas/ 'chad rtsod rtsom
pa gsum la mnga' brnyes pa'i/ bla ma mchog la sgo gsum gus pas 'dud/ de nas bdag gis gdan sa lo sum bcu so dgu byas te/ chos kyi 'brel pa thob pa bcu phrag gnyis/ bka' drin
lhag par che ba'i bla ma bdun/ mdo rgyud gzhung 'grel man ngag mang du thos/ yongs 'dzin chen pos mnyes shing rjes su gzung/ bka' brgyud bla ma'i rnam thar dri med mtsho/
bshes gnyen gdengs can stong gis legs gtams pa/ yon tan yid bzhin nor bu'i 'byung gnas la/ ngoms par btung du yod pa skal ba bzang/ zhes bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad
pa'o/ gong du smos pa stod lungs pa'i slob ma lam grags che ba/ sdings po ba/ glog skya/ dge bshes zar pa/ dge bshes lha bzo/ khyung kham/ bya 'dul 'dzin dang drug las/ dang
po gsum gong du zur tsam bshad la/ stod lungs pa'i dgongs pa lon pa phyi ma gsum yin te/ lha bzos mngon shes lnga thob/ stod lungs pa 'khor lo bde mchog dang gnyis su
med par gzigs gsung/ khyung kham gyis sgyu lus kyi rtogs pa brnyes/ stod lungs pa'i zhal nas/ khyod kyi gdul bya gtsang du yod pas der song/ dgon pa thob/ slob ma bsdus
la bden gnyis bshad do/ nga'i bden gnyis 'di ma dor cig gsung bas/

khyuung kham gtsang la 'byon khar/ bden gnyis dang khyung kham gtsang la bzhud/ bden nam mi bden/ pha bong 'phen/ g.yag la dris gsung nas/ phyag mkhar brdabs pas tshal par
gas/ de nas nyang ro tha ba tshal du byon nas/ sdings phu dgon pa'i rmang bting/ bden gnyis chos tshan bcu gnyis su bsdus pa gsungs/ gzhan phan bskyangs pas slob ma mang
du 'phel lo/ bya 'dul 'dzin ni/ 'khrungs yul gtsang rong g.yung gi nang gi gnya' pa/ yab bya rgyal ba la sras gnyis yod pa'i gcung po/ lcags pho 'brug la 'khrungs/ gzhon
nu'i dus rong snar mda' tshe dmar gyi gtsug lag khang du 'be shes rab 'bar chos gzhi la byon pa mjal du byon pas/ phar phyin gsung ba'i lam shes kyi skabs su slob chos gsan
pas lha'i me tog char 'bab pa mthong/ dad pa skyes pas/ yab la zhus te rab tu byung/ mtshan brtson 'grus 'bar du btags/ 'be'i zhal nas/ rab tu byung bas 'dul ba bslab
dgos pas/ thog mar 'dul ba slobs gsung bas/ ldan du sog tshul khrims bla ma/ de nas rgya 'dul 'dzin dang/ rma tsho la 'dul ba gsan cing mkhas par gyur/ de nas rgyal tsha
zhang yes la dbu tshad dang/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba la yo ga bslabs/ de nas bshad nyan mdzad pa'i skabs su dpe cha rnams khams pa'i grwa pas brkus pa/ thugs skyo ba skyes te/
stod lungs pa'idrung du bka' gdams zhu ru byon pa/ yon tan che ba'i nga rgyal gyis dang por phyag ma byas pa sogs spyod pa 'ga' zhig la brten nas stod lungs pas bka' bkyon
drag tu mdzad de bskrad/ der log nas byon/ stod lungs zam khar sleb pa na 'gyod pa skyes te

chos zhur 'ongs pa la/ de ltar byed pa nga ma bden snyam du dgongs pa dang/ stod lungs pa'i zhal nas/ nye gnas la da kho 'gyod pa skyes nas 'dug gi yar gdan drongs la shog
gsung/ gdan drangs bkur sti byas/ der bka' gdams kyi gdam ngag thams cad yongs su rdzogs par gsan nas thugs dam gyi gtso bo mdzad do/ de nas zul phur bshad grwa gtsugs btsugs
te tshogs lo dgu'i bar du bskyangs/ mdo rtsa'i TikkA che chung dang/ 'dul ba spyi'i rnam gzhag mdzad/ de'i tshe bsam yas dpe dkar gyis bar chad brtsom rtsom pa'i phyir
btsun par sprul nas zhabs tog lo mang du byas kyang 'dul ba dang 'gal ba'i mdzad pa na bza'i spu phyir bstan te gyon pa tsam ma gtogs skyon ma rnyed pas/ dpe dkar yang
dad par grags so/ de ltar bka' gdams kyi man ngag la nyams len mdzad/ bu chen 'dul ba la mkhas shing 'gro don phun sum tshogs pa bdun bcu rtsa drug byung ba'i nang nas/
dbus kyi bu chen gsum ni/ ga ba dar song/ rnal 'byor byang seng / rje ma chos seng dang gsum/ gtsang nas gtsang ngu rin rgyal/ rtsis pa gzhon nu seng ge sogs byon/ de ltar
bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen mdzad de/ dgung lo bdun bcu don lnga bzhes pa na/ zul phur sku gshegs/ lung bzhu bas thugs ljags ring srel sogs mang du byon no/ de nas dgyer
sgom chen po nas brgyud pa cung zad bshad na/ dang po yar lungs 'phyong rgyas kyi bang so padma can bya bar/ yon bdag nyi ma mgon gyi sras dgyer shes rab skyabs zer ba
dbu ru snon mda'i reg snar yul 'chugs/ btsun mo 'tshal stod nas klu lcam

bya ba khab tu bzhes/ sras gsum byung ba/ khye'u la stag/ bu mo stag/ khye'u la dor ro/ chung ba khye'u la dor rab tu byung ste sgom pa shes rab grags zer/ che ba khye'u la
stag dgung lo bcu gnyis pa snon phu gnyer du sprul sku bya yul bas mkhan po mdzad/ rnam thar gzhan na mkhan slob gsal ba mi snang/ zhang snying phug pas slob dpon mdzad
nas rab tu byung ste/ mtshan gzhon nu grags su btags/ dgung lo bcu bdun la sne'u zur du byon/ lo dgu bzhugs/ sne'u zur pa gshegs nas bya yul ba chen po lo lnga bsten/ bka'
gdams kyi chos skor rdzogs par zhus/ slob ma brgyad brgya tsam byon pa'i nang nas grags che ba nya/ bya/ zug dang gsum/ dge bshes g.yor ston/ skyi ston/ lho brag ston pa/
dmar ston/ khams ston/ ston pa 'od zer sla ma/ smon lam bzang po/ ston pa gzhon legs sogs byon zer ba 'dug kyang/ sa cha 'di dang/ dgon pa 'di btab sogs gsal ka ma thos
la/ sangs rgyas dbon ston ni 'gran gyi do med yin no/ me mo bya la ra sgreng btab nas lo drug bcu re gnyis song ba/ sa mo phag la rin chen sgang dang gtsug lag khang rnying
ma bzhengs/ bla ma'i gdan sa la sgo ston gsung nas bya yul phyogs su bstan/ jo bo mi g.yo ba/ dam tshigs gsum bkod/ jo bo 'jam dpal rdo rje'i zhal gzigs/ sne'u zur pa
dang bya yul ba'i gsung sgros dgang gsos nas lam rim po ti bzhi ma dang gnyis ma bya ba sangs rgyas dbon ston sogs la gnang bas/ sangs rgyas dbon ston gyi zin bris su btab/
gdan sar lo lnga bcu bzhugs/ khya gnyis pa yos lo'i dgun zla ra ba'i nyer dgu la thegs/ sangs rgyas dbon ni/ dgyer sgom chen po'i mched zla dgyer bu mo stag ces pa dang
/

yum sha mo stog go zhes pa la sras lcam sring gsum byung ba'i che ba yon bdag ya po zhes pa/ dge 'dun dang dkon mchog la dad pa zhig byung/ bar pa sangs rgyas dbon/ lca mo
rgya mo hor dang gsum mo/ sangs rgyas dbon sprul sku bya yul ba'i sku skyer byed pas/ dgyer sgom gyi zhal nas/ ngas bla ma'i gsung cig la brten nas/ btsun chung 'di la byams
par byas pa yin gsung/ sangs rgyas dbon dgung lo bcu bdun la dge bshes 'ben thang pas mkhan po/ dwags po bang rim pa lde'u sgom gyis slob dpon mdzad de rab tu byung/
mtshan gzhon nu 'byung gnas su btags/ lo bcu dgu la skyid smad du byon/ dge bshes nyang ran dang/ dge bshes kha ches mkhan slob mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ 'phan yul mdar
ka ba dar seng la 'dul ba dang/ gzhan yang sde snod mang du gsan/ de nas lo bcu bco brgyad kyi ring la dgyer sgom chen po bsten nas/ gsung rab mtha' dag dang/ lung man ngag
rdzogs par gsan/ yi dam chos skyong dpag tu med pa zhal gzigs/ rgya mar gtsug lag khang gsar ma bzhengs pa dang/ rin chen sgang gi gling rgya bkyed pa/ phyogs kyi gtsug
lag khang dang rten gsum mang po'i rab tu gnas pa sogs 'gro don rgya che zhing/ sangs rgyas skal ldan shing rta zhes par 'gyur bar zhal gyis bzhes/ spyan ras gzigs kyi
sprul par yang grags/ rgyas par don du gnyer na khu dbon gyi rnam thar thun mong ba che ba gcig dang/ mchod khang bzhengs tshul bkra shis le'u brgyad ma bya ba lho pa dbu
ma pa nam mkha' shes rab zer ba'i slob ma cig gis byas pa dang/ ri bo maNDal gyi rtser byon pa'i rnam thar rnams su gsal lo/ slob ma rtogs ldan bzang

mo ba/ hags mo ba/ zung chung mo pa/ nag mo sang yon dang mo bzhir grags pa rnams ni rgyas par khong rang gi bka' thor bkod 'dug pa rnams yin la/ gdan sar lo bzhi bcu bzhugs
te bdun bcu rtsa gsum pa lcags pho rta'i mgo'i zla ba'i tshes bzhi la rgya ma gnas su thegs/ rtogs ldan bzang mo ba ni/ yul dwags po brad lha sa ba/ gdung rus spyil/ yab
rnal 'byor jo stag la sras gsum yod pa'i 'bring po/ mtshan gzhon nu seng ge zer/ byis pa'i dus dwags po sgom tshul la phyag rgya ba'i khrid 'ga' dang/ bya yul ba'i slob
ma bong thang ba la bka' gdams kyi chos skor dang/ pu gu dor sa chen gyi slob ma gshen pa rdo rje seng ge la sa skya pa'i chos skor gsan/ bcu dgu pa la g.ye chung du zhang
ban la bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ de nas sangs rgyas dbon blo mda' grong mo che na slob ma mang po la bka' gdams kyi chos skor gsung ba dang mjal bas dad de/ nyi shu rtsa brgyad
nas rin chen sgang pa'i grwa pa mdzad yun ring du bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos rdzogs par gsan/ de nas bsam yas phu'i bzang mo dgon par bzhugs pas bzang mo bar grags/
bdun bcu rtsa bdun pa shing pho rta'i lo'i dpyid 'bring mchus nya pa'i tshes bzhi la bzang lo dgon par thegs/ khong gi slob ma jo gdan lhas phu bas lhas phu dgon gsar btab/
lha dge 'dun sgang pas dge 'dun sgang btab/ gzhan yang 'phan yul zong dgon pa sogs byung yang grags che ba lha 'phrang po ba yin te khong gis sbrags su ri zangs rtog gi
dgon pa btab/ nags mo bas byin gyi nags mo dgon pa btab/ zung chu mo pas 'phan yul mda'i zung chur

dgon pa btab ste/ phyis spos pa grab kyi gsas khang yin no/ sangs rgyas dbon gyi brgyud pa gdan sar byon pa rnams ni/ gcen po yon bdag ya po la sras bzhi byung ba'i che ba
slob dpon ston pa/ bla ma sang yon/ smon lam seng ge/ bde gshegs chen po'o/ bla ma sang yon glang lo pa po gcig pa lug gi lo la gdan sar byon/ mchod khang glo 'bur nub ma
dang gdul gdung sogs bzhengs/ sprul bsgyur nus pas nyin gcig la sprul pa gsum bstan par grags/ gdan sa lo sum bcu rtsa gnyis mdzad/ re gnyis pa stag lo'i bar bzhugs/ de
nas gcung po bde gshegs gzhon nu seng ge khyi lo pa/ zhe gcig pa stag gi lo la gdan sar byon/ lo nyi shu rtsa lnga mdzad/ re lnga pa stag lo la thegs/ de nas smon lam seng
ge'i sras skam dgon pa gzhon nu 'bum gyis gdan sa zla ba bcu bco brgyad mdzad de/ rang lo nga gcig pa la thegs/ de nas sangs rgyas 'od 'byung gis gdan sar 'brug la byon
te lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi mdzad/ gtsug lag khang la gser thog bkal/ rang lo drug bcu rtsa gcig la thegs/ de nas sangs rgyas gzhon 'od kyis rang lo nyer bzhi pa la gdan sar
byon te lo bzhi bcu bzhugs/ lo drug bcu rtsa bzhi pa la thegs/ de nas mkhas btsun rgya ma pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyis rang lo zhe gsum pa la gdan sar byon te lo bcu dgu
bzhugs nas drug bcu rtsa gnyis la thegs/ slob dpon kun bzang dang/ slob dpon gzhon nu seng ge gnyis kyi skabs gdan sa lo drug stongs nas skag rtsub mang yang khong rang
rnam gnyis kyis gdan sa lo gnyis gnyis mdzad/ de nas spyan snga bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis gdan sa

lo nyi shu rtsa lnga mdzad/ spyan snga sang yon pas gdan sa lo bdun mdzad nas lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa la thegs/ sangs rgyas byang chub pas gdan sa lo nyi shu rtsa gsum mdzad
de nga drug pa la thegs/ spyan snga kun blo bas gdan sa lo bcu gcig bskyangs te lnga bcu rtsa dgu pa la thegs/ spyan snga gzhon 'od pas gdan sa lo sum bcu rtsa bzhi mdzad/
mchod rten chen mo bzhengs/ re drug pa khyi la gshegs/ spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan skam dgon pas gdan sar lo gnyiis bzhugs nas kun spangs mdzad de don gcig pa la thegs/
spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan gnyis pas gdan sa lo gsum mdzad nas bdun bcu rtsa gnyis pa la thegs/ spyan snga blo gros 'jigs med pa shing phag la gdan sar byon te
da lta gdan sar bzhugs pa nyid do/ gong du smos pa sne'u zur pa las 'phros tshul ni/ sne'u zur pa gdung rus zhang tshe spong/ spras thong pa sar zhang stag po'i sras su
chu pho rta la 'khrungs/ byis pa'i dus nas ting nge 'dzin rang 'khrungs su mnga'/ brag rgyab tu rab tu byung/ mtshan ye shes 'bar du btags/ dgon pa la/ sku mched gsum la
sogs pa bla ma mang du bsten/ dgon pa ba dang thog mar mjal ba'i dus/ thugs ka nas thub pa'i sku 'od 'phroo ba cig byon nas sne'u zur pa la thim pas ting nge 'dzin khyad
par can brnyes/ bla ma la gus pa/ byang chub kyi sems gnas pa/ brtan pa/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin rnams 'dzom na/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dpag tu med
pa zhal gzigs pa chos nyid yin gsung/ gzhan yang sgyu lus kyi rtogs pa brnyes pas/ rang lus mi g.yo ba'i skur ldang nus pa dang /

mngon par shes pa rgya chen po mnga' zhing/ dgon pa ba dang/ sku mched gsum gyi gsung phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i bstan rim mdzad/ rang lo bdun bcu rtsa bdun pa sa khyi rta'i
zla ba'i nyer dgu la thegs/ gdung bzhu bas ring bsrel dpag tu med pa dang/ lha'i spos kyi dri sne'u zur gyi gnas thams cad khyab pa sogs rnam thar du gsal lo/ slob ma
bdun brgya tsam byung ba'i nang nas grags che ba bzhi ni/ lha bka' gdams pa thag ma ba chen po/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ gun pa lha rje thugs rje rgyal mtshan rnams
dang/ gzhan yang dgyer sgom chen po/ gtsang nas grang po lung pa zhes 'phags pa don zhags dang bcu gcig zhal gyi chos bdag tu byed pa dang/ spyi bo lhas pa byang chub 'od
ces grags pa rnams so/ 'di rnams bka' gdams gdam ngag pa gtso bor byed pa yin no/ spyi bo lhas pa la chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi tas rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyi slob dpon
zhus/ bka' gdams gzhung gdam ngag gi chos rnams gsan par rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba las gsungs so/ thag ma ba'i slob ma nam mkha' seng ge yang stod lungs thag mar byon/
de nas nam mkha' rgyal po/ seng ge bzang po/ rgyal sras bzang po/ gsang ba'i bdag pos byin gyis brlabs pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dang bzhi ni lho brag thig phyir byon
no/ yang bka' gdams gzhung pa'i brgyud pa se spyil phu ba yan sngar bzhin la/ de nas lha lung gi dbang phyug dang/ lha 'gro mgon gyi slob zangs chen pa dar ma bsod nams/
de'i slob ma mtsho sna pa chen po shes rab bzang po/ de'i slob ma mon grab pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ de'i slob ma mkhen chos skyab bzang po yang gdam ngag

pa nas brgyud pa sangs rgyas dbon ston yan sngar bzhin la/ de nas nam mkha' rgyal po man sngar dang 'dra'o/ mkhan chen chos skyabs bzang po dang/ gsang bdag nam mkha' rgyal
mtshan gyi drung du rje thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang grags pas bka' gdams gzhung gdam ngag gi chos rnams gsan nas/ gro lung pa'i bstan rim la gzhi mdzad de/ byang chub
lam sgron gyi don 'grel lam rim che chung mdzad do/ de yang bka' gdams gzhung gdam ngag gi khyad par mi 'dra ba cung zad 'dug kyang bka' gdams gzhung drug sogs gzhung bshad
gtso bor byed cing/ skyes bu gsum gyi lam rim lkog chos su ston pa gzhung pa dang lam bstan rim sogs skyes bu gsum gyi gdam ngag gtso bor ston cing/ gzhung rgyab chos
su byed pa gdam ngag par byed pa legs so/ a ti sha'i sras kyi thu bo gnyis pa rngog lo tsA ba'i bshad brgyud 'dzin pa ni/ gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bstan pa spyi la bka'
drin che bas/ de'i byon tshul sngon gyi yi ge las/ kha ba can gyi ljongs 'brog mtsho dang nye ba'i sar/ sngags rnying ma ba'i dge bshes rdo rje gzhon nu bya ba la sras lnga
yod pa'i che shos rngog legs pa'i shes rab kyis/ spyir jo bo chen po lo bcu bsten cing/ phyags phyir byon pa'i dus su gsang phu la phyag 'dzub gtsugs btsugs te/ lung pa
ya ge'i nang na dung g.yas su 'khyil ba 'dra ba yod/ der legs she khyod kyis gtsug lag khang thob la bshad nyan gyis/ bstan pa la phan par 'gyur zhes lung bstan pas/ gsang
phu ne'u thog gi sa cha gzigs te/ bla mas lung bstan pa'i gnas de yin par mkhyen nas/ gsang phu ne'u thog gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ bstan pa'i
