bya ba mdzad de/ dang por dge 'dun lnga brgya tsam 'dus so/ de las 'phros pa la gnyis/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab las slob ma 'phros tshul/ mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan
las bka' gdams glegs bam byung tshul lo/ dang po ni/ legs she'i gcung po klu khri/ klu byang/ chos skyabs/ thub pa bzhi las/ chos skyabs kyi sras lo tsA ba blo ldan shes
rab yin te/ de yang lcags mo phag gi lo la sku 'khrungs/ skyes bu dam pa des sku na gzhon nu'i dus nas/ khu bo dang/ ka chu'i slob chung tshul khrims shes rab la sogs
pa bsten nas rab tu byung / rgyud sbyangs/ dgung lo bcu bdun lon pa'i dus/ mnga' ris stod kyi lha bla ma byang chub 'od kyi dbon po mnga' bdag rtse lhes ldes rgya gar du
lo tsA slob pa la brdzangs te/ yul dbus dang kha che la sogs par byon/ paNDi ta sadzdza na dang/ 'bum phrag gsum pa/ pa ra he da/ ma hA dza na/ su ma ti kIrtI dang/ skal
ldan rgyal po la sogs pa mkhas grub mang du bsten/ rgya bal du lo bcu bdun bzhugs nas/ mnga' ris stod du phebs/ mnga' bdag dbang lde dang/ khri bkra shis dbang phyug brtsan
btsan gyis 'gyur gyi sbyin bdag mdzad nas/ tshad ma rgyan la sogs pa bstan bcos mang po bsgyur/ de nas dbus su phebs/ khu bo'i gdan sa gsung phu ne'u thog dang/ ra sgreng
la sogs pa gnas khyad par can mang por chos gsungs/ slob ma khri phrag lhag tsam 'dus par grags shing/ dbus gtsang/ lho bal/ mdo stod smad/ shar tsong kha/ rgya mi nyag
sogs su grub mtha' 'dzin pa'i slob ma dang nying slob tu ma gyur pa med cing/ dbus gtsang du lo bcu

bdun 'gro don mdzad/ rgyas par gro lung pas mdzad pa'i rnam thar du shes so/ de'i thugs sras zhang tshes spong chos kyi bla ma/ gro lung pa blo gros 'byung gnas/ khyung rin
chen grags/ 'be shes rab 'bar dang bzhi la sras kyi thu bo bzhi zer/ gzhan yang gangs pa she'u/ gong bu ra can/ sham po mi dig la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin par
mdzad pa'i ngang nas zhang tshes spong chos kyi bla mas ne'u thog gi gdan sa lo sum bcu rtsa gnyis mdzad/ de rjes gnyal pa ri lus lo gnyis/ gnam par bas lo brgyad/ de nas
gro lung pa gdan sar gdan drangs pas/ grogs chos kyi spyan ldan de'i gdan sa dron mo la shes 'dod yod kyang ral ril thams cad kyi rjes su mi byed gsung nas/ gong gi bla
ma de gsum gyi slob ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen phya pa chos kyi seng ges ne'u thog gi gdan sa lo bcu bco brgyad mdzad cing/ slar yang gro lung pa'i spyan sngar byon nas sgro
'dogs dpyad de slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon pa las sras kyi thu bo seng chen brgyad ni/ gtsang nag brtson 'grus seng ge/ dan bag smra ba'i seng ge/ bru nag bsod nams
seng ge/ rma bya rtsod pa'i seng ge/ rtsags dbang phyug seng ge/ nya bran pa chos kyi seng ge/ 'dan ma dkon mchog seng ge/ gnyal pa yon tan seng ge ste/ 'ga' zhig gtsang
pa 'jam seng 'dren no/ jo sras bzhi ni/ 'khon jo sras rtse mo/ rngog jo sras ra mo/ khu jo sras ne tso/ gnyos jo sras dpal le rnams so/ yang 'gar dbang phyug grub/ kong
po 'jag chung/ lho pa sgog zan/ par phu ba blo gros seng ge bzhi la shes rab can bzhi zer/ gzhan yang 'jad pa ston skyabs/ rdo rje 'od zer la sogs pa sde snod

'dzin pa mang po dang/ 'tshur phu ba grub thob dbu se/ zhang tshal pa/ choos rje phag mo gru pa la sogs pa mkhas grub du ma smin par mdzad pa'i nang nas rtsags dbang phyug
seng ges gdan sa lo lnga de gnyis kyi slob ma gnyal pa dad pa bzang pos lo bdun/ 'jam tse nes lo bdun byas/ 'di nas gling stod smad gnyis su gyes par 'dod do/ smad pa la
bzad pa dar ma 'od dang/ bzad pa don grub gnyis kyis lo sum bcu mdzad/ de nas slob dpon 'od zer mgon pos lo sum bcu rtsa lnga gdan sa mdzad pa la/ slob ma slob dpon shAka
gzhon/ don grub dpal/ mkha' rag pa la sogs pa byon pa'i shAka gzhon gyis gdan sa mdzad de/ de nas rim pa ltar byon no/ gling stod pa ni/ 'jam tse ne'i slob ma gtsang pa
'jam seng/ de'i rjes su 'jim ston/ zhu ston/ blo gros 'bar rnams rim par byon/ de nas slob dpon gnyal zhig 'on byang rdo nas spyan drangs te/ gdan sa lo bcu bco brgyad mdzad
cing/ slob ma bu dgur grags pa ni/ bzad rings/ phu dang dar dkon/ gtsang pa gru gu rnams la snga tshar gsum/ 'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge/ bo dong rin chen seng ge/ slob
dpon jo nam gsum la bar tshar gsum/ rgya 'ching/ 'jam gsar/ skyel nag gsum la phyi tshar gsum zer ro/ de ltar slob ma mang yang / gdan sa rgyal pa so ston gyis byas/ de
nas rgya 'ching rgyu ba bde ba can nas spyan drangs te gdan sa mdzad/ de nas chu mig pa seng ge dpal gyis gdan sa lo bcu bco brgyad mdzad/ de nas da lta'i bar la gdan sa
ma chad par byon pa'o/ lo tsA ba'i bu chen khyung rin chen grags kyi slob ma stod lungs rgya dmar/ stag pa kha che sogs las brgyud pa nyang stod

gnas gsar la sogs pa'o/ 'be shes rab 'bar gyis nyang stod gnas rnying du phar phyin gyi gra grwa sa gtsugs btsugs te/ la stod dkon mchog mkhar la sogs pa smin par mdzad do/
ar byang chub ye shes kyis gnam rtsang ldeng dang gzhu kun dga' rab sogs su chos gsungs te/ gra grwa pa dpe 'grems dus gcig la'ang brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ grags che ba dkar
chung ring mo sogs mang du byon no/ gzhan yang gnyal zhig gi slob ma las brgyud pa'i sa skya/ zha lu/ snar thang sogs gtsang gi chos sde grags che ba rnams su mtshan
nyid kyi bshad grwa btsugs te/ mdor na rngog lo tsA ba khu dpon nas brgyud pa rnams a ti sha'i slob brgyud kyi mchog tu gtogs shing/ bstan pa spyi la bka' drin che bas zur
tsam smos pa'o/ gnyis pa mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan las glegs bam byung tshul ni/ rngog legs pa'i shes rab de nyid la gsang phur gra grwa pa lnga brgya tsam 'dus
te gzhan phan skyong ba'i dus su/ de rnams kyi nang nas rnam g.yeng la mi dga' zhing/ 'dod yon la ched du mi byed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' shes rab rgyal zhes pa/ mnga'
ris stod pa/ jo bo dang 'brom gnyis ka la chos kyang thos pa cig yod pa de 'du 'tshogsmi 'ong bar gsang phu'i nags khrod cig na sgom 'ba' zhig mdzad cing bzhugs pa la/
de dus rngog gsang phu bas nag gseb na yar la skyo sangs la byon pa na/ byang chub sems dpa' shes rab rgyal mtshan dang mjal nas/ rngog la phyag 'tshal ba dang/ rngog na
re/ khyed bza' btung longs spyod la mi lta ba ngo mtshar che/ dus deng sang rnam g.yeng spangs nas 'di lta bu'i dge sbyor byed pa la dka' las yod/ khyed thugs dam gyi mthil
ci la mdzad gsungs pas/ shes rab rgyal mtshan na re/ yongs 'dzin dam pa gsan du gsol/ 'dus byas chos ni 'di 'dra ba/ skyes pa'i tha ma 'chi

ba'i chos/ bsags pa'i tha ma 'dzad pa las/ tshe 'di'i snang ba bag re la/ rgyu mtshan ci yang mi gda' ba/ de bas mi rtag thun re bsgoms/ gsungs pas/ rngog dgongs pa la 'di
jo bo yab sras kyi chos skad thun mong ma yin pa yin/ 'di la dge sbyor gyi khrigs dang/ dad gus ci 'dug blta snyam nas/ dri lan mang du mdzad pas/ bka' gdams glegs bam rngog
gi phyag tu bzhugs pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis rtsad chod de zhus pas/ thog mar bu chos kyi le'u dang po bram ze'i khye'u gsal bar sku skye ba bzhes tshul sogs gsungs/
mdor na tshig re re la'ang bslab pa gsum/ lha bzhi/ rjes dran lnga tshang ba re mdzad de/ bslab pa gsum yang tshul khrims bsrung ba dang/ gzhan don du bsam pa bzang po
byed pa/ de thams cad bden gnyis su dril nas nyams su len pa dang/ lha bzhi ni rab tu byung ba'i cha nas shAkya thub pa'i bka' thams cad la babs/ tshad med pa bzhi la dge
sbyor byed pa'i cha nas thugs rje chen po/ 'gro don byed pa'i cha nas rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ gnyen po bsten pa'i cha nas mi g.yo ba dang/ rjes dran lnga ni/ lhag par sgrol
ma 'di skad gsung/ sras kyi thu bo spyan ras gzigs/ khyod kyi rjes 'brang kho mos bskyab/ kho mo'i gdams pa 'di long la/ rjes su 'brang la bstan par bya/ skyabs gnas
bla ma dran par mdzod/ lus ni lha yi rang bzhin te/ ngag ni bzlas brjod rgyun par mdzod/ 'gro ba ma lus pha mar soms/ sems kyi gnas lugs stong par dpyod/ lnga po de yi skyabs
par nas/ dge rtsa thams cad dag par mdzod/ ces te/ 'di rnams kyi nang du nyams len 'du bar bzhed cing/ bka'i babs che chung gang zag blo mtho dman gyi rim pas

'byed tshul glegs bam las gsungs pa rnams bstan nas/ de nas rjes su glegs bam gyi po ti tshang ba bka' rgya dang bcas te gnang/ shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis kyang gnas nges med
du bzhugs nas nyams len mdzad do/ de nas spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa phu chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan la gnang/ des ka ma'i rnal 'byor pa rin chen rgyal mtshan la/
des stabs ka'i zhang ston dar ma rgyal mtshan la/ des lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyi sku skye byang chub bzang po la/ des nam mkha' rin chen la/ des 'brom ku mA ra ma ti la/
des mkhen nyi ma rgyal mtshan la gnang/ de dag gi lo brgyus rgyus rgyas par don du gnyer na glegs bam gyi byung tshul ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i dpal 'byor zhes par blta'o/
zhar la khu ston brtson 'grus g.yung drung ni/ yar lungs thang po cher byon/ spyir jo bo'i chos mang du mnga'/ khyad par shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa la rtsal thon/
gshin rje gshed kyi zhal gzigs/ slob ma'i mchog mngon pa la mkhas pa brang ti dar ma snying po sogs dang/ glegs bam las/ bA ga rA jA la sogs pa'i 'khor lnga brgya tsam
yod ces 'byung ngo/ gsum pa nag tsho'ii rjes slob byon tshul ni/ nag tsho lo tsA ba la mnga' ris skor gsum du slob ma mang du byon pa la/ dbus su grags che ba rong pa
phyag sor ba yin te/ khong rang gi skye ba bcu gsum dran cing/ mngon par shes pa rgya chen po mnga' ba/ bsgoms pa'i stobs kyis rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas pa des/ dang por
jo bo chen po'i gdam ngag kho na rtsad dpyod pa la/ jo bo'i dngos kyi slob ma yer pa ba rang gi zhang btsun yer pa ba / yer pa gzims khang gi sgom pa dad pa bla ma/ ra
sgreng du dge bshes ston pa/ rnal 'byor pa chen po

dpal ldan dgon pa ba/ mkha' ru ba snga ma/ lo tsA ba nag tsho/ jo bo legs dang brgyad/ nying slob mkha' ru ba phyi ma/ dge bshes yung ba pa dang bcu bsten nas/ bshad pa dang
sgrub pa'i gdams pa dang/ jo bo'i lo brgyus rgyus rtsad dpyad pas/ jo bo dngos kyi slob ma rnams gsung mthun par byung/ nying slob gnyis gsung ma mthun te khyad par du
bstan rim gyi mtshan 'dogs lugs la/ mkha' ru ba phyi ma'i zhal nas bstan pa'i srol kha bya ba yin gsung/ yung ba pa'i zhal nas/ khyod kyi slob dpon blo brtul bas ma zin par
snang/ bla ma rnams bstan pa'i rim pa zhes gsung ba yin/ de yang/ tshul gnas thos dang bsam ldan pas/ sgom pa la ni rab tu sbyar/ bya ba'i don yin gsung/ de nas rong pa
phyag sor ba'i thugs dgongs la/ jo bo dngos la lo bcu dgu bsten pa'i lo tsA ba chen po de/ da dung mnga' ris gung thang na bzhugs yod par 'dug pas/ jo bo dngos su bzhugs
kyang lo tsA ba bar du 'jug dgos pas/ de rang la cig gtug dgos dgongs nas/ mang yul du byon pas/ lo tsA ba chen po de gung thang yang thog gi gtsug lag khang du bzhugs
pa'i drung du byon nas/ dang por gasngags kyi gdams pa chang chung mang du zhus nas bag phab/ de nas phyi de lo la pha rol du phyin pa'i sgrub pa'i gdams pa dang/ jo bo chen
po'i sku che ba'i yon tan dang/ bod du spyan drangs lugs gsung ba'i zhu ba phul bas/ lo tsA ba'i zhal nas/ de la nga mkhas pa yin/ lo bcu dgu bsten bod du ngas spyan
drangs pas/ jo bo'i lo brgyus rgyus la shin du mkhas pa yin te/ khyod min pa rtsad dpyod pa rang yang ma byung gsung nas/ lo brgyus rgyus chen mo lam yig de'i dus su gsungs/
sgrub

pa'i gdams ngag kyang ma lus par gnang ste/ nyin re la chos thun gsum gsum gsungs/ theg pa chen po sngags kyi sgor yang bcug ste/ dbyar re la sngags kyi glegs bam drug bcu
tsam thon par byas te/ lo gsum bzhugs/ bstan rim gyi mtshan 'dogs lugs kyang yung ba pa'i gsung bzhin du 'dug gsung/ de nas mar la 'byon khar/ khyod kyi sgrub pa'i gnas 'di
lta bu gcig tu bsgrubs shig 'phag pa spyan ras gzigs zhal mthong bar 'gyur ro zhes lag sor dgon pa'i lung bstan yang mdzad/ de nas mar la skyel thung mdzad de/ 'gro chos
cig zhus pas/ gung thang pa'i zhal nas/ dal 'byor rten gyi shes rab can/ tshe 'di ji ltar byas kyang phyid/ bla med byang chub rnyed dka' bas/ 'bad pa chen po bya 'tshal
lo/ zhes pa la brten nas chos thun gcig gsungs/ der theg pa chen po mtha' dag gi chos ma lus pa 'dus pa yin gsung/ de nas mar byon phod mdo bas sba len bzang du byas te/
bstan pa la phan pa'i chos cig zhu zer bas/ mdo rtsa dang/ bslab pa kun las btus pa gnyis gsungs/ de nas thams cad lings kyis bskyur nas bla mas lung bstan pa'i gnas lag
por dgon par bzhugs te/ nye gnas dang yang mi mjal bar gsol ba bug sgo la blangs te/ sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pas/ loo gsum na thugs rje chen po'i zhal mthong/ lung
bstan te/ khyod kyis tshe 'di nyid du mthong lam thob nas/ slob ma yang sum bcus zhal mthong bar 'gyur gsung/ de nas lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi song ba'i dus rnal lam du mkhro
ma mang po byung nas/ jo bo'i ring srel ma sba bar ston zer nas/ ring srel sder gang gtad pa lho phyogs su gtor ba zhig rmis/ phyis

rong pa'i bu bzhir grags pa lhor 'byung ba la blta bar 'dug gsungs/ de nas pa tshab dang/ 'phrang kha rje'i 'khrug pa'i mdus mdzad pa la/ phod mdor byon pa dang/ rma chen po
byang rdor zer ba 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po de dang mjal bas/ khong dad nas skyid shod 'on ljang rdor spyan drangs te chos gtsugs pas/ de'i dus rma chen po'i zur chos pa
che ba bzhis chos zhus pas/ rong pa'i bu bzhir grags pa ni/ bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ rog 'ching phu ba gnam par ba dge bshes zhu lhan pa'o/ rgya ra ston rjid dge bsnyen yin
pas bur ma bgrangs/ de lngas jo bo'i gdams pa zhus/ zin bris mdzad pas/ bya 'dul ba 'dzin pas gdams pa dang lo brgyus rgyus nyung 'dus gcig mdzad/ 'ching phu bas lo brgyus
rgyus nyung 'dus la gdams pa mang ba gcig byas/ gnam par bas lo brgyus rgyus ma bris par gdam ngag rnams bris/ zhu ldan pas gdams pa dang lo brgyus rgyus gnyis ka rgyas
par byas nas khyad par du lo brgyus rgyus zhib par mdzad de/ mdo sde rnams las sangs rgyas kyis yul 'dir gang zag 'di la chos 'di gsungs bya ba yod pas chos khungs btsun
par rtogs pa la lo brgyus rgyus 'di gal che ba yin gsung nas rgyas par bris/ yi ge de thams cad bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa'i phyag tu byung bas/ khong gis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs
pas jo bo'i lam yig tu grags/ rgya ra ston brjid la sngags kyi gdams pa gtso bor gnang/ 'dis rgya ra'i dgon pa btab/ gzhan yang ba yu ba shes rab tshul khrims kyis phyags
sor ba yun ring du bsten jo bo nas brgyud pa'i chos skor dang/ khyad par spyan ras gzigs kyi gdam ngag thams cad ma lus par gnang/ lung bstan nas thugs rje chen po bsgrubs
pas/ lo lnga na zhal mthong/ theg pa

chen po sbyor lam gyi rtogs pa brnyes pa yin gsung/ ba yu nA 'phags pa lce sgom shes rab rdo rje dang/ mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gnyis la gsungs/ de gnyis tshogs lam
chen po ba yin gsung/ lce sgom gyis thog mar brag lha dgu phug tu lo brgyad sgrub pa mdzad pas 'phags pa'i zhal dngos su mthong ngo/ bla ma mnga' ris pa la rgyu mtshams
kyi brag phug tu bsgrubs/ zhal mthong bar 'gyur gsung nas lung bstan te bsgrubs pas lo bzhi na zhal mthong/ dus rgyun du mi ma yin gyis 'tsho ba drangs gsung/ de gnyis
ka la grub thob skyer sgang pas zhus te/ lo phyed dang bzhi bsgrubs pas zhal mthong nas/ snyigs ma'i dus su zhal mthong gi brgyud pa mang du 'byung gsung lung bstan mdzad
de/ slob ma'ang lnga bcus zhal mthong ngo/ des sangs rgyas gnyan ston la gsungs te/ skyer sgang du dbyar dgun bcu gsum bzhugs/ gdams ngag chig brgyud thams cad ma lus par
gnang nas/ lo gsum bsgrubs pas phyag bzhi pa kha sarpa Ni bcu gcig zhal phyag stong spyan stong rnams zhal mthong / slob ma bcu gcig gis zhal mthong ba'i lung bstan mdzad
pa bzhin byung gsung / de nas da lta yang rgyud pa ma chad par bzhugs pa dang/ gzhan yang nag tsho nas brgyud pa'i chos skor gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad brgyud ye shes rdo
rje kun las btus la brten pa'i man ngag la sogs pa 'ga' re gnang ngo / 'dir smras pa/ rnam dpyod sha ba ri'i cod pan las/ kun khyab lha yi lam las 'phags/ blo gsal skye
bo'i snang byed du/ rnam thar nyin byed 'od stong shar/ don gnyer rkang drug ldan pa'i tshogs/ dga' dang spro ba'i 'dab gshog can/ dad pa'i ser bus bskyod bzhin du/ legs
bshad padmo

'di la rol/ drug pa de rnams kyis bstan bcos ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni rgyal bas gdul bya'i bsam pa dang rjes su mthun par/ mdo rgyud kyi gsung rab mtha' yas pa zhig bka'
bstsal ba dang/ de'i dgongs pa gsal bar mdzad pa'i shing rta chen po rnams kyis bstan bcos rtsod bral du ma zhig mdzad pa de thamasacad bka' gdams rin po che'i khungs su
gtogs pa'i gzhung yin la/ de rnams kyi nang nas bslab spyod gnyis/ sa rgyan gnyis/ skyes tshoms gnyis dang drug la bka' gdams gzhung drug ces gsung ba'i don yang/ zab mo
lta ba'i brgyud kyi gzhung bsam gyis mi khyab kyang/ don bslab spyod gnyis su 'du ba dang/ rgya chen spyod pa'i brgyud kyi gzhung bsam gyis mi khyab kyang/ don sa rgyan
gnyis su 'du ba dang/ skyes rabs kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi sngon gyi mdzad pa las brtsams te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa pha rol du phyin pa drug dbye ba dang bcas pa'i
don nyams su len tshul gsungs pa dang/ ched du brjod pa'i tshoms dgra bcom pa chos skyabs kyis mdzadapa/ brjod bya sna tshogs pa tshoms su bsdus nas gsungs pas/ chos spyi
la gal che bar dgongs te gzhung drug tu mdzad do/ bshes gnyen gong ma rnams 'dul spyod gnyis sheszhes / 'dul bas lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa dang / spyod 'jug gis
byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa gsum la slob pa/ zab lam rdo rje theg pa'i rten du yang nges par dgos pa la dgongs so/ gzhan yang jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsar grags pa'am/
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gtso bor ston pas spyod phyogs brgya rtsa zhes pa la/ thog mar dkon mchog rjes su dran pa mchod brjod kyi tshul gyis bstod pa'i

skor la/ dkon mchog gsum rjes su dran pa'i mdo/ lha las phul du byung bar bstod pa/ bde byeed bdag pos mdzad pa/ bshags pa'i bstod pa tsantra go mis mdzad pa/ yon tan mtha'
yas par bstod pa dkon mchog 'bangs kyis mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa dang/ don bsdu ba'i tshigs bcad phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa dang drug/ skyabs 'gro'i skor la/ skyabs gsum
bdun bcu pa zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ skyabs 'gro drug bcu pa bi ma la mi dras mdzad pa/ skyabs 'gro bstan pa/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa dang gsum/ byang chub mchog tu sems
bskyed pa'i cho ga la/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon byang bzang gis mdzad pa/ dzai tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa/ sems skyed pa'i cho ga dang/
bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa gnyis jo bos mdzad pa/ sdom pa nyi shu pa tsantra go mis mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa zhi ba mtshos mdzad pa dang bdun noo/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod
pa'i skor la/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma/ de'i rang 'grel dang/ spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma bsdus don sgron me/ dbu ma'i man ngag/snying po bsdu ba/ snying po nges
par bsdu ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa nor bu'i phreng ba/ 'di bka' gdams glegs bam gyi rtsa tshigs yin no/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdo tsam gdam ngag tu brjod
pa/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs yi ger bsdus pa/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs shin du bsdus pa/ rang gi bya ba'i rim pa bskul ma dang bcas pa yi ger
bris pa/ mdo sde'i don kun las btus pa'i man ngag kluu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i mdo kun las btus pa'i don bsdus pa/ mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa/ las rnam par

'byed pa/ kha ton dang glegs bam klog pa'i sngon du bya ba'i cho ga/ pha rol du phyin pa'i tsha tsha gdab pa'i cho ga/ byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa'i lam la 'jug pa/
de ltar bcu dgu jo bo chen pos mdzad/ 'phags pa rtogs pa chen po yongs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde'i sdig pa bshags pa dang/ sgrub pa mdo de nyid las phyung ba/ las dang po pa'i
sa sbyang ba/ dgra las rnam rgyal gsang bas mdzad pa/ de bzhin bshegs pa'i yi ge brgya pa'i sgo nas sdig pa bshags pa/ zhi ba lhas mdzad pa dang/ nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ sgom
rim dang bsam gtan gyi yi ge sna tshogs la/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba dang/ de'i rnam par bshad pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ sgom rim gsum dang/ rnal 'byor
sgom pa la 'jug pa/ ka ma la shI las mdzad pa/ don dam byang chub sems bsgom pa rin po che'i sgron me dang/ kun rdzob byang chub sems bsgom pa padma spungs pa gnyis/ slob
dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs kyi le'u slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ yang ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bsam
gtan gyi chos drug rnam par gzhag pa/ a ba dhU ti pas mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa dA na shI las mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor rtog pa'i gegs sel ba sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/
rnal 'byor gyi mtshan nyid kyi bden pa/ slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ dbu ma'i man ngag rin chen za ma tog kha phye ba dang/ bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa dang/ dran
pa gcig pa'i man ngag gnyis/ mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor sgom pa'i lam ye shes snying pos mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor la 'jug pa phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad
pa/ mi sdug pa bsgom pa'i lam dge ba'i go chas mdzad pa/ lus yongs su

dpyad pa'i sgom rim nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ sems can mgu bar bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa/ theg chen nyi shu pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ pha rol du phyin pa'i theg pa'i rim
pa'i man ngag dpal ye shes grags pas mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med pa'i mdo sde'i rjes su 'gro ba/ ma hA ma tis mdzad pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin
pa'i man ngag rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag/ chos kyi dbang pos mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sgom pa'i don bsdus te bstan
pa/ ye shes zla bas mdzad pa dang nyi shu rtsa bdun/ gsang sngags kyi lam rim la/ yi ge drug pa'i glu/ spyod pa'i glu/ de'i 'grel pa/ 'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung ba'i
glu/ chos kyi glu/ ting nge 'dzin gyi glu/ rdo rje gdan gyi glu/ de'i 'grel pa chos kyi dbyings su lta ba'i glu/ ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs kyi le'u/ 'jig rten las 'das
pa'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga/ rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga dang bcu gcig jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ bde ba bcu gsum pa'i glu/ atShis mdzad pa/ man ngag bdud rtsi'i 'khor lo/ phyag
na rdo rjes bsdus pa/ byang chub sems kyi rnam par bshad pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ maNDal gyi cho ga dgra las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ maNDal gyi cho ga sangs
rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ maNDal gyi cho ga rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ maNDal gyi cho ga ka ma la shI las mdzad pa/ maNDal gyi cho ga rnyoog med rdo rjes mdzad pa dang
bcu dgu/ gtam du bya ba sna tshogs la/ rmi lam yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam/ klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ yon tan bdun rab tu brjod pa'i

gtam/ dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ sbyin pa'i gtam/ slob dpon gu Na pra bha bas mdzad pa/ tshul khrims kyi gtam/ tshod zin pa'i gtam/ tshogs kyi gtam dang gsum dbyig gnyen gyis
mdzad pa/ mi khoms pa brgyad kyi gtam/ rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ legs bshad za ma tog lta bu'i gtam/ slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa/ phyin ci log bzhi spang ba'i gtam dang/
rtsod pa'i dus kyi gtam/ ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa/ dben pa'i gtam/ sa 'tsho sbyin gyis mdzad pa dang bcu gcig go spring yig gi skor la/ bshes pa'i spring yig klu sgrub
kyis mdzad pa/ slob ma la spring ba tsanDa go mis mdzad pa/ rgyal po ka ni ka la spring ba/ ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa/ rab gsal gzhon nu la spring ba/ 'phags pa spyan ras
gzigs kyis mdzad pa/ sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i phrin yig/ dzai ta ris mdzad pa/ dri ma med pa rin po che'i spring yig/ rgyal po nai ya pA la la gdams pa dang/
pu rangs jo bo la spring yig sum bcu pa/ jo bos mdzad pa dang bdun dran pa nyer gzhag gi tshig le'ur byas pa dang/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa/ chos ldan rab 'byor
dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ yang mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa dang/ mya ngan bsal ba/ rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga'i nyes dmigs bshad pa/ dbyig gnyen
gyis mdzad pa dang lnga ste/ bcu gnyis su bzhed do/ rtogs brjod la/ gzhon nu ma bdun gyi rtogs pa brjod pa/ gsang bas byin gyis mdzad pa gcig/ lugs kyi bstan bcos la/
shes rab brgya pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ dri med dris lan Rin po che'i phreng ba don

yod 'char gyis mdzad pa dang gnyis/ sngo ba dang smon lam la/ yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga tshigs su bcad pa nyi shu pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ smon lam bdun bcu pa/
gzhan la phan pa'i dbyangs dgon pa bas mdzad pa dang gnyis so/ mdor na glegs bam gcig la chos tshan brgya dang bcu gnyis bzhugs so/ gzhan yang jo bo chen pos mdzad pa la/
byang chub ltung bshags kyi 'grel pa/ dam tshig bsdus pa zhes pa rtsa ltung gi bshad pa/ gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs dang/ bstod pa/ 'jam dpal
rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang phyug lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs dang/ 'jig rten dbang phyug dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten
dbang phyug gi gtor chog rgyas pa/ rgyal ba rigs lnga'i bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa/ grub chen mu yi pas mdzad pa'i dpal mngon par rtogs pa'i 'grel pa chen mo/ 'khor
lo sdom pa bcu gsum dang/ lha lnga dang/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs shar phyogs bhaM ga la'i tshal du bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor zhal gzigs pa'i dus su bstod pa/ rdo rje
phag mo'i sgrub thabs che ba rin chen rgyan zhes pa dang/ chung ba gcig/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma zhal gzigs pa'i dus su bstod pa/ yang mkha' spyod ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs
che chung gnyis/ 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ nA ro pa/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje dang gsum snyan nas snyan du brgyud
pa'i man ngag phyogs gcig tu mdzad pa/ sgrol ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal gyi bstod pa/ spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum gyi sgrub thabs/
yi ge drug pa'i man ngag/ spyan ras gzigs

kyi ri mo'i brda bshad pa/ sgrol ma sngon moo'i bstod pa zhal gzigs dus su mdzad pa/ dzam bha la dkar po'i bstod pa/ sman bla gtso 'khor gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag dkar
po'i sgrub thabs che chung gnyis/ mi g.yo ba sngon po'i sgrub thabs/ mgon po gri gug gi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje lcags sgrog gi sgrub thabs/ rta mgrin shwa na bzhi skor lha
lnga'i sgrub thabs dang/ dkyil chog/ jo bo bod du 'byon khar slob ma rnams la spyi chos su gdams pa/ rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu/ gzhan yang lha btsun pa byang chub 'od/
lo chen rin chen bzang po/ 'ol rgod pa ye shes 'bar/ zhang sna chung ston pa rnams la gdams pa dang/ gzhan yang bstan 'gyur gyi tho rnams su jo bo'i mdzad byang 'byar ba
gtsug tor dri med dang/ gdugs dkar sogs kyi rgya gzhung mang du 'dug kyang 'dir ma bkod do/ snye thang du mdzad par grags pa rigs kyi smon lam/ lta sgom spyod gsum gyi glu/
bsam gtan la bskul ba'i glu/ bde ba drug gi glu/ lta spyod zung du 'brel ba'i glu/ dus mchod bzhi'i ngos 'dzin dang phan yon/ bde mchog gi rgyud la brten pa'i rlung gi
man ngag/ gzhan yang stong thun brgyad bcu rtsa gnyis sogs mdzad byang 'byar ba mang du snang zhing phal cher mdzad par mngon te 'dir dpyad pa zhib tu ma byas so/ rtsa ltung
gi 'grel pa sogs kha gcig la yang / jo bos mdzad pa yin min bod snga ma dag dpyad pa mdzad mod 'dir zhib tu ma bris so/ bka' gdams glegs bam du gtogs pa la/ spyir dpe
tshan lnga bcu rtsa bzhi las/ sbyor ba'i chos la dpe tshan bzhi ste/ 'brom chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyis

logs su nan gyis btab pa'i bka' rgya dang/ rang rgyud la bskul ma 'debs pa dad pa'i ljon shing gnyis/ sbyor dngos gnyis kar gal che la/ lo brgyus rgyus ngo mtshar rmad du byung
ba'i dpal 'byor zhes pa glegs bam gyi chos 'byung dang/ rnying snying gi thig le'i gsal byed zung 'jug nyi zla'i thig le gnyis/ snar thang du bkod pa ste/ dpe tshan
bzhi po 'di glegs bam dngos gzhi la mi the'o/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa nor bu'i phreng ba ni/ dngos gzhi pha chos bu chos gnyis ka'i rtsa tshig yin la/ pha chos ni/
bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ zhes pa nas/ mang po'i nang du ngag la brtag/ gcig pur 'dug na sems la brtag/ ces pa'i bar/ le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum du bsdus nas gsungs pa'i
steng du bka' rgya ma/ ma 'ongs lung bstan/ 'chi med rdo rje'i glu'i le'u dang gsum bsnan pas le'u nyi shu rtsa drug dang/ bu chos la/ the tshom thams cad spang bya zhing/
zhes pa las 'phros te/ bram ze'i khye'u gsal ba'i skyes rabs dang/ de nas rim pa bzhin rtsa tshig las brtsams te/ rngog gis zhus pa'i skyes rabs nyi shu la/ rngog chos
nyi shu dang/ khu ston phebs nas zhus pa gnyis la/ khu chos gnyis te/ nyi shu rtsa gnyis bu chos yin la/ kha bskong gi le'u ste bzhi bcu zhe dgu ni/ glegs bam dngos gzhi'o/
rgyal ba yab sras kyi bkod pa phun sum pa'i gter zhes pa/ phyis snar thang du byas pa don bsdu lta bur snang la/ 'di yang dngos gzhi la mi the'o/ gzhan yang lam rim
dang/ gsung sgros thor bu ba dang/ 'phrin yig dang/ man ngag sna tshogs pa'i skor ro/ dang po lam rim la/ spo to ba nas brgyud pa/ spyan snga ba nas brgyud pa/ gsang phu

ba nas brgyud pa'o/ dang po ni/ dol pa'i be'u bum sngon po dang/ de'i 'grel pa lha 'bri sgang pas mdzad pa/ be'u bum khra bo zhes pa/ glang ri thang pa dpon slob dang/ sha
bo sgang pa rnams kyi gsung sgros phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa/ dge bshes grab pas mdzad pa'i dpe chos dang/ brag dkar bas de nyid rgyas su btang ba gnyis la brten nas/ lce
sgom gyis dpe chos rin chen spungs pa rtsa 'grel mdzad pa grags che ba 'di'i zhabs su spros bsdus byas zhes pa grab pas mdzad pa las cung zad spros/ brag dkar bas mdzad pa'i
rgyas pa las/ bsdus shes pa'i don no/ gzhan yang shar ba pas mdzad pa'i lam rim che chung gnyis/ bya mchad kyi gsung sgros thor bu pa rnams dang/ de las brgyud pa blo
sbyong gi yig cha che chung dang/ se spyil ba'i lam sgron sa bcad/ Tikka/ sbas pa ston gzhon gyi lam rim dang/ lam sgron Tikka sogs thor bu ba 'ga' dang/ rnal 'byor byang
seng gi bstan rim legs pa zhig kyang snang ngo/ snar thang pa'i yig cha yod tshul gong du cung zad re smos la/ kha rag skor gsum gyi nang du dpal ldan dgon pa ba'i gsung
sgros bsgrigs pa'i lam rim dang/ gzhan yang gzhung pa nas brgyud pa'i gsung sgros mdzad byang med pa mang du snang ngo/ gnyis pa bshes gnyen spyan snga ba nas brgyud pa
la/ dge bshes ston pa'i gsung/ spyan snga ba/ bya yul ba/ gtsang pa rin po che rnams snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa/ rin po che glang lung pas bsgrigs pa'i lam rim dang/ yang
rnal 'byor pa nas/ stod lungs pa chen po/ dge bshes lha bzo/ nya ga mo pa/ glang lung pa chen po/ glang lung pa nas/ da lta'i bar du rim par brgyud pa'i

bstan rim chen mo la/ rin po che na rim gyi zin bris mdzad byang yod med mang du snang ba/ 'be sangs rgyas sgom pas mdzad pa'i zin bris dang/ rin po che gser khang pa'i zin
bris dang/ rin po che tshul khrims dar gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i bstan rim chen mo nyid mchog yin no/ lam bstan rim gyi khyad par/ bstan rim du gsungs pa ni/ tshogs su
'chad na bstan pa'i rim pa/ nyams len du dril ba lam gyi rim pa/ gzhung du bkod pa byang chub lam gyi sgron ma ste don gcig la ming gsum btags pa dang 'dra gsung ba dang/
thar pa don gnyer gyi gang zag sangs rgyas kyi sar 'gro ba la bstan pa'i chos thams cad lam gyi rim par dril nas nyams su len pas/ lam bstan pa'i rim pa zhes gsungs pa
ltar na/ khyad par cher med kyang cung zad 'byed na/ chos khungs btsun par rtogs pa'i phyir thog mar lo brgyus rgyus dang/ de las brgyud pa rjod byed sde snod gsum dang/
brjod bya bslab pa gsum/ gang zag gcig gi lam du lung rnam dag dang sbyar te 'gal med du ston pa bstan pa'i rim pa dang/ de'i don theg pa chen po'i lam gyi rim par dril
nas ston pa/ lam rim zhes gsungs pa yin no/ yang stod lungs pa nas brgyud pa'i bden gnyis dang/ bden bzhi'i chos skor dang/ chos thun rer nyams len don tshan bzhi bzhir bsdus
pa/ bzhi tshan chos thun bcu dgu/ ja chos chos thun lnga bcu dang/ jo bos mang yul cog ga ri la ljongs rgyu ba'i dus gsungs pa/ ri chos su grags pa dang/ lam sgron la
gong du smos pa'i TIkka dang/ mtshams nam mkha' grags dang/ chu mig pa gnyis kyi TIkka / gzhan yang gsung sgros bkod pa'i TIkka mdzad byang med pa mang du snang

ba ni/ bka' gdams kyi bshes gnyen gong ma rnams bla ma'i gsung la zin bris tsam las mdzad byang mi sbyor ba dang/ slob ma rnams kyis kyang/ bka' 'bum bsgrigs pa sogs cher ma
mdzad cing/ gsung sgros thoor bu ba 'dug pa yang yun ring bas kha mthor ba sogs ma spros so/ gsum pa gsang phu ba nas brgyud pa la/ rngog legs shes mdzad pa'i lam rim sho
lo ka drug dang/ de'i gsal byed blo ldan shes rab kyis mdzad pa shog bu nyi shu tsam dang/ de nyid rgyas par 'chad pa gro lung pas mdzad pa'i bstan rim chen mo nyid yin
no/ gnyis pa gsung sgros thor bu'i skor la/ blo sbyong mtshon cha 'khor lo/ rma bya dug 'joms/ dgyer sgom rdo rje'i glu/ blo sbyong sems pa'i rim pa/ gser gling pas jo
bo la gnang ba'i rtog pa 'bur 'joms rtsa 'grel blo sbyong lhan thabs bzhi pa/ de'i sgo nas sdig pa bshags pa dang/ 'khon sbyang ba'i cho ga/ ku sna li'i tshogs sog gsog 
blo sbyong kun du bzang po/ blo sbyong stan thog gcig ma/ blo sbyong thun brgyad ma/ glang ri thang pa'i tshig rkang brgyad ma/ de'i 'grel pa bya ston gyis mdzad pa/ blo
sbyong rten 'brel snying po dang/ bka' gdams thor bu ba sogs dang/ gzhan yang rgyal po sa'i saM ghas zhus pa'i bod kyi rnam gzhag sogs mang du snang ngo/ gsum pa 'phrin yig
gi skor la/ jo bos mdzad pa gong du bshad la/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos sku mtshams nas grogs po rnams la springs pa/ dge bshes ston pas jo bo spyan 'dren pa'i dus/
mnga' ris nas bod ston rnams la springs pa tshigs su bcad pa bcu dgu pa/ zhang 'phreng kha ber chung la springs pa snga

phyi gnyis/ sgom chen byang chub la springs pa/ bshes gnyen blo gros 'byung gnas la springs pa/ a mes sman rgan sogs la gdams pa'o/ spo to bas rang gi slob ma rnams la spyir
springs pa/ rang gi grogs po dol ba'i bla ma la springs pa/ g.ya' ngos dgon par springs pa/ yung ba'i chang 'thung rnams la springs pa/ bya yul gyi mchod gnas lo chung
la springs pa/ zhogs ya gad du springs pa'i yi ge rnams so/ spyan sngas sne'u zur pa la dang por springs pa/ rjes su springs pa gdam ngag tshig drug ma dang/ dge bshes dbang
seng la springs pa/ bya yul ba nyer gnas mdzad dus gdams zer ba sogs dang/ stabs ka bas mnga' ris rgyal po la springs pa/ mkha' ru bas rngog blo ldan la springs pa/ mchod
gnas dbang nge la springs pa/ sha bo sgang pa la springs pa/ sgom chen seng ge sgra la springs pa sogs shar ba pa'i 'phrin yig sum bcu rtsa bzhi/ gzhan yang dpal ldan
dgon pa ba'i bca' yig/ spo to ba'i bca' yig/ zhang ston shar ba pas snga phyir byas pa gnyis te/ dge 'dun spyi'i bca' yig bzhi'o/ de rnams ni thos zlos tsam min par mthong
ba rnams bkod do/ bzhi pa man ngag gi skor la/ bka' gdams lha bzhir grags pa/ dam tshig gsum bkod kyi rgyud la brten pa thub pa gtso 'khor gsum bsgoms te/ de bzhin bshegs
pa'i yig brgya bzlas nas sdig pa sbyang ba dang/ byang chub sems dpa'i ltung ba bshags pa/ gtsug lag khang bzhengs tshul sogs snang ngo / spyan ras gzigs kyi skor la/
jo bos mdzad pa gong du smos la/ de'i gsal byed kyi sgrub thabs/ rdzogs rim/ las tshogs la rnal 'byor lnga dang/ dug gsum shad kyis sbyong ba'i man ngag/zhi drag gi sbyin
sreg la sogs

nyi shu tsam dang/ sgrol ma'i skor la/ jo bo rgya gar nas bod du 'byon khar/ rdo rje gdan la skor ba mdzad pa'i dus/ sgrol ma nyid kyis gsungs pa'i bstod pa sho lo ka nyer
gcig dang sbyar ba'i sgrub thabs/ las tshogs rnams dang/ sgrol ma dkar mo la jo bo'i gzhung dang rjes su 'brel ba/ ngag dbang grags pa dang/ gser gling pa nas brgyud pa'i
tshe khrid/ las tshoogs mang po dang bcas pa/ mi g.yo ba sngon po la/ jo bo'i gzhung dang/ dpal ldan dgon pa bas bur gyi nya ga mor sgom mdzad kyi bzhugs pa la/ bar chad
kyi mtshan ma byung ba jo bo la zhus pas/ nga la rnal 'byor bsrung ba'i man ngag yod gsung nas/ mi g.yo ba'i dmigs pa skor gsum dang/ sgrub yig che chung/ rgyud man ngag
dang bcas pa rdzogs par gnang/ kha gcig sgrub yig che ba/ bya rgyud kyi nang gi mi g.yo ba'i rgyud la le'u dang las tshogs mang du yod pa 'dii yin zhes zer/ sgrub yig bar
pa sogs/ man ngag rnams dgon pa ba nas sne'u zur pa la brgyud pa dang/ bya yul ba nas brgyud pa gnyis/ dgyer sgom la bzhugs pa sangs rgyas dbon la gnang/ de'i gsung la
rtogs ldan bzang mo bas zin bris su btab pa da lta yod pa 'di'o/ mi g.yo ba bla med kyi rgyud/ phyis shur ke lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing/ dbang rgyud
dang bcas pa byung ngo/ gzhan yang tshogs bdag dkar po la/ gser gling pa/ nA ro pa/ kha che rin chen rdo rje rnams kyi rgya gzhung re jo bos mdzad pa gnyis dang lnga/ tshogs
bdag gi skyes rabs/ gzungs rings/ phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ gsang sgrub kyi skor gser gling pas jo bo la gnang ba dang/ gzhan yang las tshogs le'u bcu bco

lnga pa dang/ le'u sum bcu rtsa gcig pa rnams/ jo bos rnal 'byor pa/ des spyan snga ba/ des bya yul ba la brgyud pa'o/ tshogs bdag dkar po 'di 'jig rten pa'i tshul bstan kyang/
kha gcig spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul par bzhed/ bka' brgyud 'di'i lugs kyi bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sprul par bzhed de mi 'gal lo/ yang dzam bha la dkar po 'brug zhon lha
mo bzhis bskor ba ni/ jo bos ri bo po ta la'i 'gram du byon pa'i dus/ spyan ras gzigs kyis zhal dngos su bstan nas gnang te/ phyi nang gsang gsum gyi las tshogs dang/ chu
sbyin bya thabs sogs dang/ rme brtsegs ljang khu'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa dang/ gtsug tor dri med/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar gyi rjes gnang la sogs pa jo bo nas
brgyud pa da lta ma chad par bzhugs so/ jo bo nas brgyud pa'i dbang brgyud yod pa la/ bde mchog lu yi pa/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma/ gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/ ye shes zhabs lugs/
jo bo nyid kyi gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang phyug/ ma hA ma yA/ mi 'khrugs pa/ yo ga gtsug dgu/ kun rig jo bo lugs/ sgur pa rnams de las brgyud cing phyag len mdzad pas
sgur lugs su grags pa dang/ rdo rje phag mo rin chen rgyan dang/ spyan ras gzigs lha mangs su grags pa/ klu sgrub dang jo bo nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gzhung dang rjes su 'brel
ba'i dbang bka' la sogs pa da lta bzhugs pa mang du snang ngo/ chos skyong skor la/ bka' gdams pa spyi la grags pa/ mgon po gri gug la gtso rkyang/ lha gsum/ lha bzhi/
lha lnga/ lha mangs sogs lugs mang du 'dug pa rnams la/ mgon po'i rgyud 'ga' re dang/ rgya gzhung che chung bcu bco lnga tsam snang ba'i

gtso rkyang la jo bo chen po dang/ a ba dhU ti pa gnyis kyi gzhung re dang/ de la paNDi ta 'jam dpal dbyangs kyi 'grel pa dang/ gtso 'khor gsum du byed pa paNDi ta grags pa
rdo rje'i rgya gzhung dang/ de'i gsal byed/ bya yul bas mdzad pa la brten nas/ byin brlabs kyi brgyud pa yang mnga' bas/ bla ma gong ma rnams 'di mdzad pa mang la/ lha bzhi
byed na/ mgon po'i mdun du gnod sbyin lag na rdo rje/ rdo rje gsor thabs su 'dzin pa/ gnod sbyin grangs med pa'i tshogs kyis bskor ba/ nA ro pa'i gzhung dang bskul nas
'byung ba bzhin bskyed pa dang/ yang lag na rdo rje'i dod du mgon po traka shad yod pa/ bod kyis byas pa'i lha bzhi gcig kyang 'dug go/ lha lngar byed na/ paNDi ta las
kyi rdo rje'i gzhung ltar/ lcam dral gsum gyi mdun du gtum po lce spyang gdong can dang/ rgyab tu srin po legs sred dmar po gnyis bskyed la/ legs sred dmar po 'di lho nub
pa yin par bzhed cing/ mdun du bskyed nas las la bkol ba'i sgrub yig kyang yod do/ yang jo bo'i rgya gzhung du gtso bo la mkha' 'gro ma bzhis bskor ba'i lha lnga cig gsungs
pa dang/ yang gri gug rigs lnga dang/ gtso bo la gshin rje pho brgyad mo brgyad kyis bskor ba/ lha bcu bdun zangs gri can du grags pa gnyis la/ bram ze mchog sred kyi
gzhung che chung/ dbang rgyud dang bcas pa yod pa dang/ yang gtso bo la ye shes zhabs lugs kyi phyogs skyong bcu bco lngas bskor ba dang/ mgon po rta mangs su grags pa/
mgon po'i bskul nas 'byung ba sogs yod pas/ de dag gi mngon rtogs dang rgya gzhung gang nas gang bshad sogs don du gnyer na gzhan du blta'o/ yang

mgon po lho nub pa/ zhal dmar ba/ mi thung gsod byed/ mthar skyes ma zhes mtshan gyi rnam grangs bzhi dang ldan pa 'di la/ jo bo'i rgya gzhung dang/ de'i gsung la bshes gnyen
ston pas bkod pa'i gab pa mngon phyung du grags pa/ phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ gsang sgrub sogs la phyis kyis byas pa'i yig cha mang du 'dug la/ 'di dbang gi gri gug yin
par rin po che chos kyi rdo rje bzhed do/ gri gug gi 'khor du yod pa'i mgon po lce spyang gdong can la/ glang ri thang pa nas rgya lcags ri gong kha pa la brgyud pa'i rjes
gnang dang las tshogs sogs 'dug la mgon po beng la jo bo nas brgyud pa gtso 'khor lnga'i rjes gnang/ dgos sgrub sogs dang/ mgon po traka shad la mi 'dra ba mang yang/ bka'
gdams pa nas brgyud pa rkang thang dang/ seng zhon du nges pas/ 'di la sgrub thabs dang/ zhi drag gi las tshogs mang ngo/ nam mkha'i gos can la bka' gdams glegs bam nas/
mched bcu gnyis su gsungs pa ni/ gser mtsho ma dang/ 'od mtsho ma/ bstan skyong ma dang yid 'dzin ma/ stobs mo che dang drag shul can/ khrag mdog ma dang dud kha ma/
thogs me ma dang stobs mo che/ dbang sdud ma dang las 'joms ma/ bcu gnyis stobs chen bstan bsrung kun/ kho bo'i bstan pa mi skyong na/ ci ste kho bo'i slad bzhin 'brang/
zhes gsungs shing/ lam yig las/ mched bzhir gsungs pa ni/ rdo rje shugs chen ma/ 'od ldan ma/ dung skyong ma nam mkha'i gos can rnams so/ mgon po lho nub pa dang/ nam mkha'ii
gos can ni/ rgya gar nas jo bo'i phyags phyir lugs sku dang/

rgya dpe'i dgos kyi bka' srungs la byon zhes 'byung la/ nam mkha'i gos can zhes pa sku gcer bu'i don yin kyang/ rgyan can sogs ni zhal gzigs yin no/ bya yul gyi lha mo dmar
mo ni/ re ma ti mched bzhi'i dbang gi re ma ti yin te/ 'di la tsaNDi dmar mo zhes pa gtum mo dmar mo zhes pa'o/ gzhan yang sngon gyi skyes chen rnams kyi gsan yig che chung
dang/ bla ma rnams kyi gsung las mang du thos kyang/ 'dir rgyas par ma spros shing/ 'di tsam zhig smos pa yang/ kha gcig la mangs pa dang/ dgos pa chung ba'i blo skye
ba srid pa yin pas/ legs par bshad pa snang yang don du mi gnyer la/ dus kyi dbang gis lugs 'di dag don du gnyer ba dka' bar snang yang/ 'di dag la brten nas kyang rags
pa tsam rtogs shing/ zhib tu 'tshol ba'i sgor 'gyur ba srid dam snyam nas bkod la/ blo gros dang ldan zhing bka' brgyud 'di la dad pa dang ldan pa rnams kyis ji ltar rigs
pa bsnan cing spel bar bya'o/ 'dir smras pa/ de skad mang du thos pa'i smra ba pa/ lha'i dbang po'i mgrin pa'i dkyil 'khor las/ ngo mtshar gtam gyi 'od 'phreng gsar pa 'di/
skal ldan blo gsal mgrin pa'i rgyan du 'bul/ de ltar gangs ri'i khrod 'dir rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'dzin pa'i skyes chen paN grub bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byon pa las/
bstan pa spyi la bka' drin che ba sngon mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho dpon slob nas brgyud pa dang/ phyis dpal ldan a ti sha'i bka' brgyud nyid mchog yin la/ gzhan yang mdo rgyud
tshad ldan gyi tshig don/ shing rta chen po rnams kyis bkral ba'i lam

srol 'dzin cing spel bar mdzad pa'i skyes bu dam pa rang rang gi chos srol gang 'dzin kyang gtsug gi nor bu ltar bsten cing/ yon tan brjod pa'i gnas su gyur pas/ chos dang
gang zag la ris su bcad nas smra ba'i blos ma yin gyi/ bka' gdams kyi bshes gnyen gong ma de rnams yon tan sbed pa la gtso bor mdzad pa ni/ glegs bam las/ jo bo yab sras
kyi skyes rabs rnams chos lugs mi gcig pa'i snod min la gsang bar yang gdams shing/ lam yig las kyang/ bka' gdams pa gong ma rnams kyi bzhed pa skye ba dran pa tsam la yon
tan du mi mdzad/ sbas pa'i gter bsrung sla ba bzhin du/ yon tan thams cad nang du sbed pa yin/ bla ma rje btsun chen po la phyag dar ston pa sogs kyis/ jo bo'i sku tshe
snga phyi dang/ sangs ji ltar rgya ba'i lo brgyus rgyus yi ger bri ba zhus pas/ gtsug tor du bcad do/ phur bus gdab po bya ba de bgegs la nus pa med par byed pa yin/ de
bzhin du bka' dang bla ma'i man ngag la tshig gi phur pa btab pas byin brlabs chung du 'gro ba yin/ des na chos tshong dus kyi 'o ma bzhin du 'gro bas/ tshig zin par bya/
don go bar bya/ rtogs pa rgyud la skyes par bya/ yi ger mi bri bar bya gsung nas/ phyag dar la nan chags su mdzad cing gsungs shes khungs su mdzad nas/ rjes su 'brang ba
rnams kyis kyang rnam thar rgyas pa ma bkod cing/ gdul bya thun mong ba dang bstun pa'i rnam thar mdor bsdus tsam dang/ 'das dus ngos 'dzin gyi yi ge che chung ma gtogs/
rnam thar phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa

ma mthong bas/ than mong ba gang mthong rnams 'dir phyogs gcig tu mdor bsdus te dad pa'i blos bkod pa'o/ brgyud pa gsum ldan dam pa rnams kyi rnam thar dri med yon tan rin
chen du mas gang ba can/ thugs rje'i byin brlabs gting mtha' mi mngon phrin las rnam bzhi'i rba brlabs rgyun chad med par g.yo bas brjid/ rnam dag lta ba'i rin chen mchog
gi cod pan dang ldan snying rje'i glu dbang spyan zur rol pas mdzes/ brgyad khri bzhi stong chos kyi bcud ldan rnam thar mtsho chen 'di ni 'gro ba'i dpal du rgyas gyur cig/
bla ma'i rnam thar dri med bdud rtsi'i chu/ thub bstan padmo'i bzhin ras gsal mdzad pa/ skal bzang mig la ya mtshan dpal ster ba'i/ legs bshad 'di ni sngon med gangga'i
rgyun/ kha cig rgyal dang mkhas rnams gang bzhed pa'i/ lugs chen dor nas rang gi rgan po yi/ rjes su 'brangs nas sangs rgyas bstan pa la/ zhugs kyang de don bsgrub par
mi nus shing/ dus kyi dbang gis rgyal ba'i bstan pa yang/ lkog mar phyin pa'i dbugs ltar gyur pa yi/ lugs bzang 'di yang ches cher nyams gyur pas/ bstan dang 'gro la phan
par dgongs rnams kyis/ rgyal ba'i bka' dang mkhas grub bzhed gzhung la/ legs par sbyangs pa'i bsngags 'os chen po gang/ sngon byung skyes chen dam pa de dag gi/ rnam thar
'di don nyams su blang bar rigs/ zab mo lta bas 'khrul pa'i mtshan ma zhi/ nyams len sgom pas sems nyid rang sar grol/ rgya chen spyod pas phyin drug lam du 'khyer/ brgyud
pa 'di la mi mos

su shig zhig yod/ rtogs brjod rin chen phreng ba'i do shal gyis/ mkhas pa'i yid la dga' ba bskyed pa ltar/ tsan dan ljoon pa gsar pa lho phyogs kyi/ rlung gis bskyod pa'i bsung
gis de lta min/ rmad byung rnam thar dum bur 'thor ba rnams/ kho bo'i lhag bsam pho nyas legs bsdus nas/ gzugs brnyan mdzes pa me long nang du ni/ shar ba 'di la mkhas
rnams dgyes par mdzod/ lhag bsam nyin mor byed pa'i 'od zer gyis/ rnam thar padmo'i tshal rnams kha phye ste/ ngo mtshar sbrang rtsi'i longs spyod 'di sbyar bas/ don gnyer
pung ba'i dga' ston rgyas gyur cig/ bla ma'i rnam thar nyin mor byed pa'i 'od stong zhes pa 'di ni/ rig gnas mtha' dag la mkhyen pa rgyas pa mkhan chen dge g.ye ba tshul
khrims seng ge'i gsung gis/ bka' gdams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen byon tshul rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa zhig gyis shes zhes bskul kyang/ le lo'i dbang gis re zhig
'gyangs pa la/ phyis don du gnyer ba'i bshes gnyen 'ga' zhig gis 'phral 'phral du bskul bas mtshams sbyar te/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs
pa brnyes pa/ byams mgon gnyis pa tshul khrims dar gyi zhabs rdul spyi bos bsten pa/ shAkya'i dge slong bsod nams lha'i dbang pos khro mo zhes pa shing pho 'brug gi lo/
mngon bar byang chub pa'i zla ba yar ngo'i tshes bcu la grub pa'i gnas mchog dpal ldan lo dgon pa'i dben gnas dga' ldan rtser sbyar ba'o/ 'dis kyang rgyal ba'i bstan pa
rin po che phyogs dus gnas skabs thams cad// //
